### [1] [Bash-Commenter: Leveraging Syntax-Aware Preference Optimization to Reinforce Large Language Model for Bash Code Comment Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29709v1)
*Lei Yu,Jingyuan Zhang,Xin Wang,Li Yang,Fengjun Zhang,Peng Wang,Jia Xu,Jiajia Ma*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出基于LLaMA-3.1-8B的Bash-Commenter方法，通过构建数据集、持续预训练和监督微调及语法感知偏好优化，显著提升Bash注释生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bash脚本因语法自由和缺乏注释而难以理解和维护，现有方法数据集不足且LLM对Bash理解不够。

Method: 构建高质量Bash脚本注释数据集，进行持续预训练（CPT）和监督微调（SFT），并引入语法感知偏好优化（SAPO）利用AST构建正确与细微错误脚本的偏好对。

Result: 在单行命令上BLEU-4=33.40%、METEOR=58.26%、ROUGE-L=57.03%，在多行脚本上BLEU-4=22.15%、METEOR=43.89%、ROUGE-L=32.80%，优于基线方法，人工和LLM评估确认注释质量更优。

Conclusion: 所提出的Bash-Commenter方法有效提升了Bash注释生成的正确性、完整性和自然性，解决了现有方法的不足。

中文摘要：由于Bash的语法自由性和复杂的命令结构，Bash脚本理解具有挑战性。尽管在系统管理中扮演关键角色，Bash脚本通常缺乏足够的注释，阻碍了可读性和可维护性。现有的自动注释生成方法面临两个主要挑战：（1）有限的训练数据集不能充分代表真实世界的Bash使用模式；（2）大型语言模型（LLM）对Bash特定概念的理解不足。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了Bash-Commenter，一种基于LLaMA-3.1-8B的高级注释生成方法。首先，我们构建了一个包含复杂多行Bash脚本及高质量注释的综合数据集。其次，我们在大规模Bash数据上进行持续预训练（CPT），然后进行监督微调（SFT），增强模型对Bash语法和语义的基础知识。最后，我们引入了语法感知偏好优化（SAPO），通过对脚本的抽象语法树（AST）应用原子操作来构建偏好对，创建正确和细微错误脚本的最小对，用于细粒度语义学习。我们的方法优于最先进的基线，在1,064个单行命令上实现了33.40%的BLEU-4、58.26%的METEOR和57.03%的ROUGE-L，在1,046个多行脚本上实现了22.15%的BLEU-4、43.89%的METEOR和32.80%的ROUGE-L。人工和LLM评估进一步证实了在正确性、完整性和自然性方面的优越注释质量。

Original abstract: Bash script comprehension is challenging due to Bash's syntactic freedom and complex command structures. Despite its critical role in system administration, Bash scripts often lack adequate comments, hindering readability and maintainability. Existing automated comment generation approaches face two main challenges: (1) limited training datasets that inadequately represent real-world Bash usage patterns; and (2) insufficient understanding of Bash-specific concepts by Large Language Models (LLMs). To address these, we propose Bash-Commenter, an advanced comment generation method based on LLaMA-3.1-8B. First, we construct a comprehensive dataset of complex, multi-line Bash scripts with high-quality comments. Second, we conduct Continual Pre-training (CPT) on large-scale Bash data, followed by Supervised Fine-tuning (SFT), strengthening the model's foundational knowledge of Bash syntax and semantics. Finally, we introduce Syntax-Aware Preference Optimization (SAPO), which constructs preference pairs by applying atomic operations to a script's Abstract Syntax Tree (AST), creating minimal pairs of correct and subtly incorrect scripts for fine-grained semantics learning. Our method outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving 33.40% BLEU-4, 58.26% METEOR, and 57.03% ROUGE-L for 1,064 single-line commands, and 22.15% BLEU-4, 43.89% METEOR, and 32.80% ROUGE-L for 1,046 multi-line scripts. Human and LLM evaluations further confirm superior comment quality in correctness, completeness, and naturalness.

</details>


### [2] [MicroAgent: Context-Augmented Multi-Agent Framework for Automatic Microservice Decomposition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29742v1)
*Zishan Su,Junjie Huang,Shiwen Shan,Xingyan Chen,Hui Zeng,Yuxin Su,Yanlin Wang,Michael R. Lyu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出MicroAgent，一种上下文增强的多智能体框架，通过将微服务分解分为五个子任务并分配专门智能体，结合多粒度上下文和设计原则工具，实现89.2%的分解准确率，超越现有方法24.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微服务分解是迁移遗留系统到微服务架构的关键步骤，但手动方法耗时、现有自动方法缺乏语义且大语言模型忽视上下文和设计原则，导致效果不佳。

Method: MicroAgent：将分解过程分为五个子任务，每个子任务由专门智能体处理；提供定制多粒度上下文以减少信息过载；集成分析工具确保符合设计原则。

Result: 在10个Java Web应用上平均分解准确率89.2%，比最先进方法高24.6%。

Conclusion: MicroAgent通过上下文增强和多智能体协作有效提升了微服务分解的准确性和实用性。

中文摘要：微服务架构（MSA）的采用通过增强可扩展性、敏捷性和可维护性，彻底改变了软件工程，超越了传统的单体应用。随着越来越多的开发者将其遗留系统迁移到基于微服务的架构，有效的微服务分解——将单体应用划分为高内聚的服务——变得至关重要。然而，这一分解任务面临着重大挑战。手动方法耗时且费力。现有的自动化方法通常无法从复杂应用中捕获必要的语义洞察，而大型语言模型的简单应用则容易忽视关键的上下文信息和设计原则，导致结果不理想。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了MicroAgent，一种用于微服务分解的上下文增强多智能体框架。我们的框架将分解过程分为五个不同的子任务，并为每个子任务分配一个专门的智能体。为了增强每个智能体的有效性，我们提供了定制的、多粒度的上下文，使其分析保持专注并减轻信息过载。此外，为了确保分解符合既定的设计原则，我们集成了分析工具来指导智能体的决策。在10个Java Web应用上的实验评估表明，MicroAgent实现了平均89.2%的分解准确率，比最先进的方法高出24.6%。我们还进行了一个案例研究，以突出我们设计的实际好处。

Original abstract: The adoption of Microservice Architecture (MSA) has revolutionized software engineering by enhancing scalability, agility, and maintainability over traditional monolithic applications. As more developers transition their legacy systems to microservice-based architectures, effective microservice decomposition-partitioning monolithic applications into highly cohesive services-becomes vital. However, this decomposition task presents significant challenges. Manual approaches are time-consuming and labor-intensive. Existing automated methods often fail to capture the necessary semantic insights from complex applications, while naive applications of Large Language Models tend to overlook crucial contextual information and design principles, leading to suboptimal results.
  To address these challenges, we propose MicroAgent, a Context-Augmented Multi-Agent Framework for Microservice Decomposition. Our framework divides the decomposition process into five distinct subtasks and assigns each to a specialized agent. To enhance the effectiveness of each agent, we provide tailored, multi-granularity context that keeps its analysis focused and mitigates information overload. Furthermore, to ensure the decomposition adheres to established design principles, we integrate analytical tools that guide the agents' decision-making. Experimental evaluations on 10 Java Web applications demonstrate that MicroAgent achieves an average decomposition accuracy of 89.2%, outperforming the state-of-the-art method by 24.6%. We also conduct a case study to highlight the practical benefits of our design.

</details>


### [3] [Uncovering Similar but Different Packages in PyPI and Potential Security Threats](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29785v1)
*Sunha Park,Soojin Han,Seunghoon Woo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PyPI中存在大量复制包，它们复制流行、有漏洞或恶意包的代码，造成混淆、传播漏洞并成为攻击向量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究PyPI中包复制的规模、特征和潜在威胁，特别是如何导致漏洞传播和恶意软件分发。

Method: 分析PyPI仓库三分之一（20万包）的数据，从流行包、漏洞包和恶意包三个角度识别复制包，并进行特征分析。

Result: 发现1361个流行包复制、256个未知漏洞包复制、186个恶意包复制流行包，并识别出7个新恶意复制包。

Conclusion: 包复制在PyPI中普遍存在且造成严重安全威胁，现有检测工具难以发现，需要更好的防护措施。

中文摘要：在这项研究中，我们对PyPI中的包复制进行了大规模、深入的研究。作为一个重要平台，PyPI为开发者简化了Python包的分发。然而，除了小规模代码克隆之外，我们观察到PyPI上存在许多复制的包，这些包复制了现有包的大部分代码库。这种复制不仅会混淆开发者，还会传播已知漏洞，并使得创建新的恶意包成为可能。为了解决这个问题，我们全面考察了复制包的特征和潜在威胁。利用整个PyPI仓库的三分之一（20万个包），我们从三个角度研究了复制：流行包的复制、有漏洞的包的复制以及恶意包的复制。我们的实验揭示了关于PyPI中包复制的三个关键发现：（1）通过识别前3000个流行项目中的1361个复制包，我们表明复制经常在不同维护者下重新分发现有包的实质性部分；（2）通过发现256个先前未知的复制有漏洞包，我们证明复制造成了当前检测工具很少捕获到的漏洞盲点；（3）通过分析3883个已知恶意包，我们发现186个（4.79%）复制了流行包，这一模式进一步引导我们识别出七个先前未知的复制恶意包，突显了其作为通过微小修改和代码注入进行恶意软件分发的攻击向量的作用。

Original abstract: In this study, we present a large-scale, in-depth study of package replication in PyPI. As a vital platform, PyPI streamlines Python package distribution for developers. However, beyond small-scale code cloning, we observe that many replicated packages exist on PyPI, which duplicate most of the codebase from existing packages. Such replication not only confuses developers but also propagates known vulnerabilities and enables the creation of new malicious packages. To address this issue, we comprehensively examine the characteristics and potential threats of replicated packages. Using one-third of the entire PyPI repository (200K packages), we investigate replication from three perspectives: replication of popular packages, vulnerable packages, and malicious packages. Our experiments reveal three critical findings about package replication in PyPI: (1) by identifying 1,361 replicated packages of the top 3K popular projects, we show that replication frequently redistributes substantial portions of existing packages under different maintainers; (2) by uncovering 256 previously unknown replicated vulnerable packages, we demonstrate that replication creates vulnerability blind spots that current detection tools rarely catch; (3) by analyzing 3,883 known malicious packages, we found that 186 (4.79%) replicated popular ones, and this pattern further led us to identify seven previously unknown replicated malicious packages, highlighting its role as an attack vector for malware distribution through minor modifications and code injection.

</details>


### [4] [Rethinking Build vs. Buy Decisions in Enterprise Software: Navigating Trade-offs through a Structured Decision-Support Approach](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29816v1)
*Janardan Misra,Vikrant Kaulgud,Adam Burden,Sanjay Podder*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于本体和规则推理的结构化决策支持方法，用于增强企业软件开发的构建与购买决策，并通过金融案例验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业软件构建与购买决策复杂，组织常依赖零散知识和非正式推理，缺乏系统性权衡分析，需要结构化的决策支持方法。

Method: 基于决策因素本体、规则推理和参考级别匹配的方法，实现为轻量级咨询工具，支持冷启动场景。

Result: 通过金融领域案例展示方法适用性，表明结构化因素分析能澄清决策原理并突出时变条件。

Conclusion: 使决策标准明确且可比较能提高决策质量、透明度和可审计性。

中文摘要：构建与购买的决策仍然是企业软件开发中持续存在的挑战，受到竞争性战略、技术、成本和风险考虑的影响。第三方解决方案的日益普及，以及通过云原生技术、API和低代码平台进行自定义开发的可行性不断提高，进一步加剧了这些决策的复杂性。在实践中，组织通常依赖零散的专业知识和非正式推理，难以系统分析权衡或随时间推移证明决策的合理性。本文提出了一种结构化的决策支持方法，旨在增强在这种情境下的构建与购买决策。该方法基于一个决策因素本体，涵盖战略考虑、应用特征、成本和预算约束以及风险维度。它将因素模型与基于规则的推理和参考级别匹配相结合，以支持即使在历史数据不可用的冷启动场景中的决策。该方法实现为一个轻量级咨询工具，使用户能够评估相关因素、探索权衡并获取具有透明推理过程的建议。通过金融领域的案例说明了该方法的适用性，展示了结构化因素分析如何阐明决策原理并突出决策可能随时间变化的条件。结果表明，使决策标准明确且可系统比较，可以提高企业环境中构建与购买决策的质量、透明度和可审计性。

Original abstract: Build-versus-buy decisions remain a persistent challenge in enterprise software development, shaped by competing strategic, technical, cost, and risk considerations. The increasing availability of third-party solutions alongside the growing feasibility of custom development through cloud-native technologies, APIs, and low-code platforms has further amplified the complexity of these decisions. In practice, organizations often rely on fragmented expertise and informal reasoning, making it difficult to systematically analyze trade-offs or justify decisions over time. This paper presents a structured decision-support approach designed to augment build-versus-buy decision-making in such contexts. The approach is grounded in an ontology of decision factors spanning strategic considerations, application characteristics, cost and budget constraints, and risk dimensions. It combines this factor model with rule-based reasoning and reference-level matching to support decision-making even in cold-start scenarios where historical data is unavailable. The approach is implemented as a lightweight advisory artifact that enables users to evaluate relevant factors, explore trade-offs, and derive recommendations with transparent reasoning. The applicability of the approach is illustrated through a finance domain case, demonstrating how structured factor analysis can clarify decision rationale and highlight conditions under which decisions may change over time. The results suggest that making decision criteria explicit and systematically comparable can improve the quality, transparency, and auditability of build-versus-buy decisions in enterprise settings.

</details>


### [5] [Evaluating Hardware Abstraction Layer Concepts for Software Defined Vehicles: Insights into Applicability and Effectiveness](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00039v1)
*Akshay Narla,Johannes Stümpfle,Souvik Saha,Nasser Jazdi,Michael Weyrich*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了汽车与非汽车领域的硬件抽象层，提出混合HAL设计以支持软件定义车辆的模块化、安全性和OTA更新需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前车辆系统软硬件紧密耦合，难以满足SDV对模块化、互操作性、实时处理和OTA更新的需求。解耦软硬件是首要步骤，而现有HAL在SDV环境中的适用性未知。

Method: 系统评估当前汽车HAL，并探索智能手机、网络和工业自动化等非汽车领域的HAL机制；建立基于SDV特定需求的评估框架进行对比分析。

Result: 基于中间件的HAL提供可移植性和模块化，基于虚拟机监视器的HAL在安全性、OTA就绪性和硬件效率上更优；两种方法均有局限。

Conclusion: 提出混合HAL设计，结合虚拟机监视器隔离与中间件标准化，为SDV生命周期提供灵活、可扩展的硬件抽象层指导。

中文摘要：软件定义车辆的出现代表了汽车设计的根本性转变，优先考虑以软件为中心的架构而非传统的硬件驱动模型。SDV要求在整个车辆生命周期内具备模块化、互操作性、实时处理和空中更新能力。然而，当前的车辆系统以紧密耦合的软件和硬件为特征，由于其复杂性和异构性，难以满足这些需求。实现SDV的关键第一步是将软件与硬件解耦，这可以通过稳健的硬件抽象层来促进。虽然现有的HAL提供了硬件独立性和标准化接口，但它们在SDV环境中的适用性和有效性仍不确定。本文系统地评估了当前的汽车HAL，并探索了来自非汽车领域（包括智能手机、网络和工业自动化）的HAL机制，以提取与SDV开发相关的跨领域见解。开发了一个基于标准驱动的评估框架，以根据SDV特定需求评估HAL。研究发现，虽然基于中间件的HAL提供了可移植性和模块化，但基于虚拟机监视器的方法在安全性、OTA就绪性和硬件效率方面表现更好。两种方法都存在局限性，促使提出一种混合HAL设计，该设计集成了虚拟机监视器隔离和中间件标准化。本文通过提供关于当前HAL策略的适用性和有效性的见解，为汽车软件架构的持续发展做出了贡献。它为设计灵活、可扩展且面向未来的HAL提供了可操作的指导，以在整个生命周期内支持SDV。

Original abstract: The emergence of Software-Defined Vehicles represents a fundamental shift in automotive design, prioritizing software-centric architectures over traditional hardware-driven models. SDVs require modularity, interoperability, real-time processing, and over-the-air update capabilities throughout the vehicle lifecycle. However, current vehicle systems, characterized by tightly coupled software and hardware, struggle to meet these demands due to their complexity and heterogeneity. A critical first step toward enabling SDVs is the decoupling of software from hardware, which can be facilitated through a robust Hardware Abstraction Layer. While existing HALs offer hardware independence and standardized interfaces, their applicability and effectiveness in SDV contexts remain uncertain. This paper systematically evaluates current automotive HALs and explores HAL mechanisms from non-automotive domains, including smartphones, networking, and industrial automation, to extract cross-domain insights relevant to SDV development. A criteria-driven evaluation framework is developed to assess HALs against SDV-specific needs. Findings reveal that while middleware-based HALs offer portability and modularity, hypervisor-based approaches better support safety, OTA readiness, and hardware efficiency. Limitations in both approaches are identified, prompting recommendations for a hybrid HAL design that integrates hypervisor isolation with middleware standardization. This paper contributes to the ongoing developments in automotive software architecture by offering insights into the applicability and effectiveness of current HAL strategies. It provides actionable guidance for designing flexible, scalable, and future-ready HALs to support SDVs across their lifecycle.

</details>


### [6] [SpreadsheetBench 2: Evaluating Agents on End-to-End Business Spreadsheet Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29955v1)
*Jian Zhu,Yuzheng Zhang,Zeyao Ma,Bohan Zhang,Armin Schoepf,Daniel Woloch,Peter Yiliu Wang,Guangyu Robert Yang,Samuel Jacob,Siddharth Nagisetty,Abhiram Chundru,Jean Lin,Spencer Mateega,Jing Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了一个面向电子表格智能体的工作流级基准SpreadsheetBench 2，评估显示当前系统在真实工作流程中准确率低，主要瓶颈是检查不足和错误选择目标单元格。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有电子表格基准仅评估孤立操作，无法反映真实商业场景中的端到端工作流程，缺乏对多工作表、跨依赖复杂任务的评测。

Method: 构建了包含321个任务、基于真实商业数据（财务报告、公司文件）的基准，涵盖生成、调试和可视化三类任务；在统一多轮智能体框架下评估八种大语言模型及基于LLM的电子表格产品。

Result: 最佳模型整体任务准确率34.89%，调试准确率仅12.00%；轨迹分析和失败分类显示，电子表格检查不足和目标单元格选择错误是主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: SpreadsheetBench 2是一个具有挑战性的测试平台，当前系统在真实工作流程中远不可靠，需改进电子表格检查和目标选择能力。

中文摘要：电子表格广泛应用于商业分析、财务建模、报告和决策制定。然而，大多数现有的电子表格基准评估的是孤立的操作，如单个公式生成或局部单元格编辑，因此无法捕捉真实商业场景中的端到端工作流程。我们提出了SpreadsheetBench 2，一个面向电子表格智能体的工作流级基准，涵盖三大任务类别：生成、调试和可视化。该基准基于真实的商业数据构建，包括财务报告和公司文件，并由领域专家进行标注和验证。该基准包含321个任务；每个实例平均涉及11.8个工作表和593.5次单元格修改，反映了具有跨表依赖关系的大型多工作表工作簿。我们在统一的多轮智能体框架下评估了八种前沿大语言模型，并额外纳入了几个基于LLM的电子表格产品作为补充基线。结果表明，当前系统在实际工作流程中仍远不可靠：最佳模型在整体任务准确率上达到34.89%，而调试准确率低至12.00%。轨迹分析和失败分类进一步表明，电子表格检查不足和目标单元格选择错误是主要的瓶颈。这些发现共同将SpreadsheetBench 2定位为推动可靠电子表格自动化的具有挑战性的测试平台。项目页面：https://spreadsheetbench.github.io/

Original abstract: Spreadsheets are widely used for business analysis, financial modeling, reporting, and decision-making. However, most existing spreadsheet benchmarks evaluate isolated operations such as single-formula generation or local cell edits, and therefore fail to capture end-to-end workflows in realistic business settings. We introduce \textsc{SpreadsheetBench 2}, a workflow-level benchmark for spreadsheet agents that covers three task categories: generation, debugging, and visualization. The benchmark is constructed from authentic business data, including financial reports and corporate filings, and is annotated and validated by domain experts. The benchmark contains 321 tasks; each instance averages 11.8 worksheets and requires 593.5 cell modifications, reflecting large multi-sheet workbooks with cross-sheet dependencies. We evaluate eight frontier large language models under a unified multi-turn agent scaffold, and additionally include several LLM-based spreadsheet products as complementary baselines. Results show that current systems remain far from reliable on real-world workflows: the best model achieves 34.89\% overall task accuracy, and debugging accuracy is as low as 12.00\%. Trajectory analysis and a failure taxonomy further indicate that insufficient spreadsheet inspection and incorrect target-cell selection are the dominant bottlenecks. Together, these findings position \textsc{SpreadsheetBench 2} as a challenging testbed for advancing reliable spreadsheet automation. Project page: https://spreadsheetbench.github.io/

### [7] [SWE-Together: Evaluating Coding Agents in Interactive User Sessions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29957v1)
*Yifan Wu,Zhuokai Zhao,Songlin Li,Ho Hin Lee,Jiacheng Zhu,Shirley Wu,Tianhe Yu,Serena Li,Lizhu Zhang,Xiangjun Fan,Shengzhi Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了SWE-Together多回合编程基准，由真实用户-智能体交互重构，并构建LLM用户模拟器用于评估，发现更强智能体成功率高且干预少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有编程智能体基准是静态的，只评估最终代码，而真实场景中用户通过多轮交互澄清目标、添加约束和纠正错误，因此需要支持多回合交互的基准来反映实际用户体验。

Method: 从11,260个真实用户-智能体编程会话中精选109个存储库级任务，构建SWE-Together基准；开发基于LLM的反应式用户模拟器，保留原始用户意图并在必要时提供反馈；通过最终存储库正确性和纠正反馈回合数评估智能体协作能力。

Result: 对前沿编程智能体的实验表明，更强智能体通常具有更高的最终成功率和更少的纠正反馈回合，表明用户体验改善。

Conclusion: 多回合交互基准能更真实评估编程智能体，且更强的智能体在协作中表现更好，减少用户干预需求。

中文摘要：大多数编程智能体基准是静态的：智能体预先收到完整的任务描述，并且仅根据其最终代码进行评判。然而，真正的编程辅助是交互式的，用户在多个回合中澄清目标、添加约束并纠正错误。我们引入了SWE-Together，这是一个从真实用户-智能体编程会话中重建的多回合基准。为了使真实交互可验证，我们从11,260个录制的会话中精选出109个存储库级任务，选择了具有可恢复存储库状态、清晰用户目标和可观察结果的会话。为了跨智能体重现这些交互，我们构建了一个基于LLM的反应式用户模拟器，该模拟器保留原始用户的意图，并在编程智能体的进展需要时提供反馈。为了评估智能体作为协作者的能力，我们衡量最终存储库的正确性以及交互过程中所需的纠正反馈回合数。对前沿编程智能体的实验表明，更强的智能体通常能够实现更高的最终成功率，同时需要更少的干预，这表明用户体验得到了改善。

Original abstract: Most coding-agent benchmarks are static: an agent receives a complete task description up front and is judged only by its final code. Real coding assistance is interactive, with users clarifying goals, adding constraints, and correcting mistakes over multiple turns. We introduce SWE-Together, a multi-turn benchmark reconstructed from real user-agent coding sessions. To make real interactions verifiable, we curate 109 repository-level tasks from 11,260 recorded sessions, selecting sessions with recoverable repository states, clear user goals, and observable outcomes. To replay these interactions across agents, we build a reactive LLM-based user simulator that preserves the original users' intents and provides feedback when the coding agent's progress requires it. To evaluate agents as collaborators, we measure both final repository correctness and the number of corrective feedback turns required during the interaction. Experiments with frontier coding agents show that stronger agents generally achieve higher final success rates while requiring fewer interventions, suggesting an improved user experience.

### [8] [MCP Server Architecture Patterns for LLM-Integrated Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30317v1)
*Carson Rodrigues,Oysturn Vas*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文基于15个MCP服务器枚举，识别出五种架构模式、四种反模式，并通过定量评估验证了分类可靠性、传输开销和工具选择准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管MCP协议发布后迅速出现大量社区实现，但缺乏对生产环境中MCP服务器生态系统架构模式的系统化描述。

Method: 枚举15个独立开发的MCP服务器（5个生产+10个公共），采用Gamma等人结构化形式描述模式，并通过两个LLM评估者计算Cohen's kappa验证分类信度，同时测量传输开销和工具选择准确率。

Result: 识别出五种模式和四种反模式；Cohen's kappa=0.76，表明分类信度较高；传输开销在环回和跨主机路径下被量化；工具选择准确率在特定工具数量阈值下显著下降。

Conclusion: MCP服务器架构存在可归纳的模式与反模式，分类法具有良好可靠性，且工具数量对LLM工具选择性能有显著影响。

中文摘要：模型上下文协议（MCP）由Anthropic于2024年11月提出，定义了将大型语言模型（LLM）连接到外部工具、数据源和服务的标准化接口。发布后数月内，GitHub上出现了数百个社区构建的MCP服务器，但尚无软件维护文献描述该生态系统在生产中的结构化方式。本行业经验论文基于对15个独立开发服务器（5个来自ANSYR语音AI平台的生产服务器和10个来自官方MCP注册中心的公共服务器）的枚举语料库，归纳了五种重复出现的MCP服务器架构模式：资源网关、工具编排器、有状态会话服务器、代理聚合器和领域特定适配器。每种模式均按照Gamma等人的结构化形式（上下文、问题、解决方案和结果）进行描述。我们还记录了四种反模式以及围绕认证、版本控制和可观测性的一组横切关注点。定量评估贡献了三项测量结果：两个独立LLM评估者在54个保留服务器上对分类法的评分者间信度（Cohen's kappa = 0.76），该过程还定位了三个模式边界模糊点；在环回和跨主机路径模型上端到端测量的传输开销；以及一项工具计数研究，显示Claude Haiku 4.5在每上下文10至15个工具时工具选择准确率降至90%以下，Sonnet 4则在20至30个工具之间。代码、语料库和提示已作为复现包发布。

Original abstract: The Model Context Protocol (MCP), introduced by Anthropic in November 2024, defines a standardized interface for connecting large language models (LLMs) to external tools, data sources, and services. Within months of release, hundreds of community-built MCP servers appeared on GitHub, but no software-maintenance literature has yet described how the ecosystem is being structured in production. This industry experience paper catalogues five recurring MCP server architectural patterns observed across an enumerated corpus of fifteen independently developed servers (five production servers from the ANSYR voice AI platform plus ten public servers from the official MCP registry): Resource Gateway, Tool Orchestrator, Stateful Session Server, Proxy Aggregator, and Domain-Specific Adapter. Each pattern is described in the structured form of Gamma et al.: context, problem, solution, and consequences. We also document four anti-patterns and a set of cross-cutting concerns around authentication, versioning, and observability. The quantitative evaluation contributes three measurements: inter-rater reliability of the taxonomy across two independent LLM raters on 54 held-out servers (Cohen's kappa = 0.76), which also localizes three pattern-boundary ambiguities; transport overhead measured end-to-end on loopback and modeled for cross-host paths; and a tool-count study showing tool-selection accuracy drops below 90% between 10 and 15 tools per context for Claude Haiku 4.5 and between 20 and 30 tools for Sonnet 4. Code, corpus, and prompts are released as a replication package.

### [9] [How do Execution Features Improve Statistical Fault Localization? An Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30324v1)
*Marius Smytzek,Andreas Zeller*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究评估了通过执行特征增强统计故障定位（SFL）对定位准确性和检查工作量的影响，使用了EFDD、随机森林和混合效应模型等方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SFL仅使用执行行信息，忽略了数据流、值和分支条件等可能解释故障的更丰富信息，因此需要探索通过执行特征增强SFL是否能提升定位效果。

Method: 使用EFDD提取Tests4Py主题的执行特征，为每个主题训练随机森林，将特征重要性映射到源代码行，并与SFL公式结合；采用混淆调整混合效应模型评估参考补丁准确性、行级和函数级工作量、鲁棒性和可行性，辅以配对统计检验和质量检查。

Result: 评估了参考补丁准确性、行级和函数级工作量、鲁棒性和可行性等指标，但摘要未给出具体数值或结论性结果。

Conclusion: 研究提出并评估了一种通过执行特征增强SFL的方法，但尚未给出最终结论，而是详细描述了评估框架。

中文摘要：自动故障定位帮助开发人员在大代码库中查找故障。统计故障定位（SFL）根据通过/失败谱对可疑行进行排序，但仅靠执行行会遗漏诸如数据流、值或分支条件等信息，这些信息可以解释故障发生的原因。本研究评估了通过执行特征增强SFL是否能提高定位准确性和面向开发人员的检查工作量。我们使用EFDD为所有Tests4Py主题提取执行特征，针对每个主题训练随机森林，将重要性映射到源代码行，并将得到的权重与已建立的SFL公式结合。评估使用混淆调整混合效应模型测量参考补丁准确性、行级和函数级工作量、鲁棒性和可行性，并通过配对统计检验和结果中立的质量检查进行验证。

Original abstract: Automated fault localization helps developers find faults in large code bases. Statistical fault localization (SFL) ranks suspicious lines from pass/fail spectra, but line execution alone misses information like data-flow, values, or branch conditions that explain why a failure occurs.
  This study evaluates whether augmenting SFL with execution features improves localization accuracy and developer-oriented inspection effort. We extract execution features with EFDD for all Tests4Py subjects, train per-subject random forests, map importances to source lines, and combine the resulting weights with established SFL formulas. The evaluation measures reference-patch accuracy, line- and function-level effort, robustness, and feasibility using a confounder-adjusted mixed-effects model, corroborated by paired statistical tests and outcome-neutral quality checks.

### [10] [ATM: CID-Brokered Pre-Write Admission for Multi-Agent Code Co-Synthesis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00041v1)
*Eagl Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出AI-Atomic-Framework (ATM) 来解决多智能体LLM系统中并发写入意图的治理问题，通过规范驱动的治理链和内容标识符代理实现安全有序的共享变更。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM系统在分解软件工程任务时，需要决定并发写入意图的并行、组合或失败路径，缺乏一个规范化的治理机制。

Method: 提出ATM框架，包括将任务意图、仓库范围、写入准入等绑定成治理链，使用CID代理进行共享变更准入，适配器引导原子化映射，以及虚拟原子处理不完整覆盖，最终由中立管理员应用写入。

Result: 在12场景矩阵、归档案例、外部研究等评估中，证明了可行性、可审计性和有界可恢复性，但未声称广泛优势。

Conclusion: ATM框架有效解决了单域内多智能体系统共享写入的治理问题，支持审计和恢复，但需要进一步扩展到跨域治理。

中文摘要：多智能体大语言模型系统可以将软件工程工作分解为规划、生成、验证和修复，但一个更狭窄的系统问题仍然存在：在应用任何受治理的共享变更之前，系统必须决定哪些并发形成的写入意图可以并行进行，哪些需要确定性组合或序列化，以及哪些必须走故障关闭路径。我们通过AI-原子-框架（ATM）来解决这个问题，这是一个基于规范的管理基础，适用于在单一管理域内运行的软件代理。ATM将任务意图、仓库范围、写入准入、验证和证据义务绑定到一个治理链中。内容标识符（CID）代理作为共享变更准入子系统。适配器引导的原子化将写入意图映射到语义原子和有界区域；当持久原子映射覆盖不完整时，虚拟原子提供临时的可审计治理单元，用于保守比较和路由。受治理的共享写入最终由中立的管理员应用，而不是由提议代理直接应用。评估结合了受控、现场、采用和扩展证据，包括12场景确定性设计矩阵、三个归档运行案例、ATM-AdmissionBench、三个归档的同文件边界案例、为期三周的外部采用者研究以及一个操作恢复路由基准。结果支持在观察到的单域设置中的可行性、可审计性和有界可恢复性，但未声称广泛的比较优越性或跨克隆治理。

Original abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems can decompose software-engineering work into planning, generation, validation, and repair, but a narrower systems problem remains: before any governed shared mutation is applied, a system must decide which concurrently formed write intents may proceed in parallel, which require deterministic composition or serialization, and which must take a fail-closed path. We address this problem with the AI-Atomic-Framework (ATM), a specification-grounded governance substrate for software agents operating within a single governance domain.
  ATM binds task intent, repository scope, write admission, validation, and evidence obligations into one governance chain. A Content Identifier (CID) broker serves as the shared-mutation admission subsystem. Adapter-guided atomization maps write intents to semantic atoms and bounded regions; when persistent atom-map coverage is incomplete, virtual atoms provide temporary auditable governance units for conservative comparison and routing. Governed shared writes are ultimately applied by a neutral steward rather than directly by proposing agents.
  Evaluation combines controlled, field, adoption, and extension evidence, including a 12-scenario deterministic design matrix, three archived runner cases, ATM-AdmissionBench, three archived same-file boundary cases, a three-week external-adopter study, and an operational recovery-routing benchmark. The results support feasibility, auditability, and bounded recoverability within the observed single-domain settings, but do not claim broad comparative superiority or cross-clone governance.

</details>


### [11] [The Illusion of Agentic Complexity in README.md Generation: Evaluating Single-Agent vs. Multi-Agent RAG Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30524v2)
*Abu Saleh,Tesfay Welegebreal Tesfay,Phuong T. Nguyen,Juri Di Rocco,Muhammad Umar Zeshan,Davide Di Ruscio*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 单智能体管道在令牌消耗和速度上优于MAS，但MAS结构一致性更高；自主规划是瓶颈，开发者指导计划质量最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统架构复杂性对实际效率的影响尚未被充分研究。

Method: 系统比较单智能体管道、专门的多智能体系统（MAS）和开发者指导规划（DevPlan）变体，以LARCH为基线，评估README生成质量。

Result: 单智能体管道词汇质量与MAS相当，令牌消耗降低86%，速度快一倍；MAS结构一致性98%；自主规划是瓶颈；DevPlan质量最高。

Conclusion: 轻量级开发者指导规划在文档质量上超越所有配置，自主规划是主要效率瓶颈。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于自动化多个软件工程任务，包括代码补全、代码摘要、测试以及仓库级文档的生成。虽然多智能体系统（MAS）经常被采用以支持此类任务，其前提是任务分解能提升性能，但架构复杂性对实际效率的影响仍未得到充分研究。本研究实证评估了依赖于检索增强生成（RAG）的架构，用于生成GitHub仓库的README文件。在这项工作中，我们对单智能体管道、专门的MAS以及开发者指导规划（DevPlan）变体进行了系统比较，并以LARCH（一种最先进的基线）和原始真实值作为基准。结果表明存在一个关键的架构权衡：单智能体管道在词汇质量上与MAS相当，同时将令牌消耗降低了86%，运行速度是单智能体管道的两倍。相比之下，手工分类分析表明MAS实现了高结构一致性（98%），解决了单智能体方法中观察到的格式化问题。自主规划被确定为主要管道瓶颈；结合轻量级开发者指导计划产生了最高的整体文档质量，超过了所有分析的配置。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly utilized to automate several software engineering tasks, including code completion, code summarization, testing, and the generation of repository-level documentation. While Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) are often adopted to support such tasks under the premise that task decomposition improves performance, the impact of architectural complexity on practical efficiency remains under-examined. This study empirically evaluates Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) dependent architectures for the generation of README files for GitHub repositories. In this work, we conducted a systematic comparison between a Single-Agent pipeline, a specialized MAS, and a developer-guided planning (DevPlan) variant, benchmarked against LARCH -- a state-of-the-art baseline -- and the original ground truth. Results indicate a critical architectural trade-off: the Single-Agent pipeline achieves lexical quality comparable to MAS while reducing token consumption by 86% and operating at twice the speed. In contrast, manual taxonomy analysis demonstrates that MAS achieves high structural consistency (98%), resolving formatting issues observed in single-agent approaches. Autonomous planning is identified as the primary pipeline bottleneck; incorporating lightweight developer-guided plans produces the highest overall documentation quality, surpassing all the analyzed configurations.

### [12] [PyMETA: A Benchmark Dataset for Hierarchical Student Code Error Classification with Python-Interpreter-Based Labels](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30610v1)
*Chuyue Li,Ziqi Tang,Jingyi Wang,Yu Wu,Kazuma Hashimoto,Lingyu Gao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了PyMETA数据集，包含48,646份学生Python代码错误标注，并评估了多种模型，发现提示式LLM在错误分类上仍不及微调小模型，且存在过度预测逻辑错误的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码错误检测方法缺乏大规模数据集、多错误分析能力和统一的错误分类体系，难以满足教育场景中上下文敏感的调试需求。

Method: 构建了PyMETA数据集，包含单错误标签和专家标注的多错误子集，采用三级层次错误分类体系；评估了两个微调模型和四个LLM（通过提示）在多级分类任务上的性能。

Result: 最佳模型Gemini 2.5 Pro在多错误提示下达到81.8%宏F1；提示式LLM整体不如微调小模型；多数LLM过度预测逻辑错误，GPT-3.5过度预测率最高，Gemini 2.5 Pro最低。

Conclusion: PyMETA为代码错误分类研究提供了数据基础，揭示了当前LLM在错误检测中的局限性，为未来研究指明了方向。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLM）的进步，代码错误检测已扩展到教育场景中上下文敏感的调试，超越了传统的IDE诊断。然而，现有方法缺乏大规模数据集、多错误分析和统一的错误分类体系。为解决此问题，我们提出了PyMETA，一个大规模Python代码错误分类数据集，包含48,646份学生提交的代码，所有样本均带有单错误标签，以及一个由97个专家标注的多错误样本组成的诊断子集。该数据集采用三级层次分类体系，从二值错误/无错误划分到14种细粒度错误类型，这些类型基于Python官方异常层次结构。我们在两个微调模型和四个大语言模型（通过提示）上评估了多级分类任务，比较了它们的分类性能和运行时成本。对于多错误提示，最佳模型Gemini 2.5 Pro在“包含”标准下达到了81.8%的宏F1。我们观察到：1）提示式LLM仍不及微调的小模型；2）模型在不同错误类型间表现存在显著差异；3）大多数LLM过度将代码分类为逻辑错误，其中GPT-3.5的逻辑错误过度预测率最高，而Gemini 2.5 Pro最低。我们的工作为基于LLM的代码错误研究建立了数据基础并提供了见解。

Original abstract: With the advancement of Large Language Models (LLMs), code error detection has extended beyond traditional IDE diagnostics to context-sensitive debugging in educational scenarios. However, existing approaches lack large-scale datasets, multi-error analysis, and unified error taxonomies. To address this, we introduce PyMETA, a large-scale Python code error classification dataset of 48,646 student submissions, with single-error labels for all samples and a diagnostic subset of 97 expert-annotated multi-error samples. The dataset uses a three-level hierarchical taxonomy, from a binary error/no-error split down to 14 fine-grained error types grounded in Python's official exception hierarchy. We evaluate multi-level classification tasks on two finetuned models and four LLMs with prompting, comparing their classification performance and runtime cost. For multi-error prompting, the best model, Gemini 2.5 Pro, achieves 81.8% macro F1 under the "contains" criterion. We observe that: 1) prompted LLMs still underperform finetuned smaller models; 2) models exhibit significant disparities across error types; 3) most LLMs over-classify code as Logic Error, with GPT-3.5 showing the highest Logic Error Overprediction Rate and Gemini 2.5 Pro the lowest. Our work establishes a data foundation and provides insights for LLM-based code error research.

</details>


### [13] [Towards Knowledge Alignment in Code LLMs: Contrastive Unlearning for Evolving APIs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30810v1)
*Huy Q. Tran,Dang H. Vu,Tuyen N. Dinh,Anh H. D. Nguyen,Anh N. H. Vu,Anh M. T. Bui,Phuong T. Nguyen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: CURE是一种对比遗忘方法，通过同时抑制已弃用API并鼓励正确替代，有效更新LLM的知识以适应软件库演变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要抑制已弃用API但未引导正确替代，导致生成不匹配或不完整的代码。

Method: CURE采用对比遗忘，联合优化：抑制已弃用API的同时促进正确替代品，从而更可靠地更新模型知识。

Result: 在已弃用API基准数据集上，CURE不仅减少已弃用API使用，还提高正确替代，且优于两个最先进基线。

Conclusion: 结合抑制与替代对于LLM适应软件生态系统的演变至关重要。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）近期在代码生成方面取得了强劲的表现。然而，由于知识截止日期和软件库的快速演变，它们经常生成已弃用的API用法，导致代码不可靠且不兼容。现有的微调方法在仅需修改模型知识的一小部分时缺乏选择性。最近的模型级方法，如机器遗忘和模型编辑，为修改参数化知识提供了有希望的方向。然而，它们在缓解已弃用API方面的应用仍然未被充分探索。此外，现有方法主要抑制过时的API，但并未明确引导模型走向正确的替代品，常常导致不匹配或不完整的生成。为了解决这一局限性，我们开发了CURE，一种对比遗忘方法，将遗忘从纯粹抑制过时知识转变为明确促进正确的API替代。具体来说，CURE同时阻止已弃用的API并鼓励其有效替代品，从而更可靠地适应不断发展的软件库。在最近的已弃用API基准数据集上的实验表明，CURE不仅减少了已弃用API的使用，还提高了正确的API替代，同时保持了通用的代码生成性能。CURE在各种质量指标上显著优于两个最先进的基线。这些发现强调了在使LLMs适应不断发展的软件生态系统时，将抑制与替代相结合的重要性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have recently achieved strong performance in code generation. However, due to knowledge cut-off and the rapid evolution of software libraries, they often generate deprecated API usages that lead to unreliable and incompatible code. Existing fine-tuning methods lack selectivity when only a small portion of model knowledge requires modification. Recent model-level approaches, such as machine unlearning and model editing, offer a promising direction for modifying parametric knowledge. However, their use for deprecated API mitigation remains largely unexplored. Moreover, existing methods primarily suppress outdated APIs, but do not explicitly steer models toward correct replacements, often leading to mismatched or incomplete generations. To address this limitation, we developed CURE, a contrastive unlearning approach that shifts unlearning from purely suppressing outdated knowledge to explicitly promoting correct API replacements. Concretely, CURE jointly discourages deprecated APIs while encouraging their valid alternatives, enabling more reliable adaptation to evolving software libraries. The experiments on recent deprecated API benchmark dataset show that CURE not only reduces deprecated API usage but also improves correct API replacement, while preserving general code generation performance. CURE substantially outperforms two SOTA baselines with respect to different quality metrics. These findings highlight the importance of combining suppression with replacement when adapting LLMs to evolving software ecosystems.

</details>

Result: 识别出30种独特且规范的提示模式，并构建了分类法。

Conclusion: 提出的分类法为提示工程提供了统一框架，有助于系统理解和应用提示模式。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）现已广泛应用于软件开发和日常使用。与LLM交互需要编写提示，这些提示范围从简单的临时句子到广泛、详细且结构化的指令。关于提示工程的知识已在文献中的若干综述和目录中进行了记录。然而，术语“提示模式”在不同来源中定义不同，现有工作也以不同方式对提示模式进行了分类。在本报告中，我们针对单轮、基于文本的交互提出了一种提示模式分类法。通过遵循可重复的方法，我们识别出30种独特且规范的提示模式，并沿两个维度进行了组织。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are now widely employed in software development and everyday use. Interacting with LLMs requires crafting prompts, which range from simple ad hoc sentences to extensive, detailed, and structured instructions. Knowledge about prompt engineering has been documented in several surveys and catalogs in the literature. However, the term ``prompt pattern'' is defined differently across sources, and existing works have classified prompt patterns in different ways. In this report, we present a taxonomy of prompt patterns for single-turn, text-based interactions. Following a reproducible method, we identified 30 unique and canonical prompt patterns, organized along two dimensions.

### [15] [Loc2Repair: A Framework for Evaluating the Impact of File-Level Issue Localization in Repo-Level LLM Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30963v1)
*Mohammad Nour Al Awad,Sergey Ivanov*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Loc2Repair是一个模块化评估框架，用于隔离文件级定位对基于仓库的自动修复的影响，实验表明显式定位一致提升修复率和降低平均耗时。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于仓库的自动修复常被视为端到端能力，隐藏了不同失败模式（如文件定位差、补丁合成错误和迭代调试失败），因此需要一个模块化框架来单独分析文件定位的影响。

Method: 提出Loc2Repair框架，将定位与修复解耦，共享运行时、工件模式和评估框架，允许组合不同定位模型和修复骨干；在SWE-bench Verified上使用三个修复骨干，比较无定位基线、两种预测定位和金标准定位下的修复效果。

Result: 显式定位一致提升所有骨干的解决率：池化解决率从44.7%升至48.9%、49.1%（预测定位）和52.4%（金标准）；平均耗时分别减少100.94秒、52.25秒和154.45秒，但模型间存在异质性。

Conclusion: 文件级定位是提升自动修复有效性和平均延迟的一致杠杆，但金标准指导下的失败显示定位之外仍有改进空间。

中文摘要：基于仓库的自动修复通常被报告为一种端到端的能力，这隐藏了不同的失败模式，如文件定位不佳、补丁合成不正确以及迭代调试失败。我们提出了Loc2Repair，一个用于对基于仓库的修复流水线进行受控分析的模块化评估框架，并使用它来隔离文件级问题定位作为上游变量。Loc2Repair在共享运行时、工件模式和评估框架下解耦定位和修复，允许研究人员在匹配条件下组合不同的定位模型和修复骨干。使用SWE-bench Verified上的三个修复骨干，我们比较了没有显式定位的基线修复、由两个定位器预测定位指导的修复以及由金标准修改文件集指导的修复。显式定位一致地提高了所有骨干的解决率：池化性能从基线修复的44.7%提高到预测定位的48.9%和49.1%，以及金标准定位的52.4%。定位还总体上减少了平均耗时：在池化配对分析中，两个预测定位设置的平均耗时分别减少了100.94秒和52.25秒，金标准指导减少了154.45秒，尽管不同模型的token效应仍存在异质性。总体而言，Loc2Repair表明文件级定位是一个一致的修复杠杆，在池化分析中提高了有效性和平均延迟，同时金标准指导下的失败暴露了定位之外的改进空间。

Original abstract: Repository-grounded automated repair is often reported as a single end-to-end capability, which hides distinct failure modes such as poor file targeting, incorrect patch synthesis, and failed iterative debugging. We present Loc2Repair, a modular evaluation framework for controlled analysis of repository-grounded repair pipelines, and use it to isolate file-level issue localization as an upstream variable. Loc2Repair decouples localization and repair under a shared runtime, artifact schema, and evaluation harness, allowing researchers to combine different localization models and repair backbones under matched conditions. Using three repair backbones on SWE-bench Verified, we compare baseline repair without explicit localization, repair guided by predicted localization from two localizers, and repair guided by gold modified-file sets. Explicit localization consistently improves resolved rate across all backbones: pooled performance increases from 44.7% for baseline repair to 48.9% and 49.1% with predicted localization, and to 52.4% with gold localization. Localization also reduces mean elapsed time overall: in pooled paired analysis, mean elapsed time decreases by 100.94 s and 52.25 s for the two predicted-localization settings, and by 154.45 s with gold guidance, although token effects remain heterogeneous across models. Overall, Loc2Repair shows file-level localization is a consistent repair lever, improving effectiveness and mean latency in pooled analysis, while gold-guided failures expose headroom beyond localization.

</details>


### [16] [Comparing Large Language Models on Scrum Certification-Style Questions: Accuracy, Stability, and Error Patterns](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00048v1)
*Robson Alves Vilar,Emanuel Dantas Filho,Ademar França de Sousa Neto,Mirko Perkusich,Danyllo Wagner Albuquerque,João Paiva,Kyller Gorgônio,Angelo Perkusich*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了三种LLM在Scrum认证问题上的表现，发现Gemini 3 Flash准确率最高，错误模式系统化，且模型在规范性明确主题上表现更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估LLMs在需要严格遵循规范知识的认证测试中的能力，特别是Scrum领域，以了解其可靠性和局限。

Method: 使用993道PSM I格式问题，通过零样本、思维链、基于来源三种提示策略测试GPT-5 mini、Gemini 3 Flash和DeepSeek Chat 3.2，重复执行评估稳定性，并结合定量与定性分析。

Result: Gemini 3 Flash准确率最高，GPT-5 mini次之，DeepSeek Chat 3.2最低；模型内变异低；单选题表现最佳，多选题和判断题易错；艺术、经验主义等主题表现稳定，价值观、自管理团队等主题脆弱；错误系统化，涉及过度泛化、限制性措辞等。

Conclusion: LLMs在认证问答中表现出差异且系统化错误，提示需谨慎使用，尤其在规范严格领域；未明确提及但隐含需改进模型或提示策略。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被用于考试和认证式问答任务中，在这些任务中，可以系统地评估它们检索、解释和应用领域特定知识的能力。在软件工程中，当问题严格依赖于规范性定义、角色、工件和规则时，此类设置尤为相关。本文评估了三个当代LLMs——《GPT-5 mini》、《Gemini 3 Flash》和《DeepSeek Chat 3.2》——在回答993道符合专业Scrum Master I（PSM I）评估格式的Scrum认证样式问题时的表现。我们在三种提示策略（零样本、思维链和基于来源的）下评估了模型，并进行了重复执行以评估模型内的稳定性。我们还分析了模型在不同Scrum主题和问题格式上的表现，并辅以对错误答案中反复出现的错误模式的定性分析。结果显示了模型之间的明显差异，其中Gemini 3 Flash达到了最高准确率，其次是GPT-5 mini和DeepSeek Chat 3.2，而模型内变异在所有条件下都很低。按问题格式，模型在单选题上达到了最高准确率，而多选题和判断题更容易出错。按主题，在规范性明确的领域（如工件、经验主义和产品价值）表现更为一致，但在Scrum价值观、自管理团队以及利益相关者和客户方面更为脆弱。定性分析表明，错误是系统性的而非随机性的，涉及过度泛化、限制性措辞、复合干扰项以及常见市场解释与严格Scrum定义之间的冲突。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in exam- and certification-style question answering tasks, where their ability to retrieve, interpret, and apply domain-specific knowledge can be systematically assessed. In Software Engineering, such settings are particularly relevant when questions depend on strict adherence to normative definitions, roles, artifacts, and rules. This paper evaluates the performance of three contemporary LLMs, \textit{GPT-5 mini}, \textit{Gemini 3 Flash}, and \textit{DeepSeek Chat 3.2}, in answering 993 Scrum certification-style questions aligned with the Professional Scrum Master I (PSM I) assessment format. We evaluated the models under three prompting strategies (\textit{zero-shot}, \textit{chain-of-thought}, and \textit{source-grounded}), with repeated executions to assess intra-model stability. We also analyzed performance across Scrum topics and question formats, complemented by a qualitative analysis of recurring error patterns in incorrect answers. Results revealed clear differences among models, with Gemini 3 Flash achieving the highest accuracy, followed by GPT-5 mini and DeepSeek Chat 3.2, while intra-model variability remained low across all conditions. By question format, the models achieved the highest accuracy on single-answer multiple-choice items, whereas multi-select and True/False questions were more error-prone. By topic, performance was more consistent in normatively explicit areas such as Artifacts, Empiricism, and Product Value, but more fragile in Scrum Values, Self-Managing Teams, and Stakeholders \& Customers. The qualitative analysis showed that errors were systematic rather than random, involving overgeneralization, restrictive wording, compound distractors, and conflicts between common market interpretations and strict Scrum definitions.

</details>


### [17] [Prompting GPT-5 on Scrum Certification Questions: An Empirical Accuracy Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00049v1)
*Mirko Perkusich,Danyllo Albuquerque,João Paiva,Robson Vilar,Emanuel Dantas,Ademar França de Sousa Neto,Rohit Gheyi,Kyller Gorgônio,Angelo Perkusich*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文测试了不同提示技术对GPT-5回答Scrum认证问题的准确性影响，发现所有技术均达到85%以上准确率，其中基于引用的提示最佳（89.1%），错误主要集中在范围外内容、过时解释和与指南不一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证LLM在规范性框架（如Scrum）推理中的可靠性，特别是在认证准备场景下，因为LLM的普及与Scrum规则明确性之间需要实证评估。

Method: 使用993个PSM认证风格问题，通过GPT-5零样本、思维链和带源引用三种提示技术回答，并分析准确率与错误类型。

Result: 所有提示准确率>85%，引用提示最佳（89.1%）；16.2%的问题至少一个提示失败，错误分为与指南不一致（28%）、超出范围（34%）、过时/偏见（38%）；正确集中在定义明确主题和单选题。

Conclusion: 提示技术可适度提升LLM的可靠性，减少误解和版本漂移，支持其在敏捷学习和认证中的使用，但多选和解释性领域仍需谨慎。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在敏捷软件开发中越来越多地被用于文档、辅导和培训。随着从业者采用这些工具来准备专业Scrum大师（PSM）等认证，一个关键问题是LLM能否可靠地推理Scrum——一个在《Scrum指南（2020）》中描述的有规范性、明确规则的框架。本文研究了不同提示技术如何影响LLM对Scrum认证风格问题的事实准确性。一个包含993个经过验证的PSM对齐问题的数据集由GPT-5使用三种技术回答：零样本、思维链和带源引用。所有提示均达到超过85%的认证级准确率，其中基于引用的变体表现最佳（89.1%），并产生最低错误率。正确答案集中在定义明确的主题，如“完成定义”、事件和产品待办列表管理，以及单答案选择题上，而多选问题和更具解释性的领域（如Scrum团队和产品价值）则不太稳定。在至少一个提示失败的问题中（16.2%），错误分为与Scrum指南不一致（28%）、超出其范围的内容（34%）以及过时或有偏见的解释（38%）。总体而言，提示技术产生了适度但一致的改进，特别是在减少误解和版本漂移方面，支持LLM在敏捷学习和认证准备中更可靠的使用。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in Agile Software Development for documentation, coaching, and training. As practitioners adopt these tools to prepare for certifications such as Professional Scrum Master (PSM), a key question is whether LLMs can reliably reason about Scrum, a framework with normative, well-defined rules described in the Scrum Guide (2020). This paper examines how different prompt techniques affect the factual accuracy of LLM responses to Scrum certification-style questions. A dataset of 993 validated PSM-aligned questions was answered by GPT-5 using three techniques: zero-shot, chain-of-thought, and with-source citation. All prompts achieved certification-level accuracy above 85\%, with the citation-based variant performing best (89.1\%) and yielding the lowest error rate. Correct answers concentrated in well-defined topics, such as \emph{Definition of Done}, Events, and Product Backlog Management, and in single-answer multiple-choice items, while multi-select questions and more interpretive areas, such as Scrum Team and Product Value, were less stable. Among questions where at least one prompt failed (16.2\%), errors clustered into misalignment with the Scrum Guide (28\%), content outside its scope (34\%), and outdated or biased interpretations (38\%). Overall, prompt techniques produced modest but consistent improvements, particularly in reducing misinterpretation and version drift, supporting more reliable use of LLMs in Agile learning and certification preparation.

</details>

### [18] [Diversity is the Strength of the AI Crowd](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29661v1)
*Matthew Aitchison,Scott Jeen,Toby Shevlane,Ben Day*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究LLM预测系统集成多样性，对多agent集成有启发。

TL;DR: 通过组合准确但多样化的模型预测（如Grok 4）可以提升AI预测系统的集成准确度，而非单纯增加样本数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI预测系统依赖现成LLM，但个体准确度不足以提升集成效果，需要研究如何组合模型以最大化准确度。

Method: 在Metaculus AI基准测试的二分类问题上，分析不同LLM的预测相关性，并评估组合准确且多样化的预测者的集成效果。

Result: 发现前沿LLM预测高度相关，而像Grok 4这样相关性较低的模型在集成中贡献更大，最强的集成是准确且多样化的组合。

Conclusion: AI预测系统的提升应优化模型质量和多样性，而非单纯增加预测样本数。

中文摘要：顶尖的AI预测系统在预测未来世界事件方面正接近超级预测者的准确度，但仍然主要依赖现成的LLM结合针对预测的上下文收集和框架。我们研究如何通过集成来改进这一方法：在给定固定样本数的情况下，应组合哪些现成模型预测以最大化准确度？在Metaculus AI基准测试的二分类问题上，我们发现个体准确度并不足够：许多前沿LLM产生高度相关的预测，限制了来自相同或类似模型的额外预测的价值。相反，最强的集成组合了准确但多样化的预测者，其中Grok 4等模型因其预测与其他前沿LLM的相关性较低而贡献不成比例。这些结果表明，AI群体的力量不在于不加区分地采样更多预测，而在于组合具有互补错误的模型预测，从而激励预测系统明确优化模型质量和多样性。

Original abstract: Top AI forecasting systems are approaching superforecaster-level accuracy on future world events, but still rely primarily on off-the-shelf LLMs combined with forecasting-specific context gathering and scaffolding. We study how to improve this recipe through ensembling: given a fixed number of samples, which off-the-shelf model forecasts should be combined to maximize accuracy? On binary questions from the Metaculus AI Benchmark, we find that individual accuracy is not enough: many frontier LLMs make highly correlated predictions, limiting the value of additional forecasts from the same or similar models. Instead, the strongest ensembles combine accurate but diverse forecasters, with models such as \model{Grok 4} contributing disproportionately because their predictions are less correlated with other frontier LLMs. These results suggest that the strength of the AI crowd comes not from sampling more forecasts indiscriminately, but from combining forecasts across models with complementary errors, motivating forecasting systems that explicitly optimize for both model quality and diversity.

</details>


### [19] [Toward Secure and Reliable PDDL Formalization of Large Language Models with Planner-in-the-Loop Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29700v1)
*Jiamei Jiang,Jiajing Zhang,Feifei Mo,Linjing Li,Daniel Zeng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: NL-to-PDDL规划agent，planner-in-the-loop自改进，可直接迁移至代码优化agent的验证与修复。

TL;DR: 提出NL-PDDL-Bench基准和规划器在环框架，结合LoRA微调、DPO和推理时修复，显著提升大语言模型生成PDDL规范的可执行性和一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在自主系统中需要可执行且可验证的符号规范，但现有形式化方法常导致不可验证或执行失败，影响安全部署。

Method: 构建NL-PDDL-Bench基准；提出规划器在环框架，利用验证器和规划器诊断进行局部修正；开发规划器引导的优化配方，包括LoRA监督微调、离线DPO偏好优化和推理时规划器在环修复。

Result: 在多种模型上，规划器成功率和计划级一致性显著提升，且对难度缩放和跨域变化具有更好的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 外部可验证形式化对于大语言模型在安全敏感规划系统中的可靠部署至关重要，该工作验证了结合规划器反馈的微调方法的有效性。

中文摘要：规划通常需要既可执行又可验证的符号规范。对于部署在自主或决策支持系统中的大语言模型，此类形式化的失败可能导致不可验证的决策、执行失败或不安全的下游行为。我们提出了NL-PDDL-Bench，一个多领域基准，用于自然语言到PDDL规范的构建，具有规划器验证的可执行性和通过对象数量控制的难度缩放。我们进一步提出了一个规划器在环框架，使用验证器和规划器诊断通过局部编辑来修正不可执行的规范。基于此基础设施，我们开发了一种规划器引导的优化配方，结合了参数高效的低秩自适应监督微调、离线规划器派生的偏好对用于直接偏好优化，以及推理时的规划器在环修复，而无需在训练期间进行在线规划器调用。我们还提供了一个统一的评估套件，用于可解析性、可解性、规范相似性以及基于规划器参考的结果感知的计划级一致性。在代表性模型家族上的实验表明，规划器成功率和计划级一致性取得了显著提升，并在难度缩放和跨域变化下具有更好的鲁棒性。这些结果突显了外部可验证形式化对于在安全或安全敏感的规划系统中可靠部署大语言模型的价值。代码和数据可在https://github.com/ibasicplan/NL-PDDL-Bench获取。

Original abstract: Planning often requires symbolic specifications that are both executable and verifiable. For large language models deployed in autonomous or decision-support systems, failures in such formalization may lead to unverifiable decisions, execution failures, or unsafe downstream behavior. We present NL-PDDL-Bench, a multi-domain benchmark for natural-language-to-PDDL specification construction with planner-verified executability and controlled difficulty scaling by object count. We further propose a planner-in-the-loop framework that uses validator and planner diagnostics to revise non-executable specifications through localized edits. Building on this infrastructure, we develop a planner-grounded optimization recipe that combines parameter-efficient Low-Rank Adaptation supervised fine-tuning, offline planner-derived preference pairs for Direct Preference Optimization, and inference-time planner-in-the-loop repair, without requiring online planner calls during training. We also provide a unified evaluation suite for parseability, solvability, specification similarity, and outcome-aware plan-level consistency against planner references. Experiments on representative model families show substantial gains in planner success and plan-level agreement, with improved robustness under difficulty scaling and cross-domain variation. These results highlight the value of externally verifiable formalization for reliable deployment of LLMs in safety- or security-sensitive planning systems. Code and data are available at: https://github.com/ibasicplan/NL-PDDL-Bench

### [20] [GUICrafter: Weakly-Supervised GUI Agent Leveraging Massive Unannotated Screenshots](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29705v1)
*Sunqi Fan,Lingshan Chen,Runqi Yin,Qingle Liu,Yongming Rao,Meng-Hao Guo,Shi-Min Hu*

TL;DR: GUICrafter是一种弱监督GUI智能体，通过课程学习从大量未标注截图训练，仅用0.1%数据即达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前GUI智能体面临数据收集成本高、跨设备泛化差和视觉定位能力有限的问题。

Method: 提出GUICrafter，采用两阶段课程学习：第一阶段从大量未标注截图学习视觉定位，第二阶段用少量高质量数据通过强化学习校准模型。

Result: 仅用0.1%数据即达到与UI-TARS相当或更优性能；相同标注数据量下超越GUI-R1等方法。

Original abstract: Data, as the fundamental substrate of modern intelligence, has greatly driven the development of current foundation models. Naturally, researchers aim to extend this paradigm to the domain of GUI agents, hoping to build strong GUI agents through a similar paradigm. However, GUI agent data cannot be directly harvested from the internet, making it costly and difficult to collect at scale. As a result, current GUI agents suffer from poor cross-device generalization and limited visual grounding ability for fine-grained GUI elements. As an attempt to address data challenge in GUI agents, we propose GUICrafter, a weakly-supervised GUI agent leveraging massive unannotated screenshots to substantially reduce the reliance on expensive human annotations. GUICrafter explores a curriculum learning framework for training GUI agents through two progressive stages. First, the model learns visual grounding from large-scale unannotated screenshots and webpages, leveraging the rich contextual signals inherent in GUI interactions without human annotations. Then, in Stage 2, we leverage a small amount of high-quality data to calibrate the model via reinforcement learning. Experiments show that GUICrafter achieves competitive, or even superior, performance to advanced systems like UI-TARS while using only 0.1% of its data. Furthermore, under the same amount of annotated data, GUICrafter surpasses all previous methods such as GUI-R1. Code, data, and models are available at https://github.com/fansunqi/GUICrafter.

### [21] [DeepTrans Studio: Turning Expert Interventions into Shared Team Knowledge in Agentic Translation Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29727v1)

Original abstract: Professional translation is often a team-based process: translators, reviewers, and project managers must coordinate terminology, legal force, and accountability across documents. Yet many LLM-based translation tools treat human corrections as isolated edits. Expert decisions made in one segment or by one member are rarely captured as reusable knowledge for the rest of the team. We present DeepTrans Studio, a collaborative translation workspace that lets professionals intercept selected nodes in an agentic translation workflow, review evidence, revise AI outputs, and save approved decisions to a shared team memory. During the demo, attendees will role-play translators and reviewers, resolve preset terminology and legal-modal risks, and see how their decisions are propagated to downstream segments and surfaced in a teammate's workspace as reusable precedents. The demo illustrates how human interventions in AI-mediated work can become shared, traceable knowledge rather than one-off corrections.

### [22] [DEEPMED Search: An Open-Source Agentic Platform for Medical Deep Research with Introspective Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29746v1)
*Maolin Liu,Fanyu Xu,Ruoqing Xu,Jiahang Zhang,Hao Wang,Rui Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有商业工具不透明，开源RAG有推理漂移，需要透明可靠的医学研究平台。

Method: 基于Next.js架构，包含源自适应路由器和因果一致多智能体辩论框架的内省验证模块。

Result: 能够自主分解高难度罕见病查询，过滤噪声，快速生成带引用的结构化报告。

中文摘要：在从学术文献（PubMed）到临床指南（网络）和私有知识库的异质性医疗数据洪流中导航，仍然是循证医学的关键瓶颈。虽然商业黑盒工具缺乏透明度，但标准的开源RAG实现在处理复杂的长尾查询时经常出现推理漂移。我们提出了DEEPMED Search，一个完全开源、智能体驱动的平台，专为透明的医学深度研究而设计。基于高性能Next.js架构，DEEPMED Search具有一个源自适应路由器，可根据信息密度自动将子查询分派到PubMed、网络搜索或本地基于图的知识库。关键的是，该平台集成了一个内省验证模块，由因果一致的多智能体辩论框架驱动，在综合之前根据诊断逻辑验证检索到的证据。为了展示其鲁棒性，我们展示了DEEPMED Search能够自主分解高难度罕见病查询、过滤混淆噪声，并在几分钟内生成结构化的、带有引用的研究报告。通过开源此软件，我们为社区提供了强大的基础设施，以在研究原型设计中民主化获取可信的、玻璃盒式的医学推理。

Original abstract: Navigating the deluge of heterogeneous medical data, from academic literature (PubMed) to clinical guidelines (Web) and private knowledge bases, remains a critical bottleneck for evidence-based medicine. While commercial black-box tools lack transparency, standard open-source RAG implementations frequently suffer from reasoning drift when handling complex, long-tail queries. We present DEEPMED Search, a fully open-source, agentic platform designed for transparent medical deep research. Built on a high-performance Next.js architecture, DEEPMED Search features a source-adaptive router that autonomously dispatches sub-queries to PubMed, web search, or local graph-based knowledge bases based on information density. Crucially, the platform integrates an introspective verification module, powered by a causal-consistent multi-agent debate framework, to validate retrieved evidence against diagnostic logic before synthesis. To demonstrate its robustness, we showcase DEEPMED Search's ability to autonomously decompose high-difficulty rare disease queries, filter out confounding noise, and generate structured, citation-backed research reports in minutes. By open-sourcing this software, we provide the community with a robust infrastructure to democratize access to trustworthy, glass-box medical reasoning in research and prototyping settings.

### [23] [CLQT: A Closed-Loop, Cost-Aware, Strategy-Consistent Benchmark for Diagnostic Evaluation of LLM Portfolio-Management Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29771v1)
*Bo Qu,Mingguang Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出LLM投资组合agent的诊断性基准和五轴能力评分卡，评测方法对coding agent有借鉴意义。

TL;DR: CLQT是一个将闭环交易评估从排名转向诊断的框架，通过细粒度审计和五轴能力评分卡来定位LLM代理在交易过程中的成功与失败原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于收益的代理排名无法区分市场走势和真实能力，且容易受前瞻性泄漏影响，因此需要一种新的评估方法，能够诊断代理的推理过程、策略一致性和持久优势，而非仅仅比较收益。

Method: CLQT构建了一个完全闭环、成本感知、策略一致、时间门控的环境，代理运行五阶段循环（收集、综合、分配、执行、反思），每轮生成可验证的哈希链决策轮次。通过六大支柱（硬时间门控、成本建模、策略一致性评分、三层记忆、工具层、授权感知）支撑，并设计五轴能力评分卡（一致性、敏锐度、沉着性、纪律性、可靠性），其中一致性由外部LLM评判以避免自偏好。

Result: 在污染控制的多模型回测和实时数据上验证，CLQT能够将结果与能力分离，识别代理的具体优势和局限，而非仅给出排名，且评分卡具有可重复性和可解释性。

Conclusion: CLQT提供了一种替代排名的评估范式，通过诊断代理的决策过程来揭示其真实能力，为LLM代理在金融领域的应用提供了更可靠的评估基础，并支持持续改进和审计。

中文摘要：LLM代理越来越多地被赋予自主投资组合管理角色，基准测试已从金融问答转向序列交易。然而，大多数基准测试仍然根据固定窗口内的收益对代理进行排名——这是一种较弱的代理指标，因为一个时期的收益主要受市场路径主导，且一旦控制了前瞻性泄漏，表面的阿尔法就可能消失。这种排名既不能证明合理的推理、一致的策略，也不能证明持久的优势。我们引入了CLQT，它将闭环交易评估重新定义为诊断而非排名：一种定位代理过程在何处以及为何成功或失败的工具。CLQT是一个完全闭环、成本感知、策略一致、时间门控的环境，其代理运行一个五阶段循环：收集、综合、分配、执行、反思。每轮生成一个完整的决策轮次，并密封到可重新计算验证的哈希链中，因此每个指标都可以从痕迹中重建。六个支柱构成了基础：硬性时间门控、机构交易和融资成本建模、策略一致性评分、三层记忆、模型-上下文-协议工具层以及授权感知综合。同一代理可以作为约束委员会（专业化角色）或单全自主编排器运行，使过程架构成为实验变量。从审计轨迹中，我们计算一个五轴能力评分卡（APM-CS：一致性、敏锐度、沉着性、纪律性、可靠性），其中一致性部分由持有、队列外的LLM评判，以抑制自我偏好偏差。我们在受污染控制的多模型回测上（带有消融网格）以及在实时经纪商轨迹上（针对未见过的、截止后的数据）进行验证，并与重复运行的噪声下限进行比较。CLQT将结果与能力分离，产生的不是模型排名，而是代理能力和局限性的持久、可扩展地图。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly cast as autonomous portfolio managers, and benchmarks have moved from financial question-answering to sequential trading. Yet most still rank agents by returns over a fixed window -- a weak proxy, since a period's return is dominated by the market path and apparent alpha can dissolve once look-ahead leakage is controlled. Such a ranking certifies neither sound reasoning, nor a consistent strategy, nor a durable edge. We introduce CLQT, which reframes closed-loop trading evaluation as diagnosis rather than ranking: an instrument that localizes where and why an agent's process succeeds or fails. CLQT is a fully closed-loop, cost-aware, strategy-consistent, temporally-gated environment whose agents run a five-stage cycle: gather, synthesize, allocate, execute, reflect. Each round emits a complete DecisionRound sealed into a recompute-verifiable hash chain, so every metric is reconstructable from the trail. Six pillars form the substrate: a hard TimeGate, institutional transaction- and financing-cost modeling, strategy-consistency scoring, three-tier memory, a Model-Context-Protocol tool layer, and mandate-aware synthesis. The same agent runs as a constrained committee of specialized roles or a single full-autonomy orchestrator, making process scaffolding an experimental variable. From the audit trail we compute a five-axis capability scorecard (APM-CS: Coherence, Acuity, Composure, Discipline, Reliability), with Coherence judged partly by a held-out, out-of-cohort LLM to curb self-preference bias. We validate it on a contamination-controlled multi-model backtest with an ablation grid and a live broker track on unseen, post-cutoff data, against a repeated-run noise floor. CLQT separates outcome from capability, yielding not a model ranking but a durable, extensible map of agent competencies and limitations.

</details>


### [24] [The CRISTAL Method: Neurosymbolic analysis from AI-synthesized world models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29799v1)
*Rafael Kaufmann,Felix Neubürger,Michael Walters,Thomas Kopinski,Dimitrije Marković*

Selection reason: 神经符号分析框架，LLM生成代码并持续学习，方法可用于agent推理与代码生成。

TL;DR: CRISTAL是一个神经符号框架，通过统计模型合成、持续学习和主动学习实现复杂分析自动化，在投资分析中仅用少量样本和计算即可达到贝叶斯最优精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类分析师存在认知偏差，LLM智能体在数值推理、不确定性感知和可重复性方面存在局限，亟需更有效的自动化分析框架。

Method: CRISTAL结合统计模型合成、持续学习和主动学习，从自然语言先验知识课程构建动态可解释概率程序，实现完整贝叶斯推理和预算感知数据采集，并利用LLM进行代码合成。

Result: 在合成股票分类任务中，CRISTAL仅用5个样本和5秒预算达到贝叶斯最优精度，而最先进LLM在更多数据和计算下精度仅约40%。

Conclusion: CRISTAL通过神经符号方法有效克服了LLM在复杂分析中的局限，实现了高效、准确且可解释的自动化分析。

中文摘要：本项目介绍了CRISTAL方法（Coherent Reliable Intentional Synthesis of Truthful Analysis Logic），这是一个神经符号框架，用于自动化复杂分析工作流，以基本面投资分析为主要用例。该领域面临重大挑战：高结构不确定性、嘈杂和主观的数据、紧张的注意力预算，以及需要合理且可重复的决策。人类分析师由于认知偏差和局限性常常在这个领域挣扎，这表明自动化的巨大价值。但是，尽管基于LLM的智能体被提议作为分析辅助工具，它们的局限性——糟糕的数值推理、对不确定性的无意识以及缺乏可重复性——阻碍了它们在此背景下的有效性。CRISTAL通过统计模型合成、持续学习和主动学习的原理混合来解决这些差距。从自然语言先验知识课程开始，CRISTAL构建了一个动态、可解释的概率程序，实现了完整的贝叶斯推理，包括不确定性量化和预算敏感的数据采集。CRISTAL在分析过程中不断优化其世界模型，利用LLM进行代码合成和学习。我们在一个包含丰富财务和文本数据的合成股票新基准上验证了CRISTAL。在一个公司分类任务中，CRISTAL仅用5个样本和5秒预算就实现了贝叶斯最优精度，超过了最先进的LLM，后者即使使用数量级更多的输入数据和计算，精度也徘徊在40%左右。

Original abstract: This project introduces the CRISTAL Method (Coherent Reliable Intentional Synthesis of Truthful Analysis Logic), a neurosymbolic framework for automating complex analysis workflows, with fundamental investment analysis as a primary use case. This domain poses major challenges: high structural uncertainty, noisy and subjective data, tight attention budgets, and the need for justified, reproducible decisions. Human analysts often struggle in this domain due to cognitive biases and limitations, suggesting significant value in automation. But while LLM-based agents have been proposed as analytical aids, their limitations -- poor numerical reasoning, unawareness of uncertainty, and lack of reproducibility -- hinder their effectiveness in this context. CRISTAL addresses these gaps through a principled blend of statistical model synthesis, continuous learning, and active learning. Starting from a natural-language prior knowledge curriculum, CRISTAL builds a dynamic, interpretable probabilistic program that enables full Bayesian inference, including uncertainty quantification and budget-aware data acquisition. CRISTAL continually refines its world model during analysis, leveraging LLMs for code synthesis and learning. We validate CRISTAL on a novel benchmark of synthetic equities with rich financial and textual data. On a company classification task, CRISTAL achieves Bayes-optimal accuracy with just 5 examples and a 5-second budget, outperforming state-of-the-art LLMs that plateau around 40\% accuracy even with order-of-magnitude more input data and compute.

### [25] [AI Training Manager: Bounded Closed-Loop Control of Adaptive Training Recipes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29871v1)
*Anjali Rao,Nikhil Kamalkumar Advani*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出LLM作为监督控制器管理训练，具有bounded closed-loop控制，属于通用agent方法，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出一个基于LLM的有界监督控制器（AI训练管理器），通过读取训练遥测数据并调整参数，在语言建模和强化学习中有效纠正过拟合、不平衡等问题，性能显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准训练流程依赖固定配方或单轴调度器，无法应对过拟合、损失不平衡、探索崩溃等中运行故障，且现有方法缺乏可解释的多轴干预能力。

Method: 设计基于LLM的监督控制器，通过模式条件接口读取结构化遥测快照，在受限动作空间内返回验证过的参数更新（如学习率、正则化等），支持异步应用更新而不阻塞训练循环。

Result: 在TinyStories上验证损失降低60%，在机器人强化学习任务中缓解保守和不安全探索，生成可审计日志。

Conclusion: 模式条件的LLM可作为有界监督管理器，为实时训练提供可解释的多轴干预，补充传统优化器和调度器。

中文摘要：我们提出了AI训练管理器，一个基于LLM的有界监督控制器，用于自适应机器学习训练。标准训练流程通常依赖于固定配方或单轴调度器，这可能在运行中遇到严重过拟合、损失不平衡、探索崩溃或不安全探索等故障。该管理器并非取代数学优化器或作为无约束的编码代理，而是通过一个模式条件接口运作：它从正在运行的训练中读取结构化遥测快照，审查一个受限的动作空间，并返回对训练参数（如学习率、正则化强度、损失权重系数和探索设置）的验证更新。我们在监督语言建模和强化学习上评估了这种架构。在TinyStories数据集上，管理器检测并纠正了过拟合，实现了比基线低60%的验证损失，同时生成可审计的干预日志。在这个监督设置中，我们还展示了管理器推理不需要阻塞训练循环：训练可以在等待管理器响应时继续，验证更新可以在可用时异步应用。在机器人操作强化学习任务中，我们在一个 episodic 闭环设置中使用相同的边界决策接口，其中管理器更新在评估或检查点边界处应用。该管理器缓解了保守和不安全的探索模式。这些结果表明，模式条件的LLM可以作为实时训练运行的有界监督管理器，以可解释的多轴干预能力补充传统的优化器和调度器。

Original abstract: We present the AI Training Manager, a bounded LLM-based supervisory controller for adaptive machine learning training. Standard training pipelines often rely on fixed recipes or single-axis schedulers, which can struggle with mid-run failures such as severe overfitting, loss imbalance, exploration collapse, or unsafe exploration. Rather than replacing mathematical optimizers or acting as an unconstrained coding agent, the manager operates through a schema-conditioned interface: it reads structured telemetry snapshots from an active run, audits a constrained action space, and returns validated updates to training parameters such as learning rate, regularization strength, loss-weight coefficients, and exploration settings. We evaluate this architecture across supervised language modeling and reinforcement learning. On TinyStories, the manager detects and corrects overfitting, achieving a validation loss 60% lower than the baseline while producing auditable intervention logs. In this supervised setting, we additionally show that manager inference does not need to block the training loop: training can continue while a manager response is pending, and validated updates can be applied asynchronously once available. In a robotic manipulation reinforcement-learning task, we use the same bounded decision interface in an episodic closed-loop setting, where manager updates are applied at evaluation or checkpoint boundaries. The manager mitigates both conservative and unsafe exploration regimes. These results suggest that schema-conditioned LLMs can serve as bounded supervisory managers for live training runs, complementing conventional optimizers and schedulers with interpretable, multi-axis intervention capabilities

### [26] [SafePyramid: A Hierarchical Benchmark for In-context Policy Guardrailing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29887v1)
*Jiacheng Zhang,Haoyu He,Sen Zhang,Shen Wang,Xiaolei Xu,Yuhao Sun,Meng Shen,Feng Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 面向in-context policy guardrailing的benchmark，涉及LLM agent安全控制，可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出SafePyramid基准评估上下文策略护栏，发现当前模型表现差，GPT-5.5在最高难度仅12.9%完全识别违规规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实应用中护栏需根据应用特定策略而非预定义分类识别不安全交互，现有方法不足，需系统性评估。

Method: 构建SafePyramid基准，含1000个多轮对话、3000个策略、61699条规则，分三级难度；用多阶段流水线确保质量；评估10个LLM和5个护栏。

Result: 上下文策略护栏挑战大，GPT-5.5在L0/L1/L2完全识别违规规则率仅54.0%/35.3%/12.9%。

Conclusion: 当前护栏局限，需更强上下文策略护栏以可靠执行策略、处理依赖和适应新框架。

中文摘要：在实际应用中，护栏通常需要根据应用特定的安全策略来识别不安全的用户-模型交互，而不是依赖预定义的风险分类。在这项工作中，我们研究了上下文策略护栏范式下的这一设置，其中护栏根据上下文中提供的策略规范来预测安全违规行为。为了系统性地评估这种能力，我们引入了SafePyramid，一个包含1000个跨10个领域的多轮对话和3000个相应应用特定策略的安全基准，这些策略总共包含61,699条不同的自然语言规则。SafePyramid将评估组织为三个难度级别：L0评估单规则理解，L1评估规则依赖推理，L2评估对上下文中定义的完整新颖策略框架的适应。为了确保基准质量，我们采用严格的流水线多阶段构建和验证基准。使用SafePyramid，我们评估了10个前沿LLM和5个策略可配置护栏，发现上下文策略护栏仍然极具挑战性：即使表现最好的模型GPT-5.5，在L0、L1和L2上分别仅有54.0%、35.3%和12.9%的情况下完全识别了违规规则集。这些结果凸显了当前护栏的局限性，并呼吁更强大的上下文策略护栏，能够可靠地执行策略、解决规则依赖并适应新颖的策略框架。

Original abstract: In real-world applications, guardrails are often expected to identify unsafe user-model interactions according to application-specific safety policies, rather than relying on predefined risk taxonomies. In this work, we study this setting under the paradigm of in-context policy guardrailing, where guardrails predict safety violations based on policy specifications provided in context. To systematically evaluate this capability, we introduce SafePyramid, a safety benchmark comprising 1,000 multi-turn conversations across 10 domains and 3,000 corresponding application-specific policies, which together contain 61,699 distinct natural-language rules. SafePyramid organizes the evaluation into three difficulty levels: L0 evaluates individual-rule understanding, L1 evaluates reasoning over rule dependencies, and L2 evaluates adaptation of full novel policy frameworks defined in context. To ensure benchmark quality, we employ a rigorous multi-stage pipeline to construct and validate the benchmark. Using SafePyramid, we evaluate 10 frontier LLMs and 5 policy-configurable guardrails and find that in-context policy guardrailing remains highly challenging: even the best-performing model, GPT-5.5, exactly identifies the full set of violated rules in only 54.0%, 35.3%, and 12.9% cases on L0, L1, and L2, respectively. These results highlight the limitations of current guardrails and call for stronger in-context policy guardrails that can reliably execute policies, resolve rule dependencies, and adapt to novel policy frameworks.

### [27] [HippoSpark: An On-Demand Experience System for LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29929v1)
*Jingyao Liu,Danling Meng,Chen Huang,Yukun Yan,Zhenghao Liu,Wenqiang Lei,See-Kiong Ng,Maosong Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM推理的状态级经验系统，按需检索，可迁移至coding agent的规划与经验复用。

TL;DR: 提出HippoSpark，一种状态级别的经验系统，通过在关键推理瓶颈处进行按需检索，显著提升复杂推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多在任务层面提供通用经验，难以解决复杂推理中的局部瓶颈问题，需要更精细的状态级指导。

Method: 构建状态级经验系统，根据当前推理状态按需检索相关经验，提供精确指导。

Result: 在数学、科学和编程基准测试中，HippoSpark优于标准提示和任务级经验方法。

Conclusion: 最有效的经验系统应在关键瓶颈处提供可操作指导，而非通用任务上下文。

中文摘要：将历史轨迹提炼为可复用的经验以增强未来问题解决能力已成为近期大语言模型研究的焦点。然而，现有方法主要在任务层面运作，基于通用摘要或规则，假设类似任务共享通用的解决方案模式。这种方法在复杂推理中常常失败，因为复杂推理通常会在局部瓶颈处出错，需要精确的、特定于状态的指导，而非宽泛的启发式方法。我们引入了HippoSpark，一个状态级别的经验系统，它根据当前推理状态的即时需求进行按需检索。在数学、科学和编程基准测试中，HippoSpark始终优于标准提示和任务级经验基线。我们的研究结果表明，最有效的经验系统是在关键瓶颈处提供可操作指导的系统，而非作为通用任务级上下文。我们的代码可在https://github.com/DanlingMeng/HippoSpark获取。

Original abstract: Distilling historical trajectories into reusable experience to enhance future problem-solving has become a focal point of recent LLM research. However, existing methods predominantly operate at the task level, leveraging general summaries or rules under the assumption that analogous tasks share universal solution patterns. This approach often fails in complex reasoning, which typically falters at local bottlenecks that require precise, state-specific guidance rather than broad heuristics. We introduce HippoSpark, a state-level experience system that performs on-demand retrieval tailored to the immediate needs of the current reasoning state. Across mathematical, scientific, and programming benchmarks, HippoSpark consistently outperforms both standard prompting and task-level experience baselines. Our findings reveal that the most effective experience systems are those that provide actionable guidance at critical bottlenecks rather than serving as generic task-level context. Our code is available at https://github.com/DanlingMeng/HippoSpark.

### [28] [SAGA: Scene-Aware, Goal-Evolving Agents for Long-Horizon Strategy Game Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29932v3)
*Tianyu Jin,Shuo Chen,Yida Wang,Liuyu Xiang,Yingzhuo Liu,Zhiyao Jiang,Yexin Li,Peipei Li,Zhaofeng He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent长程策略规划框架，包含场景图、工具增强、双环反馈，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: SAGA是一个LLM多智能体框架，通过场景图、工具增强规划和双视野反馈循环解决长期战略规划中的上下文溢出、关系稀疏和奖励滞后问题，在CivRealm中取得最高得分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在长期战略规划中面临三个挑战：从原始坐标中恢复关系结构不足；序列化整个状态导致上下文溢出且紧急领域排挤长期领域；仅靠滞后最终得分缺乏进度信号。

Method: 提出SAGA框架，包含三个机制：地图语义场景图（Map-Semantic Scene Graph）将实体关系渲染为简洁文本；工具增强规划器（Tool-Augmented Planner）按需检索状态并路由领域指令；双视野反馈循环（Dual-Horizon Feedback Loop）设置中间目标并跨游戏提炼因果教训。

Result: 在CivRealm基准上，SAGA在六种方法中取得最高平均最终得分，基础设施增益统计最强，输出token减少27%，启用跨游戏进化后连续五场游戏得分最高。

Conclusion: SAGA通过结构化表示、按需规划和多视野反馈有效提升了长期战略规划中的LLM智能体性能。

中文摘要：在复杂策略游戏中，长期战略规划需要协调紧密耦合的决策领域，包括技术、经济、外交和军事，在数百回合中面对不完美信息。现有的基于LLM的智能体在这种设置下面临三个挑战。它们从原始坐标观测中恢复出很少的关系结构，如距离或威胁。它们将整个不断增长的博弈状态序列化到每个提示中，并在单个输出中规划所有领域，因此上下文最终溢出，紧急领域排挤长期领域。唯一的奖励是滞后的最终得分，它在游戏内或游戏间不提供进度信号。<br/><br/>我们提出了SAGA，一个LLM多智能体框架，通过三种机制应对这些挑战：一个地图语义场景图，将类型化的实体关系渲染为简洁的每个实体文本；一个工具增强规划器，按需检索状态并将不相交的每个领域指令路由到专家控制器；以及一个双视野反馈循环，在游戏内设置中间目标并在游戏间提炼因果教训。在基于策略游戏FreeCiv的基准CivRealm上，SAGA在六种方法中取得了最高的平均最终得分，在基础设施上取得了统计上最强的增益，并减少了27%的输出token。启用跨游戏进化后，它在连续五场游戏中达到了最高得分。

Original abstract: Long-horizon strategic planning in complex strategy games requires coordinating tightly coupled decision domains, including technology, economy, diplomacy, and military, across hundreds of turns under imperfect information. Existing LLM-based agents face three challenges in this setting. They recover little relational structure, such as distance or threat, from raw coordinate observations. They serialize the entire growing game state into every prompt and plan all domains in a single output, so the context eventually overflows and urgent domains crowd out long-term ones. The only reward is a lagged final score, which provides no progress signal within or across games.<br/><br/>We present SAGA, an LLM multi-agent framework that addresses these challenges with three mechanisms: a Map-Semantic Scene Graph that renders typed entity relations as concise per-entity text, a Tool-Augmented Planner that retrieves state on demand and routes disjoint per-domain directives to specialist controllers, and a Dual-Horizon Feedback Loop that sets intermediate goals within a game and distills causal lessons across games. On CivRealm, a benchmark built on the strategy game FreeCiv, SAGA attains the highest mean final score among six methods, the statistically strongest gains on infrastructure, and a 27% reduction in output tokens. With cross-game evolution enabled, it reaches the highest score over five successive games.

### [29] [AlgoSkill: Learning to Design Algorithms by Scheduling Human-Like Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29999v1)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai,Liang Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出AlgoSkill框架，将算法设计分解为类型化技能序列决策，结合MCTS和验证反馈，显著提升算法生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM方法在算法设计中缺乏对问题结构显式建模和多步推理，导致隐含步骤和性能瓶颈。

Method: 构建类型化算法技能库，使用学习调度器按设计状态推荐技能，并通过MCTS搜索技能序列，利用编译、测试、压力测试和复杂度分析的反馈进行验证和修复。

Result: 在竞争性编程和组合优化基准上，AlgoSkill优于直接生成、思维链提示、自优化和无类型MCTS；消融实验证实各组件均有贡献。

Conclusion: 自动算法设计应被建模为验证引导的技能调度，而非一次性生成，强调结构化推理和反馈迭代。

中文摘要：从自然语言问题陈述设计算法需要识别问题结构、阅读约束、选择合适的范式、检查正确性以及优化复杂性。现有的大语言模型（LLM）方法通常依赖于直接生成或通用的自我优化，使这些步骤隐含。我们提出AlgoSkill，它将算法设计建模为对类型化算法技能库的序列决策，包括抽象、约束分析、状态设计、数据结构选择、证明检查、反例构建和复杂性优化。一个学习的调度器从当前设计状态提出技能，而蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）控制器利用编译、测试、压力测试和复杂性分析的验证反馈来探索技能序列。在竞争性编程和组合优化基准上的实验表明，AlgoSkill优于直接LLM生成、思维链提示、自我优化以及无类型技能的MCTS。消融实验表明，类型化技能、基于验证的修复和基于搜索的调度各自对性能有贡献。这些结果支持将自动算法设计视为验证引导的技能调度，而非一次性代码生成。

Original abstract: Designing an algorithm from a natural-language problem statement requires identifying the problem structure, reading constraints, choosing a suitable paradigm, checking correctness, and refining complexity. Existing large language model (LLM) methods often rely on direct generation or generic self-refinement, leaving these steps implicit. We propose AlgoSkill, which models algorithm design as sequential decision-making over a typed library of algorithmic skills, including abstraction, constraint analysis, state design, data-structure selection, proof checking, counterexample construction, and complexity refinement. A learned scheduler proposes skills from the current design state, while a Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) controller explores skill sequences using verification feedback from compilation, testing, stress testing, and complexity analysis. Experiments on competitive programming and combinatorial optimization benchmarks show that AlgoSkill improves over direct LLM generation, chain-of-thought prompting, self-refinement, and MCTS without typed skills. Ablations show that typed skills, verification-based repair, and search-based scheduling each contribute to performance. These results support treating automatic algorithm design as verification-guided skill scheduling rather than one-shot code generation.

</details>


### [30] [ACPO: Agent-Chained Policy Optimization for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30072v1)
*Daiki E. Matsunaga,Junho Na,Tri Wahyu Guntara,Scott Sanner,Pascal Poupart,Jongmin Lee,Kee-Eung Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多智能体策略梯度分解的ACPO算法，属于多agent协作通用方法。

TL;DR: 提出智能体链式策略优化（ACPO），通过序列化联合决策的信念机制实现联合策略梯度的精确分散分解，在多智能体协作任务中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CTDE下策略梯度方法要么缺乏联合改进保证，要么收敛到次优纳什均衡，需要一种能保证精确联合梯度更新的分散策略梯度方法。

Method: 基于联合策略梯度的精确分散分解，提出ACPO，通过序列化决策中智能体对先前动作的信念作为协调机制，实现独立演员更新的联合梯度步骤。

Result: 在多机器人仓库、SMACv2和MA-MuJoCo上，ACPO优于强基线，且随着智能体数量增加优势扩大。

Conclusion: ACPO通过序列化信念机制实现了有效的分散联合策略优化，为大规模多智能体协作提供新方法。

中文摘要：多智能体强化学习（MARL）中的协作任务要求智能体共同最大化共享回报。在集中训练与分散执行（CTDE）范式下，策略梯度一直难以直接计算。先前的方法主要遵循两种思路：一种是使用集中式评论家的独立分解更新，但缺乏没有价值分解假设的通用联合改进保证；另一种是交替最佳响应更新，这可能会收敛到次优的纳什均衡。在本文中，我们展示了联合策略梯度允许每个智能体项的精确分散分解，每个项由每个智能体的得分函数和分散评论家构成。基于这种分解，我们开发了智能体链式策略优化（ACPO），其中演员独立训练，它们的更新共同构成联合策略梯度上的单一步骤。这一结果的核心是对同时联合决策的序列化视图，其中智能体一次一个地提交动作，每个动作基于对先前动作的信念进行条件化。该信念充当协调机制，将独立的每个智能体更新捆绑成联合梯度步骤。我们在多机器人仓库、SMACv2和MA-MuJoCo上评估了ACPO，它在强基线上表现优越，并且随着智能体数量的增加，差距扩大。

Original abstract: Cooperative tasks in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) require agents to collectively maximize a shared return. Under the Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) paradigm, policy gradients have remained difficult to compute directly. Prior methods largely follow two approaches: independent factorized updates with centralized critics, which lack general joint-improvement guarantees without value decomposition assumptions, or alternating best-response updates, which can converge to suboptimal Nash Equilibria. In this paper, we show the joint policy gradient admits an exact decentralized decomposition of per-agent terms, each formed from per-agent score functions and decentralized critics. Based on this decomposition, we develop Agent-Chained Policy Optimization (ACPO), where actors are trained independently, with their updates together constituting a single step on the joint policy gradient. Central to this result is a serialized view of the simultaneous joint decision in which agents commit actions one at a time, each conditioning on a belief over preceding actions. The belief acts as the coordination mechanism which ties the independent per-agent updates into a joint gradient step. We evaluate ACPO on Multi-Robot Warehouse, SMACv2, and MA-MuJoCo, where it outperforms strong baselines, with the gap widening as the number of agents grows.

</details>


### [31] [Structural Certification for Reliable Physical Design with Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30107v1)
*Nakul Vyas,Iliya D. Stoev*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出propose-certify循环，可迁移为agent验证框架。

TL;DR: 提出物理锚定认证（PHACT），通过将断言权从模型移出给确定性引擎，实现零错误认证，保证物理设计可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型不可靠，直接输出物理设计可能包含错误，需要一种机制确保设计的正确性。

Method: 采用提出-认证循环，模型仅提出设计，由确定性引擎基于固定输入计算认证量，返回认证、不可能或未知，从结构上防止伪造。

Result: 在跨越两个模型、两种解码温度和故意出错的引擎的80次对抗性试验中，未产生任何错误认证。

Conclusion: PHACT通过将认证权从模型转移至确定性引擎，有效防止了伪造，确保了物理设计的可靠性。

中文摘要：一个不可靠的语言模型可以被制作成产生可靠物理设计，如果将断言权限移出模型：模型提出，仅由确定性引擎认证，返回已认证、不可能或未知。我们引入了物理锚定认证（PHACT），一个跨越五个科学领域的提出-认证循环，并确定了使此类证书值得信赖的因素。接受模型提供值的检查器可能被篡改；而从固定输入推导出认证量则从结构上使得伪造不可能。在跨越两个模型、两种解码温度和故意出错的引擎的八十次对抗性试验中，该合约产生了零次错误认证。

Original abstract: An unreliable language model can be made to produce reliable physical designs if the authority to assert is moved out of the model: the model proposes, and a deterministic engine alone certifies, returning certified, impossible, or unknown. We introduce Physics-Anchored Certification (PHACT), a propose-certify loop spanning five scientific domains, and identify what makes such a certificate trustworthy. A checker that accepts a model-supplied value can be forged; deriving the certified quantity from fixed inputs instead makes forgery impossible by construction. Across eighty adversarial trials spanning two models, two decoding temperatures, and a deliberately faulted engine, this contract produced zero false certifications.
