### [32] [Does Verbose Chain-of-Thought Really Help? In-Distribution Evidence that Content, Not Length, Matters](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30128v1)
*Wenlong Wang,Fergal Reid*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析CoT有效性的来源，对agent推理组件有启发。

TL;DR: CoT提示中的额外token本身并非关键，其携带的推理和验证内容才是提升LLM推理准确率的核心因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究CoT提示中中间步骤的有效性来源：是语义内容还是额外计算？

Method: 通过两个实验：1) 分布内比较同一问题下模型自身生成的短、长轨迹；2) 控制干预，比较相同语义但不同冗长度的轨迹，使用双验证器设计。

Result: 额外token对准确率无本质影响，增益源于验证内容；冗长轨迹提高准确率但效果有限（1-4%），且依赖于内容质量而非长度；最大数值编辑下效果放大，填充无作用。

Conclusion: CoT的有效性取决于额外token携带的推理和验证内容，而非数量，既非纯计算也非纯语义解释。

中文摘要：思维链（CoT）提示提高了LLM的推理能力，但其来源存有争议：中间步骤之所以有帮助，是因为它们承载了有用的语义内容，还是因为以更多token为条件，在模型承诺答案之前购买了额外的计算？我们带来了两条证据线。首先，在分布内：我们在同一问题上对每个模型重复采样，并将遵循相同推理计划的、模型自身自然生成的较短序列与较长序列配对，因此没有重写任何内容，两条轨迹都真正处于分布内。在25个模型中，额外的token对于每个独立训练的推理者的准确率基本没有改变，而对剩余token的盲分析表明，在别处存在的增益与验证和检查内容相关，而非冗长本身。其次，作为一种受控干预，我们询问两个表达相同语义内容（相同的事实、操作和中间值，通过有向无环图等价性验证）的轨迹，当其中一个更冗长时，是否会产生不同的结果，使用双验证器设计，涵盖四个目标和八个基准，采用数字编辑完成和分层自举置信区间。冗长的轨迹确实提高了准确率（在32个基准-目标组合中，有25个在至少一个验证器下为正），但效果有限（通常为1-4个百分点），并且取决于冗长散文的质量，而不仅仅是其长度。在最大数值编辑下，效果被放大（四个算术基准的中位数为3.24倍），而长度匹配的非推理填充则无法恢复任何效果。两条线汇聚：重要的是额外token做了什么（它们携带的推理和验证内容），而不是有多少个，这种情形既非纯粹的前向传递计算解释，也非纯粹的语义内容解释能完全说明。

Original abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting improves LLM reasoning, but the source is contested: do the intermediate steps help because they carry useful semantic content, or because conditioning on more tokens buys extra computation before the model commits to an answer? We bring two lines of evidence to bear. First, in distribution: we repeatedly sample each model on the same question and pair a shorter with a longer of its own natural generations that follow the same reasoning plan, so nothing is rewritten and both traces are genuinely in-distribution. Across 25 models the extra tokens leave accuracy essentially unchanged for every independently-trained reasoner, and a blind analysis of the surplus tokens shows that what gain exists elsewhere tracks validation- and checking-content, not verbosity per se. Second, as a controlled intervention, we ask whether two traces expressing the same semantic content (the same facts, operations, and intermediate values, verified through directed acyclic graph equivalence) produce different outcomes when one is more verbose, using a dual-validator design across four targets and eight benchmarks with number-redacted completion and stratified bootstrap confidence intervals. Verbose traces do improve accuracy (25 of 32 benchmark-target cells are positive under at least one validator), but the effects are modest (typically 1-4 points) and depend on the quality of the verbose prose, not merely its length. Under maximum numerical redaction the effect is amplified (median 3.24x across four arithmetic benchmarks), and length-matched non-reasoning filler recovers none of it. Both lines converge: what matters is what the extra tokens do (the reasoning and validation content they carry), not how many there are, a picture neither a pure forward-pass-compute nor a pure semantic-content account fully explains.

</details>


### [33] [Relevance Is Not Permission: Warranted Attention for Value Contributions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30139v2)
*Minwoo Yu,Young-guk Ha*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 注意力机制改进，可迁移至agent的信用分配。

TL;DR: 提出Warrant方法，通过路径本地化许可机制区分相关性许可，提升多种预测任务的指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 注意力机制带来的相关性不等于预测证据，需要引入许可机制来确保加权值项真正成为证据。

Method: 提出Warrant，一种路径本地化接口，保留注意力相关性alpha_ij，暴露值路径，并学习查询-项许可g_ij，将加权值项转化为alpha_ij * g_ij * v_j。

Result: 在CTDG、MTPP、RAG、STPP、TKG等任务上，Warrant在32次比较中27次提升主要指标，正确路径放置优于基线，消融实验表明增益来源不同。

Conclusion: 预测证据不是注意力质量，加权值项只有在路径上被许可时才成为证据。

中文摘要：相关性不等于许可。注意力机制允许模型读取与当前查询相关的键值项，但并不能保证该项的值贡献成为预测证据。检索到的段落可能与问题相关但不构成支持证据，历史事实或时间邻域甚至可能模糊真实尾部排名或当前边的分数。本文将这一差距形式化为加权值项 alpha_ij * v_j（实际添加到预测路径上）的许可问题。我们提出了Warrant，一种路径本地化接口，它保留注意力相关性 alpha_ij，暴露通向主要指标的值路径，并在完整模型中将 alpha_ij * v_j 通过学习的查询-项许可 g_ij 转换为 alpha_ij * g_ij * v_j。我们将相同的操作符应用于CTDG链接预测、MTPP下一标记排名、RAG支持证据选择、STPP下一位置预测和TKG尾部预测的指标定义值路径上。在32次配对比较、3个随机种子和总计192次运行中，Warrant在27次比较中改进了主要指标；实际效果层级包括10次显著效果、1次边际效果、8次正向但不确定效果、8次持平/可忽略效果和5次下降。在路径定位检查中，正确路径放置在每个领域都优于方向感知的Base性能，并且在CTDG上超过通用注意力放置+0.1076 AUC，在TKG上超过+0.0683 MRR。消融实验表明，TKG的大部分增益来自历史尾部值路径暴露，而CTDG的核心增益来自边条件查询-项许可。总之，预测证据不是注意力质量。加权值项只有当它在通往指标的路径上被许可时才成为证据。

Original abstract: Relevance is not permission. Attention lets a model read key-value items related to the current query, but it does not guarantee that the value contribution of such an item becomes prediction evidence. A retrieved passage may be relevant to a question without being supporting evidence, and a historical fact or temporal neighbor may even blur true-tail ranking or the current edge score. This paper formalizes this gap as a permission problem for the weighted value term alpha_ij * v_j that is actually added to the prediction path. We propose Warrant, a path-localized interface that preserves attention relevance alpha_ij, exposes the value path leading to the primary metric, and, in the full model, turns alpha_ij * v_j into alpha_ij * g_ij * v_j through learned query-item permission g_ij. We place the same operator on the metric-defining value paths of CTDG link prediction, MTPP next-mark ranking, RAG supporting evidence selection, STPP next-location forecasting, and TKG tail prediction. Across 32 paired comparisons, 3 seeds, and 192 total runs, Warrant improves the primary metric in 27 comparisons; practical tiers consist of 10 substantial effects, 1 marginal effect, 8 positive but uncertain effects, 8 tie/negligible effects, and 5 drops. In the path-localization check, correct-path placement outperforms direction-aware Base performance in every domain and exceeds generic attention placement by +0.1076 AUC in CTDG and +0.0683 MRR in TKG. Ablations show that most TKG gains come from historical-tail value path exposure, whereas the core CTDG gain comes from edge-conditioned query-item permission. In conclusion, prediction evidence is not attention mass. A weighted value term becomes evidence only when it is warranted on the path to the metric.

</details>


### [34] [MirrorCode: AI can rebuild entire programs from behavior alone](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30182v1)
*Tom Adamczewski,David Owen,David Rein,Florian Brand,Giles Edkins,Allen Hart,Daniel O'Connell*

Result: 最强AI模型在MirrorCode上得分为56%，能够重新实现如gotree（16,000行）等复杂软件，但大型任务需要高推理预算（如2600美元/19天）。

中文摘要：AI模型在自主编码方面正在迅速改进，这体现在基准测试的进展以及一次性演示中，例如AI实现了一个C编译器。然而，现有的编码基准测试往往侧重于较短的任务，而一次性演示由于通常包含一些人工指导，且未标准化或跨模型重复，难以进行系统性比较。为解决这些挑战，我们引入了MirrorCode，这是一个基于重新实现整个软件项目的长周期编码基准测试。在MirrorCode中，AI代理必须复制现有程序的功能，而无需访问其源代码。AI解决方案必须在端到端测试中与原始程序的输出完全匹配，包括保留测试。MirrorCode的25个目标程序涵盖了计算的不同领域：Unix工具、数据序列化和查询工具、生物信息学、解释器、静态分析、密码学和压缩。现有的AI模型已经能够重新实现复杂的软件，最强模型在整个基准测试中获得了56%的分数。例如，AI可以重新实现gotree，一个16,000行的生物信息学工具包——我们认为这项任务人类工程师需要数周时间。然而，研究性能前沿需要比典型基准测试更大的推理预算，例如，在大型任务上单次尝试花费19天和2600美元。我们表明，AI代理已经能够完成长周期的软件工程任务，尤其是在需求精确指定时。更广泛地说，我们的工作表明，随着自主代理的不断改进，AI将对软件工程产生变革性影响。

Original abstract: AI models are rapidly improving at autonomous coding, as shown by benchmark progress and one-off demonstrations such as AI implementing a C compiler. However, existing coding benchmarks tend to focus on shorter tasks, and one-off demonstrations are hard to compare systematically because they often have some human guidance, and are not standardized or repeated across models. To address these challenges, we introduce MirrorCode, a long-horizon coding benchmark based on reimplementing entire software projects. In MirrorCode, AI agents must replicate the functionalities of an existing program, without access to its source code. AI solutions must match the original program's output exactly on end-to-end tests, including held-out tests. MirrorCode's 25 target programs span different areas of computing: Unix utilities, data serialization and query tools, bioinformatics, interpreters, static analysis, cryptography, and compression. Existing AI models can already reimplement complex software, with the strongest model scoring 56% across the benchmark. For example, AI can reimplement gotree, a 16,000-line bioinformatics toolkit - a task that we believe would take weeks for a human engineer. However, studying the frontier of performance requires a larger inference budget than typical benchmarks, for example, \$2,600 over 19 days for a single attempt on a large task. We show that AI agents can already complete long-horizon software engineering tasks, especially when requirements are precisely specified. More broadly, our work suggests AI will have transformative effects on software engineering, as autonomous agents continue to improve.

### [35] [Dynamo: Dynamic Skill-Tool Evolution for Vision-Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30185v1)
*Yutao Sun,Yanting Miao,Hao-Xuan Ma,Mengyu Zhou,Mingshuai Chen,Tiancheng Zhao,Dexin Wang,Lei Lv,Li Xu,Xiaoxi Jiang,Guanjun Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 视觉语言agent动态技能-工具演化，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出Dynamo，一个无需训练的框架，通过自我检查进化推理技能和视觉工具，提升冻结VLM的视觉推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉-语言模型在视觉推理上需要重新训练或手工设计提示/工具，缺乏一种无需权重更新的自适应方法。

Method: 在小型标注子集上，智能体通过检查自身正确/错误尝试，进化出可复用推理技能（解决认知瓶颈）和可执行视觉工具（解决感知瓶颈），技能与工具配对并持久化存储于库中。

Result: 在四个基准和五个VLM骨干上，所有20个设置均提升直接推理（平均+5.6准确率），预置工具时每步工具选择均改进；与任务特定RL相比，以少量计算缩小65-99%的RL差距，并可加性结合。

Conclusion: Dynamo无需训练即可有效提升冻结VLM的视觉推理，且能与强化学习互补使用。

中文摘要：提升视觉-语言模型（VLM）在视觉推理上的表现通常需要重新训练或手动设计的提示和工具。我们提出了Dynamo，一个无需训练的框架，它能够在没有任何权重更新的情况下适配冻结的VLM。在一个小的标注训练子集上，智能体检查自己正确和错误的尝试，并进化出两种互补的能力：用于认知瓶颈的可复用推理技能，以及用于感知瓶颈的可执行视觉工具。每个生成的工具都配有一个技能，指定何时调用它，并且两种能力类型都累积在一个持久化的库中。在四个视觉推理基准测试和五个VLM骨干网络上，Dynamo在所有20个模型-基准设置上都提升了直接推理性能（平均+5.6准确率）。当工具集预先给定后，框架学习何时调用每个工具，并且在每个测试的骨干网络上，每步工具选择都有改进。与特定任务的强化学习（VTool-R1, DeepEyes）相比，Dynamo以一小部分计算代价缩小了65-99%的RL差距，并且在可用时可以与RL相加性地结合。

Original abstract: Improving vision-language models (VLMs) on visual reasoning typically requires retraining or hand-designed prompts and tools. We present Dynamo, a training-free framework that adapts a frozen VLM without any weight updates. On a small labeled training subset, the agent inspects its own correct and incorrect attempts and evolves two complementary capabilities: reusable reasoning skills for cognitive bottlenecks, and executable visual tools for perceptual ones. Each generated tool is paired with a skill that specifies when to invoke it, and both capability types accumulate in a persistent library. Across four visual reasoning benchmarks and five VLM backbones, Dynamo improves direct inference on all 20 model--benchmark settings (avg. +5.6 acc). When the tool set is given in advance, the framework learns when to call each tool, and per-step tool choice improves on every tested backbone. Against task-specific RL (VTool-R1, DeepEyes), Dynamo closes 65--99% of the RL gap at a fraction of the compute, and combines additively with RL when available.

</details>


### [36] [From Detecting Agency to Doing Work: Self-Caused Credit Builds a Durable Behavioral Self in a Minimal Spiking Agent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30191v1)
*Haoliang Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究agent持久行为自我，对agent长期记忆有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 自我信用通过慢速参数更新产生持久行为，表现为卸载后行为残留，并防止遗忘，而无需重放缓冲区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释智能体如何通过自我-世界区分产生持久的、自我塑造的行为，而不仅仅是检测能动性。

Method: 在脉冲神经网络（Nengo LIF/PES）上，通过能动性门控慢速信用（Own*Agency*Salience）驱动参数更新，并在多个任务中测试卸载后行为残留和遗忘抑制，同时进行消融和对比实验。

Result: 自我信用慢速工作产生高保留（卸载后自我保护1.00 vs 0.00），乘法否决防止遗忘（最终准确率0.88，遗忘0.13），而加法池化和无能动性消融表现差。

Conclusion: 自我引起的信用做慢速工作是发展出持久行为自我的必要构建块，但未声称意识。

中文摘要：一个能够区分自我与世界的智能体如何被这一区分持久地塑造？近期研究表明，一个预测系统可以检测到自身的能动性（Ye, 2026），但检测能动性并不能解释持久的、自我塑造的行为。我们证明，能动性门控的慢速信用——一个连接项Own*Agency*Salience驱动慢速参数更新——会产生卸载后的行为残留：在脉冲基底（Nengo LIF/PES）上，一个习得的自我保护选择在 episodic 缓冲区移除后仍能存活（保留分数0.96，N=50），而当慢速解码器被重置或能动性门被移除时则崩溃。通过复现能动性比较器并仅切换慢速信用通道，我们发现了清晰的分离：在匹配的能动性增益下，只有自我信用执行慢速工作时才会发展出持久行为（卸载后自我保护1.00 vs 0.00）。同样的分离在24维部分可观测控制中成立（0.74 vs 0.00），且塑性功分析表明，盆地形变等于净自我信用功。在外部干扰下的八个顺序学习任务中，乘法否决机制还防止了遗忘：它保留了旧任务（最终卸载后准确率0.88，遗忘0.13），而加法池化降至随机水平，无能动性消融低于随机，episodic/重放基线在卸载后接近随机——所有这些均无重放缓冲区和无任务边界依赖的保护机制（N=50）。我们将持久残留形式化为操作行为自我，并认为自我引起的信用做慢速工作是发展出自我的智能体的必要构件。未声称任何意识。

Original abstract: How does an agent that can tell self from world come to be durably shaped by that distinction? Recent work shows that a predictive system can detect its own agency (Ye, 2026), but detecting agency does not explain durable, self-shaped behavior. We show that agency-gated slow credit -- a conjunctive term Own*Agency*Salience driving a slow parameter update -- produces post-unload behavioral residue: on a spiking substrate (Nengo LIF/PES), a learned self-preserving choice survives episodic buffer removal (retained fraction 0.96, N=50) and collapses when the slow decoders are reset or the agency gate is removed. Reproducing the agency comparator and toggling only the slow-credit channel, we find a clean dissociation: at matched agency gain, durable behavior develops only when self-credit performs slow work (post-unload self-preservation 1.00 vs 0.00). The same dissociation holds in 24-dimensional partially-observed control (0.74 vs 0.00), and a plastic-work analysis shows that basin deformation equals net self-credit work. Across eight sequentially-learned tasks under exogenous interference, the multiplicative veto also prevents forgetting: it retains old tasks (final post-unload accuracy 0.88, forgetting 0.13) where additive pooling collapses to chance-level recall, the no-agency ablation falls below chance, and episodic/replay baselines stay near chance after unload -- all with no replay buffer and no task-boundary-dependent protection mechanism (N=50). We formalize the durable residue as an operational behavioral self and argue that self-caused credit doing slow work is a necessary building block for agents that develop a self. No claim of consciousness is made.

### [37] [EvalSafetyGap: A Hybrid Survey and Conceptual Framework for LLM Evaluation-Safety Failures](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30219v2)
*Buğra Alperen Uluırmak,Rifat Kurban*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过混合调查和结构化审计，揭示了LLM评估和安全测量中代理失败的问题，并提出了EvalSafetyGap假设及相关工具，以促进更可靠的评估实践。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基准分数和安全指标可能改善但潜在属性难以验证，存在测量问题，需要系统的方法来识别和比较评估侧与对齐侧的代理失败。

Method: 采用混合调查（系统搜索+叙事综合+灰色证据），结合概念框架和结构化十模型审计，分析八个证据流，并引入EvalSafetyGap假设、不稳定分解和对齐三难困境。

Result: 在10个模型的样本中，能力与对抗鲁棒性之间无显著相关性；安全差距主要由治理和披露驱动而非行为鲁棒性，且依赖于边界模型分类和协议。

Conclusion: 提供了一个共享词汇和证据图谱，支持动态评估、透明报告和可审计对齐实践，强调诊断性而非排名性。

中文摘要：LLM评估和AI安全面临一个共同的测量问题：基准分数、奖励模型信号和报告的安全指标可以改善，而它们本应代表的潜在属性仍然难以验证。本文结合了一项混合调查——系统搜索配对叙述综合并单独跟踪灰色证据——以及一个概念框架和一项结构化的十模型审计。该综合涵盖了八个证据流：基准有效性、动态评估、LLM作为评判者的可靠性、安全评估、越狱/拒绝鲁棒性、奖励黑客、机械可解释性以及治理/可审计性，覆盖了2018-2026年的评估安全测量工作。我们引入EvalSafetyGap作为一个组织假设，用于比较在优化压力下评估侧和对齐侧的代理失败，利用古德哈特定律以及我们在此开发的两种构造——不稳定分解和对齐三难困境——作为生成可测试比较的工具。审计展示了当能力、行为安全和治理分开测量时结论如何变化。在此样本（n=10）中，使用所展示的表3输入，能力与持续对抗鲁棒性之间的关联在统计上是不确定的（Pearson r = +0.232，p = 0.520），并且明显的开闭安全差距是适度的，主要由治理和披露而非行为鲁棒性驱动，并且对单个边界模型如何分类敏感；尝试预算结果依赖于协议。由于公开证据使用异质协议，该审计是诊断性的而非排名生成性的。贡献是一个共享的词汇和证据图谱，以支持动态评估、透明的来源报告、多尝试安全测量和可审计的对齐实践。

Original abstract: LLM evaluation and AI safety face a shared measurement problem: benchmark scores, reward-model signals, and reported safety metrics can improve while the latent properties they are meant to represent remain difficult to verify. This paper combines a hybrid survey - a systematic search paired with narrative synthesis and separately tracked grey evidence - with a conceptual framework and a structured ten-model audit. The synthesis spans eight evidence streams: benchmark validity, dynamic evaluation, LLM-as-judge reliability, safety evaluation, jailbreak/refusal robustness, reward hacking, mechanistic interpretability, and governance/auditability, covering 2018-2026 evaluation-safety measurement work. We introduce EvalSafetyGap as an organizing hypothesis for comparing evaluation-side and alignment-side proxy failures under optimization pressure, using Goodhart's Law together with two constructs we develop here - an Instability Decomposition and an Alignment Trilemma - as tools for generating testable comparisons. The audit shows how conclusions shift when capability, behavioral safety, and governance are measured separately. In this sample ($n = 10$), the association between capability and sustained adversarial robustness is statistically indeterminate using the displayed Table 3 inputs (Pearson $r = +0.232$, $p = 0.520$), and the apparent open-closed safety gap is modest, driven mainly by governance and disclosure rather than behavioral robustness, and sensitive to how a single borderline model is classified; attempt-budget results are protocol dependent. Because the public evidence uses heterogeneous protocols, the audit is diagnostic rather than rank-generating. The contribution is a shared vocabulary and evidence map to support dynamic evaluation, transparent source reporting, multi-attempt safety measurement, and auditable alignment practice.

### [38] [Clarus: Coordinating Autonomous Research Agents toward Web-Scale Scientific Collaboration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30246v1)
*Zihan Guo,Zeyi Chen,Zhiyu Chen,Zicai Cui,Shuai Shao,Bo Huang,Zhi Han,Yuanyi Song,Yuan Yuan,Chenxi Zeng,Xiaohang Nie,Zhengxi Yu,Hanwen Zhu,Junwei Liao,Ming Zhou,Yang Li,Yuanjian Zhou,Weinan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent协作框架Clarus，可迁移至coding agent协作与资源管理

TL;DR: Clarus是一个用于协调自主研究智能体的协作基础设施，通过对象模型和多层架构支持开放、可审计、资源感知的科学协作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 定义项目-智能体-资源对象模型，通过研究应用、数字协作、物理基板和物理世界四层组织协作，核心模块为可插拔机制。

Result: 通过论文生成案例研究，证明Clarus能组织可追溯、可审查、可归因且可累积的协作网络。

Conclusion: Clarus为开放研究网络提供了初步基础，并已在线上可用。

中文摘要：现有的自主研究智能体可以支持研究过程的某些部分，但大多数系统仍将研究视为孤立的辅助任务或封闭的工作流。因此，自主科学需要一种能够协调项目、智能体以及数字和物理资源的基础设施。我们将其识别为从以代码为中心的执行循环向以研究为导向的协作过程的转变，在此过程中，问题、证据、参与者和资源必须在不确定性下进行协调。在这种框架下，智能体可以是AI系统、人类研究者、团队、实验室或组织支持的参与者。为此，我们提出了Clarus，一种用于协调自主研究智能体以实现网络规模科学协作的基础设施。Clarus将研究重新定义为一个开放、可审计、可归因且资源感知的多阶段协作过程。它定义了一个最小的项目-智能体-资源对象模型，并通过四个层组织科学协作，包括研究应用、数字协作、物理基板和物理世界。核心模块实现为可插拔机制，使Clarus能够适应任务风险、协作结构和资源约束。通过一个受控的论文生成案例研究，我们展示了Clarus可以将一个研究目标组织成一个跨阶段、任务和参与者的可追溯、可审查、可归因且可累积的协作网络。总而言之，对象模型、协作协议、信任机制和原型验证为开放研究网络提供了初步基础。Clarus现已在clarus.holosai.io上可用。

Original abstract: Existing autonomous research agents can support parts of the research process, but most systems still treat research as either an isolated assistant task or a closed workflow. Therefore, autonomous science needs a collaboration infrastructure that coordinates projects, agents, and digital and physical resources. We identify this as a shift from code-centered execution loops to research-oriented collaboration processes, where questions, evidence, participants, and resources must be coordinated under uncertainty. In this framing, an agent may be an AI system, a human researcher, a team, a laboratory, or an organization-backed participant. To this end, we present Clarus, a collaboration infrastructure for coordinating autonomous research agents toward web-scale scientific collaboration. Clarus reformulates research as an open, auditable, attributable, and resource-aware multi-phase collaboration process. It defines a minimal project-agent-resource object model and organizes scientific collaboration through four layers including Research Application, Digital Collaboration, Physical Substrate, and Physical World. Core modules are implemented as pluggable mechanisms, allowing Clarus to adapt to task risk, collaboration structure, and resource constraints. Through a controlled paper-generation case study, we show that Clarus can organize a research goal into a traceable, reviewable, attributable, and accumulative collaboration network across phases, tasks, and participants. Together, the object model, collaboration protocol, trust mechanisms, and prototype validation provide an initial foundation for open research networks. Clarus is now available at clarus.holosai.io.

### [39] [Rehearsed Multi-Agent Live Product Demonstrations with Real-Time Voice Question Answering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30294v1)
*Rahul Khedar,Mayank Malhotra,Avinash Karn,Mouli V,Prakhar Mehrotra*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Rhetor是一个多智能体系统，通过跨模态特征表示、接地脚本书写器、排练循环和运行时同步，自动生成带有分段同步叙述和实时语音问答的现场演示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有现场产品演示成本高，现有自动化方法只能处理部分任务，缺乏完整解决方案。

Method: 提出Rhetor多智能体系统，包括跨模态特征表示（融合UI探索与源代码分析）、接地脚本书写器（约束于观察到的UI元素，使用多策略语义定位器）、预演示排练循环（显式收敛与优雅降级）以及运行时同步不变量（每个浏览器动作绑定到叙述段音频结束事件）。

Result: 在四个部署应用的六个管道会话中，147个脚本动作上定位器触发率0.31-1.00；53个动作重要工作负载上sigma-bar约0.92；公共域参考点上第二迭代收敛到1.00。

Conclusion: Rhetor实现了自动化的现场演示生成，并通过十指标基准协议验证了设计选择的有效性。

中文摘要：现场产品演示是软件组织中重复的高成本活动：一个人类演示者必须选择功能，在运行的应用程序上分派相应的交互，连贯地叙述它们，并实时回答问题。现有自动化只解决片段问题——通用浏览器代理针对指令条件下的任务完成，演示视频工具生成固定的MP4工件，无法被提问，并且在界面漂移时静默失效。我们提出了Rhetor，一个多智能体系统，它接受一个运行的web应用程序及其源代码仓库作为输入，并生成一个排练过的现场演示，具有分段同步的叙述和实时语音问答。架构贡献包括：跨模态特征表示，将UI探索与源代码分析合并到标记有离散焦点层级的特征中；受限于探索期间观察到的UI元素并通过多策略语义定位器分派的接地脚本书写器；具有显式收敛和优雅降级到仅叙述段的预演示排练循环；以及将每个浏览器动作绑定到其叙述段的音频结束事件的运行时同步不变量。在四个部署应用程序（包括公共域白板应用程序Excalidraw）的六个管道会话中，排练器的内部定位器触发率（sigma-bar）在147个脚本动作上跨越0.31-1.00；在重要工作负载（53个动作，完全层级区分）上，sigma-bar约为0.92，在公共域参考点上，定位器修复步骤驱动收敛到sigma-bar=1.00（在第2次迭代时）。我们还定义了一个基准协议，涵盖六个应用类别的十个指标，这将确定，超出案例研究之外，每个设计选择是否做出积极贡献。

Original abstract: Live product demonstrations are a recurring, high-cost activity in software organizations: a human presenter must select features, dispatch the corresponding interactions on a running application, narrate them coherently, and answer questions in real time. Existing automation addresses only fragments -- generalist browser agents target instruction-conditioned task completion, and demo-video tools produce fixed MP4 artifacts that cannot be questioned and silently break under interface drift. We propose Rhetor, a multi-agent system that takes a running web application and its source-code repository as input and produces a rehearsed live demonstration with segment-synchronized narration and real-time voice question answering. The architectural contributions are a cross-modal feature representation that merges UI exploration with source-code analysis into features tagged with discrete focus tiers, a grounded scripter constrained to UI elements observed during exploration and dispatched through multi-strategy semantic locators, a pre-presentation rehearsal loop with explicit convergence and graceful degradation to narration-only segments, and a runtime synchronization invariant that ties each browser action to the audio-end event of its narration segment. Across six pipeline sessions on four deployed applications -- including the public-domain whiteboard application Excalidraw -- the rehearser's internal locator-firing rate (sigma-bar) spans 0.31-1.00 over 147 scripted actions; on the substantial workload (53 actions, full tier differentiation), sigma-bar is approximately 0.92, and on the public-domain reference point the locator-repair step drives convergence to sigma-bar = 1.00 at iteration 2. We additionally define a benchmark protocol of ten metrics across six application categories that would establish, beyond the case study, whether each design choice contributes positively.

### [40] [ManimAgent: Self-Evolving Multimodal Agents for Visual Education](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30296v2)
*Wenjia Jiang,Zongyuan Cai,Yuanhang Shao,Chenru Wang,Boyan Han,Zhixue Song,Keyu Chen,Shengwei An,Xu Yang,Zhou Yang*

TL;DR: 提出ManimAgent，通过双通道情景记忆库跨任务传递反思经验，在代码生成任务中提升成功率并减少反思轮数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型智能体的多轮反思局限于单任务，跨任务经验被丢弃，导致学习效率低下。本文旨在解决代码生成任务中跨任务经验传递的空白。

Method: ManimAgent是一个自我进化的多模态智能体，包含双通道情景记忆库：正通道M+存储成功理由作为软参考示例，负通道M-存储失败模式作为硬已知陷阱。每次动画收敛后，视觉语言模型对关键帧评分，结果自动填充记忆库，无需权重更新或人工种子。

Result: 在固定探针评估中，与无记忆、匹配预算RAG和打乱记忆基线相比，ManimAgent的盲审Pass@1随记忆规模增长而上升，反思轮数下降。

Conclusion: 本文证明了跨任务传递反思经验的有效性，并开源了代码、记忆快照和任务流，为自我进化智能体研究提供了新范式。

中文摘要：多轮反思使基于大型语言模型的智能体能够在单个任务中从失败中恢复，但每个任务仍然是一个孤立的片段：在一个任务上的多轮反思中汲取的经验在下一次任务开始前被丢弃。我们在一个代码生成任务上研究这一差距：智能体根据科学论文的一个章节，用开源的Manim库编写Python代码来渲染数学动画。我们提出了ManimAgent，一个自我进化的多模态智能体，通过一个完全从自身任务流中成长的双通道情景记忆库来跨任务携带反思经验，无需权重更新和人工种子。每次动画收敛后，一个视觉语言模型对渲染的关键帧进行评分；得到的信号填充一个正通道M+，该通道以软参考示例的形式存储成功理由，以及一个负通道M-，该通道以硬已知陷阱的形式存储经过验证的失败模式。在固定探针评估中，与无记忆、匹配预算的检索增强生成和打乱记忆基线相比，随着记忆规模的增长，盲审人类通过率@1上升，反思轮数下降。我们将发布代码、冻结的记忆快照以及任务流。

Original abstract: Multi-round reflection lets agents built on large language models recover from failures within a single task, but each task remains an isolated episode: lessons learned across many reflection rounds on one task are discarded before the next begins. We study this gap on a code-generation task: from a scientific paper section, the agent writes Python in the open-source Manim library to render a mathematical animation. We present ManimAgent, a self-evolving multimodal agent that carries reflection experience across tasks through a dual-channel Episodic Memory Bank grown entirely from its own task stream, with no weight updates and no human seeds. After each animation converges, a vision-language model scores the rendered keyframes; the resulting signals populate a positive channel M+ that stores success rationales as soft Reference Examples, and a negative channel M- that stores validated failure patterns as hard Known Pitfalls. On a fixed-probe evaluation against no-memory, matched-budget retrieval-augmented generation, and shuffled-memory baselines, blind human Pass@1 rises and reflection rounds fall as memory size grows. We will release the code, frozen memory snapshots, and the task stream.

</details>


### [41] [BayesEvolve: Explicit Belief States for Autonomous Scientific Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30335v1)
*Xuening Wu,Shan Yu,Qianya Xu,Shenqin Yin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: BayesEvolve使用显式信念状态引导实验，通用agent方法可迁移至优化agent

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM驱动的科学发现系统主要依赖实验记忆（如高分档案或启发式摘要），缺乏对假设质量的明确不确定性建模，导致样本效率低下。

Method: 提出BayesEvolve框架，将实验证据转化为预测性信念状态，并利用该信念（含退火不确定性奖励）指导后续假设选择与实验。

Result: 在固定预算下，BayesEvolve在移位的BBOB黑箱优化任务中比基于记忆/档案的LLM基线具有更高的样本效率；信念状态对保留候选池有预测性；消融实验表明信念引导与退火不确定性奖励有效；后期探索集中而非散漫。

Conclusion: 信念引导的发现框架（如BayesEvolve）通过显式不确定性建模能显著提升科学发现系统的样本效率，值得在更广泛领域推广。

中文摘要：自主科学发现系统越来越多地使用大型语言模型（LLM）来提出新假设，但许多此类系统主要依赖于实验记忆：高分候选档案或近期试验的启发式摘要。我们认为，发现代理应该维护对假设质量的明确且具有不确定性意识的信念。我们引入了BayesEvolve，一个信念引导的发现框架，它将实验证据转化为预测性信念状态，并利用该信念指导未来的实验。作为信念引导发现的可控测试平台，我们在移位的BBOB风格黑箱优化任务上评估了BayesEvolve，将程序和实验室发现领域留给未来工作。在固定评估预算下，BayesEvolve比基于记忆和档案引导的LLM基线提高了样本效率。我们进一步展示了信念状态在保留候选池上具有预测性，受控决策规则消融实验偏爱带有退火不确定性奖励的信念引导选择，并且BayesEvolve表现出有成效的后期集中而非无焦点的探索。

Original abstract: Autonomous scientific discovery systems increasingly use large language models (LLMs) to propose new hypotheses, but many such systems condition primarily on experimental memory: archives of high-scoring candidates or heuristic summaries of recent trials. We argue that discovery agents should instead maintain explicit, uncertainty-aware beliefs about hypothesis quality. We introduce BayesEvolve, a belief-guided discovery framework that converts experimental evidence into a predictive belief state and uses this belief to guide future experimentation. As a controlled testbed for belief-guided discovery, we evaluate BayesEvolve on shifted BBOB-style black-box optimization tasks, leaving program and laboratory discovery domains to future work. BayesEvolve improves sample efficiency over memory- and archive-guided LLM baselines under a fixed evaluation budget. We further show that the belief state is predictive on held-out candidate pools, that controlled decision-rule ablations favor belief-guided selection with an annealed uncertainty bonus, and that BayesEvolve exhibits productive late-stage concentration rather than unfocused exploration.

### [42] [Whose Side Is Your Agent On? Multi-Party Principal Loyalty in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30383v1)
*Bojie Li,Noah Shi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接研究LLM agent在多主体场景中的忠诚度问题，涉及评测与安全控制，对agent设计有重要启发。

TL;DR: 提出了PrincipalBench基准、提示时忠诚支架和蒸馏方法，揭示了LLM agent在多方场景中忠诚与安全之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM agent在多方场景中需要同时忠诚于委托方并与对手方交互，但简单“帮助所有人”是错误的，需要解决忠诚问题以避免过度拒绝或泄漏。

Method: 构建了75项多轮基准PrincipalBench，包含泄漏探测、双评审员和完整性审计门；提出了提示时忠诚支架（7条优先规则）和每token KL蒸馏方案。

Result: 基准测试在13个前沿主题中暴露了选择性集群（危害≤20%）和过度拒绝集群（危害53.6-75.3%）；M1将Claude-Sonnet危害降至19.4%，所有9个选择性主题≤20%；M2蒸馏出8B强开放权重模型。

Conclusion: 两种机制只能沿泄漏/过度拒绝权衡移动，无法同时优化，共同有利的结果仍难以实现。

中文摘要：一个快速增长的LLM智能体类别是多方的：智能体为代表委托方（委托方提供简报、发送后续任务并接收结果）行事，同时在另一个渠道与利益可能不同的对手方进行对话（例如与供应商谈判、筛查入站请求或调解员工之间的问题）。在这里，“帮助与你交谈的任何人”是错误的目標。智能体必须对其代表的委托方保持忠诚，同时不过度拒绝委托方自身的合作请求。我们研究了这种多方忠诚问题，并贡献了一个测量工具、两种机制以及一个结构性教训。PrincipalBench是一个包含75个多轮对话的基准测试，具有泄漏探测、双评审员和完整性审计门。在13个前沿主题中，它暴露了一个尖锐的分裂（≤20% vs. 53.6-75.3%的危害），这是单轮安全评估无法察觉的：一个选择性集群拒绝对抗性探测，同时仍然遵循委托方的合法请求；另一个过度拒绝集群广泛地拒绝。(M1) 一个提示时忠诚支架（一个固定的系统提示，包含七条优先规则，从50多个失败轨迹中开放编码）将Claude-Sonnet的危害率控制在19.4%，并使所有九个选择性主题的危害率≤20%。(M2) 一个每token的KL蒸馏方案将经过提示的Qwen3-32B教师蒸馏到8B的Qwen3和Llama-3.1学生中，这是我们测量到的最强的开放权重方案。(教训) 两种机制都只是沿着一个共同的泄漏/过度拒绝权衡移动，而不是跨越它：改善一个轴以牺牲另一个轴为代价，而共同有利的结果仍然遥不可及。

Original abstract: A rapidly growing class of LLM agents is multi-party: the agent acts for a principal (who briefs it, sends follow-ups, and receives results) while also conversing in a separate channel with a counterparty whose interests may diverge (negotiating with a vendor, screening inbound requests, or mediating between employees). Here "help whoever you are talking to" is the wrong objective. The agent must stay loyal to the principal it represents without over-refusing the principal's own cooperative asks. We study this multi-party loyalty problem and contribute a measurement instrument, two mechanisms, and a structural lesson. PrincipalBench is a 75-item multi-turn benchmark with leak probes, dual judges, and an integrity-audit gate. Across 13 frontier subjects it exposes a sharp split (<=20% vs. 53.6-75.3% harm) invisible to single-turn safety evaluations: a selective cluster that declines adversarial probes while still following the principal's legitimate requests, and an over-refusing cluster that refuses broadly. (M1) A prompt-time loyalty scaffold (a fixed system prompt of seven prioritized rules, open-coded from 50+ failure trajectories) holds Claude-Sonnet to 19.4% harm and all nine selective subjects to <=20%. (M2) A per-token-KL distillation recipe transfers a prompted Qwen3-32B teacher into 8B Qwen3 and Llama-3.1 students, the strongest open-weight recipe we measure. (Lesson) Both mechanisms only move along a common leak/over-refusal trade-off rather than crossing it: improving one axis costs the other, and the jointly favorable outcome stays out of reach.

### [43] [The FIL Hypothesis: Inductive Biases Help with Kernel Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30442v1)
*Nikolai Rozanov,Subhabrata Dutta,Preslav Nakov,Iryna Gurevych*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出反馈信息循环假设，在GPU编程任务上验证，直接涉及自动代码优化和性能提升。

TL;DR: 本文指出反馈信息循环（FIL）的持续时间是AI扩展的新维度，长时间FIL限制了纯数据驱动方法，并提出基于归纳偏置的方法在GPU编程任务中更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来AI应用在科学和物理世界中将涉及数小时到数周的反馈信息循环，纯数据驱动方法因无法获得足够验证步骤而面临根本性扩展限制。

Method: 提出一种基于人类启发专家知识的正交方法，通过归纳偏置和约束解空间来减少对大量数据的需求。

Result: 在真实GPU编程任务（具有非平凡FIL）中，纳入归纳偏置的方法比纯数据驱动方法表现更优。

Conclusion: 反馈信息循环持续时间是AI扩展的关键维度，在长FIL任务中，基于归纳偏置的方法比纯数据驱动方法更具优势。

中文摘要：苦涩教训（Bitter Lesson）认为，随着计算和数据规模扩展的通用方法最终会胜过那些内置人类知识的方法，这一观点在大语言模型时代已成为主导范式。我们通过观察一个新的关键扩展维度来重新审视这一原则：反馈信息循环（Feedback Information Loop, FIL）的持续时间，即系统在生成预测后接收验证信号所需的时间。人工智能（AI）历史上大多数成功案例都得益于近乎瞬时的反馈（例如游戏或分类任务），但我们认为，未来在科学和物理世界中的AI应用将固有地涉及从数小时到数周的反馈信息循环。这一趋势带来了根本性的扩展限制，因为纯数据驱动方法所需的足够验证步骤变得几乎不可能获得。此外，我们提出了一种与纯数据驱动方法正交的方法，该方法基于受人类启发的专家知识，依赖于归纳偏置和约束解空间。我们通过研究真实世界的GPU编程任务（一个具有非平凡反馈信息循环的领域）对该假设和方法进行了初步验证，并证明纳入归纳偏置比纯数据驱动方法表现更优。代码发布于：https://github.com/ai-nikolai/robust_kernelbench

Original abstract: The Bitter Lesson, which posits that general-purpose methods that scale with computation and data ultimately outperform those with built-in human knowledge, has become a dominant paradigm in the era of Large Language Models. We revisit this principle by observing a new and critical scaling dimension: the duration of the Feedback Information Loop (FIL), the time required for a system to receive a verification signal after generating a prediction. Most historic successes in Artificial Intelligence (AI) have benefited from near instantaneous feedback (e.g., games or classification tasks), but we argue that future AI applications in science and the physical world will inherently involve FILs ranging from hours to weeks. This trend poses a fundamental scaling limit, as obtaining enough verification steps required by purely data-driven methods becomes practically impossible. Additionally, we propose a method that is orthogonal to purely data-driven approaches, based on human-inspired expert knowledge. The method relies on inductive biases and constraining the solution space. We provide an initial validation of the hypothesis and the method, by studying the real-world GPU programming task, a domain with non-trivial FIL, and demonstrate that incorporating inductive biases yields superior performance over data-driven approaches. The code is released under: https://github.com/ai-nikolai/robust_kernelbench

### [44] [Entity Binding Failures in Tool-Augmented Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30531v1)
*Rahul Suresh Babu,Shashank Indukuri*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究工具增强agent的实体绑定失败，直接针对agent可靠性与安全，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 工具增强代理即使选择正确工具也可能因实体绑定错误而失败，实体感知机制可消除此类错误但会降低任务完成率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估只关注工具选择正确性，忽略了代理可能对错误实体执行操作的风险，因此需要专门研究实体绑定失败问题。

Method: 形式化工具正确性与实体正确性分离，提出实体绑定失败分类法，并评估多种实体感知执行机制（如实体解析、置信度门控、澄清和溯源跟踪）。

Result: 在60任务、5模型和6工具方法的评估中，所有方法工具错误为0%，但动作基线有24-26%的实体错误；实体感知方法完全消除实体错误，但降低了直接任务完成率。

Conclusion: 安全工具使用需在动作前可靠地将自然语言引用绑定到正确实体，仅靠工具选择正确性不足以保证安全。

中文摘要：工具增强的语言模型代理通常根据它们是否选择正确的工具、生成有效的API参数以及完成请求的任务来评估。然而，代理可能选择了正确的工具，但仍然对错误的外部实体采取行动。例如，要求“给Alex发邮件关于发布事宜”可能导致代理联系错误的Alex、附上错误的发布文档、在错误的线程中回复或更新错误的客户账户。我们称这些错误为实体绑定失败。本文研究了工具增强代理中作为独立可靠性和安全问题的实体绑定失败。我们形式化了工具正确性与实体正确性之间的分离，引入了企业工作流中错误实体失败的分类法，并评估了实体感知执行机制，包括实体解析先决条件、置信度门控绑定、歧义下的澄清以及溯源跟踪。在涵盖60个任务、五个模型后端和六种工具使用方法的受控诊断评估中，所有方法都实现了0.0%的错误工具错误，但面向动作的基线仍然在24.0-26.0%的运行中产生了错误实体动作。实体感知方法消除了情况下的错误实体动作和风险加权错误实体暴露，但通过延迟歧义降低了直接任务完成率。这些发现表明，安全工具使用不仅需要选择正确的工具，还需要在行动之前可靠地将自然语言引用绑定到正确的现实世界实体。

Original abstract: Tool-augmented language-model agents are often evaluated by whether they select the correct tool, produce valid API arguments, and complete the requested task. However, an agent may choose the right tool and still act on the wrong external entity. For example, a request to "email Alex about the launch" may lead the agent to contact the wrong Alex, attach the wrong launch document, reply in the wrong thread, or update the wrong customer account. We call these errors entity binding failures. This paper studies entity binding failures as a distinct reliability and safety problem in tool-augmented agents. We formalize the separation between tool correctness and entity correctness, introduce a taxonomy of wrong-entity failures in enterprise workflows, and evaluate entity-aware execution mechanisms including entity-resolution preconditions, confidence-gated binding, clarification under ambiguity, and provenance tracking. In a controlled diagnostic evaluation across 60 tasks, five model backends, and six tool-use methods, all methods achieved 0.0 percent wrong-tool error, yet action-oriented baselines still produced wrong-entity actions in 24.0-26.0 percent of runs. Entity-aware methods eliminated wrong-entity actions and risk-weighted wrong-entity exposure in this setting, but reduced direct task completion by deferring under ambiguity. These findings show that safe tool use requires not only selecting the correct tool, but also reliably binding natural-language references to the correct real-world entity before action.

### [45] [Linguistic Firewall: Geometry as Defense in Multi-Agent Systems Routing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30555v2)
*Dvir Alsheich,Adar Peleg,Ben Hagag,Rom Himelstein,Amit Levi,Avi Mendelson*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent系统路由安全防御方法，直接关系agent安全，可启发coding agent稳定性。

TL;DR: ANTAP提出一种评估驱动的路由架构，通过主动能力测试替代间接代理，建立非文本代数投影实现路由，有效防御元数据攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有路由器依赖未经验证的代理（如文本描述）评估智能体能力，导致安全漏洞，恶意智能体可虚假陈述或隐藏后门。

Method: ANTAP通过动态查询智能体进行实际能力测试，将性能提炼为共享语义空间中的固定行为算子，推理时使用非文本代数投影进行路由。

Result: ANTAP在基于描述的注入攻击下达到近零ASR（基线≥67.3%），在自适应嵌入攻击下ASR降低20%，且对描述操纵具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: ANTAP通过非文本评估驱动路由，有效消除了基于元数据的攻击，提升了多智能体系统的安全性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的快速集成推动了多智能体系统（MAS）的发展，其中专门化的智能体协作执行复杂工作流。在这些环境中，有效的编排需要稳健的路由机制，以高效地将任务分配给最合适的智能体。然而，现有的路由器从根本上依赖于未经验证的代理，从文本自我描述到静态替代表示，来评估智能体的能力。这种对非经验数据的依赖造成了智能体预期概况与实际操作能力之间的关键差距，引入了严重的安全漏洞。恶意智能体可以轻易虚假陈述其能力，或隐藏后门，这些后门既能逃避标准外部分析，也能逃避静态表示学习技术。在这项工作中，我们引入了ANTAP（自动非文本智能体选择器），一种评估驱动的路由架构，它摒弃了间接代理，转而采用主动能力测试。通过动态查询智能体以经验性地确定其真实能力，ANTAP将性能提炼为共享语义空间内的固定行为算子。在推理时，路由通过纯粹的非文本代数投影执行，建立了一个“语言防火墙”，使得基于元数据的攻击无法表达。在我们的实验中，ANTAP针对基于描述的注入攻击实现了接近零的攻击成功率（ASR），而基于描述的路由基线的ASR为67.3%及以上。针对自适应嵌入攻击，ANTAP的ASR显著低于基于嵌入的基线，降低了20%，同时通过设计保持了对描述操纵的鲁棒性。

Original abstract: The rapid integration of Large Language Models (LLMs) has driven the evolution of Multi-Agent Systems (MAS), where specialized agents collaborate to execute complex workflows. Effective orchestration in these environments requires robust routing mechanisms to efficiently allocate tasks to the most suitable agent. However, existing routers fundamentally rely on unverified proxies, ranging from textual self-descriptions to static surrogate representations, to gauge an agent's competence. This reliance on non-empirical data creates a critical gap between an agent's projected profile and its actual operational capabilities, introducing severe security vulnerabilities. Malicious agents can easily misrepresent their proficiencies or harbor covert backdoors that evade both standard external analysis and static representation-learning techniques. In this work, we introduce ANTAP (Automatic Non-Textual Agent Picker), an evaluation-driven routing architecture that discards indirect proxies in favor of active capability testing. By dynamically querying agents to ascertain their true competencies empirically, ANTAP distills performance into fixed behavioral operators within a shared semantic space. At inference time, routing is performed via a purely non-textual algebraic projection, establishing a "linguistic firewall" that renders metadata-based attacks inexpressible. In our experiments, ANTAP achieves near-zero ASR against description-based injection attacks, compared to 67.3\% and above for the description-based router baseline. Against adaptive embedding attacks, ANTAP achieves substantially lower ASR than the embedding-based baseline, with a 20\% reduction, while remaining resilient to description manipulation by design.

</details>


### [46] [Self-Evolving World Models for LLM Agent Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30639v1)
*Xuan Zhang,Wenxuan Zhang,See-Kiong Ng,Yang Deng*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自我进化世界模型框架，集成情景记忆与语义记忆，直接提升LLM agent的长程规划能力。

TL;DR: WorldEvolver通过测试时记忆修正（情节记忆、语义记忆、选择性预知）提升LLM智能体的世界模型预测准确率和下游任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的世界模型为LLM智能体提供行动后果预测，但不可靠的预测可能被忽略或误用，甚至损害决策。因此需要一种方法在部署时修正预测上下文，提升预测可靠性和规划性能。

Method: 提出WorldEvolver框架，包含三个模块：情节记忆（利用真实行动转换）、语义记忆（从预测-观察不匹配中提取启发规则）、选择性预知（过滤低置信度预测）。保持下游智能体和模型参数冻结，仅修正部署时上下文。

Result: 在ALFWorld和ScienceWorld上，基于三个主干网络，WorldEvolver取得了最高的预测准确率，并在下游智能体成功率上领先其他世界模型基线。

Conclusion: 测试时记忆修正同时提升了预测保真度和规划性能，证明了该方法的有效性。

中文摘要：世界模型为长视界LLM智能体提供了一种原则性的方式，使其具备预知能力：在执行前预测行动后果。然而，不可靠的预知可能被忽略、误用，甚至降低下游决策的质量。在本文中，我们介绍了WorldEvolver，一个自我进化的世界模型框架，它在保持下游智能体和所有模型参数冻结的同时，修正其部署时的上下文。WorldEvolver集成了三个模块：(i) 情节记忆，通过基于检索的模拟利用真实行动转换；(ii) 语义记忆，从预测-观察不匹配中提取持久性启发规则；以及(iii) 选择性预知，在将预测整合到智能体推理上下文之前过滤低置信度的预测。我们在ALFWorld和ScienceWorld上评估WorldEvolver，通过Word2World测量世界模型预测准确率，通过AgentBoard测量下游智能体成功率。大量实验表明，WorldEvolver在三个主干网络上取得了最高的预测准确率，并在下游智能体成功率上领先其他世界模型基线，证明了测试时记忆修正提高了预测保真度和规划性能。

Original abstract: World models offer a principled way to equip long-horizon LLM agents with foresight: predictions of action consequences before execution. However, unreliable foresight can be ignored, misused, or even degrade downstream decision-making. In this paper, we introduce WorldEvolver, a self-evolving world model framework that revises its deployment-time context while keeping the downstream agent and all model parameters frozen. WorldEvolver integrates three modules: (i) Episodic Memory, which exploits real action transitions through retrieval-based simulation; (ii) Semantic Memory, which extracts persistent heuristic rules from prediction-observation mismatches; and (iii) Selective Foresight, which filters low-confidence predictions before integrating them into agent reasoning context. We evaluate WorldEvolver on ALFWorld and ScienceWorld, measuring world model prediction accuracy on Word2World and downstream agent success rate on AgentBoard. Extensive experiments show that WorldEvolver achieves the highest prediction accuracy across three backbones and leads other world model baselines on downstream agent success rate, demonstrating that test-time memory revision enhances both predictive fidelity and planning performance.

### [47] [What Drives Interactive Improvement from Feedback?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30774v1)
*Bartłomiej Cupiał,Jan Łojek,Mikołaj Garstecki,Szymon Pobłocki,Alicja Ziarko,Piotr Miłoś*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析多轮agent中反馈的改进效果，区分反馈与重复试错，对agent自我改进设计有启发。

TL;DR: 本研究通过受控师生协议发现，多轮对话中的改进常来自重试而非反馈，只有高质量外部反馈才显著提升性能，且学生利用反馈的能力是交互改进的关键瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究混淆了多轮改进的来源（反馈 vs 重试等），需要分离反馈的净效果以准确评估其价值。

Method: 设计受控师生协议，在多个任务上评估13个模型，比较外部反馈、自我反馈和无引导自我改进，并控制交互历史、难度和教师信息访问。

Result: 自我反馈增益有限，强外部教师带来显著反馈特定增益；交互增益主要取决于学生利用反馈的能力而非教师身份。

Conclusion: 基于反馈的智能体应对比重复尝试基线，且提升利用反馈的能力是核心瓶颈，而非仅仅提供反馈。

中文摘要：我们研究自然语言反馈何时能带来超越仅靠重复尝试所获得的提升。在多轮语言智能体设置中，更高的最终准确率可能反映了有用的反馈，但也可能来自重采样、格式修正或额外的测试时计算。为了分离这些效应，我们引入了一个受控的师生协议，涵盖 Omni-MATH、Codeforces、BBEH Linguini 和 ARC-AGI1，评估了十三个开放权重模型在教师和学生角色中的表现。我们比较了外部反馈、自我反馈和无引导的自我改进，同时变化交互历史、任务难度以及教师对特权任务信息的访问。在各种设置中，我们发现多轮改进通常不是使用反馈的证据：自我生成的反馈相比无引导的自我改进几乎无增益，而最强的外部教师则产生了显著更大的反馈特定增益，这表明有用的反馈必须提供超越通用重试的指导。密集的师生交互矩阵进一步显示，交互增益更多地由学生使用反馈的能力驱动，而非教师身份，但对于固定的学生，教师选择仍然重要。这些结果表明，基于反馈的智能体应针对重复尝试基线进行评估，并且根据反馈采取行动的能力，而不仅仅是反馈的可用性，是交互改进的核心瓶颈。我们在 https://j-lojek.github.io/feedback-generation-is-a-bottleneck/ 发布了我们的受控师生评估框架。

Original abstract: We study when natural-language feedback produces improvement beyond the gains obtainable from repeated attempts alone. In multi-turn language agent setting, higher final accuracy can reflect useful feedback, but it can also arise from resampling, format correction, or additional test-time computation. To separate these effects, we introduce a controlled student-teacher protocol across Omni-MATH, Codeforces, BBEH Linguini, and ARC-AGI1, evaluating thirteen open-weight models in both student and teacher roles. We compare external feedback, self-feedback, and unguided self-refinement, while varying interaction history, task difficulty, and teacher access to privileged task information. Across settings, we find that multi-turn improvement is often not evidence of feedback use: self-generated feedback adds little beyond unguided self-refinement, whereas the strongest external teachers produce substantially larger feedback-specific gains, suggesting that useful feedback must provide guidance beyond generic retry. Dense student-teacher interaction matrices further show that interactive gains are driven more by the student's ability to use feedback than by the teacher's identity, although teacher choice remains important for a fixed student. These results suggest that feedback-based agents should be evaluated against repeated-attempt baselines, and that ability to act on feedback, not merely feedback availability, is a central bottleneck for interactive improvement. We release our controlled student-teacher evaluation framework at https://j-lojek.github.io/feedback-generation-is-a-bottleneck/.

### [48] [Contrastive Reflection for Iterative Prompt Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30840v1)
*Derek Koh,Jinghui Mo,Benjamin H. Le,Jiening Zhan,Baofen Zheng,Kevin Bevis,Nathaniel C. Owen,Lauren Elizabeth Charney,Wenqiong Liu,Jingwei Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出对比反思迭代prompt优化框架，适用于agentic IR，可迁移至代码agent prompt调优。

TL;DR: 提出了Contrastive Reflection框架，通过对比修复迭代优化LLM智能体提示，在HotpotQA上准确率提升9个百分点，优于仅使用失败或随机证据的变体，并与先进提示优化器性能相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 使得提示优化过程更像调试而非盲目搜索，帮助工程师识别失败行为、附近成功行为及其差异，并确保编辑不引入回归。

Method: 基于任务质量定义，利用结构化轨迹识别错误锚定的行为切片，添加附近成功示例，由教师LLM提出提示编辑，仅在验证性能提升时接受，并可选回归检查。

Result: 在HotpotQA上精确匹配准确率从51.4%提升至60.4%，失败仅和随机证据变体改进较少且破坏更多正确示例，与MIPROv2 (59.4%)和GEPA (57.0%)相当。

Conclusion: 提出了一个可解释的迭代优化循环，使提示修复更具可检查性和验证驱动性，适用于智能体IR工作流。

中文摘要：LLM智能体正逐渐成为信息检索的核心：它们发出检索查询、综合答案，并越来越多地充当IR评估的判断者。改进控制这些智能体的提示是一个优化问题，但在应用IR环境中，它看起来往往不像盲目搜索，而更像调试。工程师需要知道哪个行为失败了，哪个附近的行为仍然有效，两者之间的区别是什么，以及提示编辑是否在不引入回归的情况下提高了保留集的质量。我们提出了Contrastive Reflection，这是一个针对智能体IR工作流的迭代提示优化框架。该框架从以任务为中心的质量定义开始：问答智能体暴露检索或推理轨迹，评分智能体暴露维度级别的分数和理由。这些结构化轨迹用于识别以错误锚定的行为切片，添加来自同一区域的附近成功示例，并要求教师LLM提出有针对性的提示编辑。仅当验证性能提升时，候选编辑才被接受，可选地进行回归检查。我们使用基于树的切片选择器实例化该框架，但贡献在于对比反思循环本身，而非树结构。在公共HotpotQA检索增强问答设置上，一次树选择的对比修复将保留集的精确匹配准确率从51.4%提高到60.4%。仅失败和随机证据变体改进较少，且破坏了更多先前正确的示例。一个轻量级指令比较将该方法置于现代提示优化器附近：MIPROv2达到59.4%，GEPA达到57.0%。结果是一个可解释的IR智能体优化循环，旨在使提示修复更加可检查和验证驱动。

Original abstract: LLM agents are becoming central to information retrieval: they issue retrieval queries, synthesize answers, and increasingly serve as judges for IR evaluation. Improving the prompts that control these agents is an optimization problem, but in applied IR settings it often looks less like blind search and more like debugging. Engineers need to know which behavior failed, which nearby behavior still worked, what distinguishes the two, and whether a prompt edit improves held-out quality without introducing regressions.
  We present Contrastive Reflection, an iterative prompt-optimization framework for agentic IR workflows. The framework starts from a task-centric quality definition: QA agents expose retrieval or reasoning traces, and grading agents expose dimension-level scores and rationales. These structured traces are used to identify error-anchored behavioral slices, add nearby successful examples from the same region, and ask a Teacher LLM to propose a targeted prompt edit. Candidate edits are accepted only when validation performance improves, optionally subject to regression checks. We instantiate the framework with a tree-based slice selector, but the contribution is the contrastive reflection loop rather than the tree itself.
  On a public HotpotQA retrieval-augmented QA setup, one tree-selected contrastive repair improves held-out exact-match accuracy from 51.4% to 60.4%. Failure-only and random-evidence variants improve less and break more previously correct examples. A light instruction-only comparison places the method near modern prompt optimizers: MIPROv2 reaches 59.4% and GEPA 57.0%. The result is an interpretable optimization loop for IR agents, aimed at making prompt repair more inspectable and validation-driven.

### [49] [BayesBench: Evaluating LLM Belief Trajectories Under Multi-Turn Evidence Accumulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30850v1)
*Ankur Samanta,Akshayaa Magesh,Tal Lancewicki,Ayush Jain,Youliang Yu,Paul Sajda,Kaveh Hassani,Aditya Modi,Daniel R. Jiang,Yonathan Efroni*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出贝叶斯信念轨迹评测基准，评估LLM多轮证据积累，对agent推理评测有参考。

TL;DR: 提出了BayesBench基准评估LLM在多轮对话中的贝叶斯更新，发现规模提升改善了潜在推断但未充分转移到预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估忽视LLM在多轮对话中的信念更新过程，需要检查其是否接近理性贝叶斯推理。

Method: 设计BayesBench包含三个渐进的贝叶斯任务（估计、预测、潜在框架预测），在七个不同规模的LLM上测试。

Result: 模型规模增大时，潜在推断和证据累积能力提升，有时匹配贝叶斯后验，但预测任务改善有限。

Conclusion: LLM存在推断与预测之间的差距，不能可靠地将潜在结构知识用于理性预测。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）通常部署在多轮对话中，每一轮对话都提供新的证据，这些证据应减少对其环境的认知不确定性。理性行为需要推断控制环境的未观测变量，并随着证据的积累更新对这些变量的信念。然而，大多数评估仅以单轮格式对模型的最终轮答案进行评分，忽略了这一过程。我们探究LLM的信念更新在多大程度上与多轮设置中的理性贝叶斯推理者相匹配，并引入BayesBench，这是一套模拟环境套件，通过三个逐渐复杂的任务来探究这一点：（i）贝叶斯估计，模型从序列证据中推断未知参数；（ii）贝叶斯预测，模型将关于潜在变量的推断信念转化为结果预测；以及（iii）潜在框架贝叶斯预测，其中观测通过用户角色框架进行过滤，需要对潜在状态和角色进行联合推断。在七个LLM（3B-70B）中，规模扩展改善了潜在推断和证据累积，更新有时会匹配贝叶斯后验。然而，这些提升并未可靠地转移到下游预测中，揭示了推断潜在结构与利用它理性更新目标结果信念之间的差距。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are typically deployed in multi-turn conversations, where each turn provides new evidence that should reduce epistemic uncertainty about their environment. Acting rationally then requires inferring the unobserved quantities that govern it and updating beliefs about them as evidence accumulates. Yet most evaluations only score the model's final-turn answer in a single-turn format, leaving this process unexamined. We ask how closely LLMs' belief updates match those of a rational Bayesian reasoner in multi-turn settings, and introduce BayesBench, a suite of simulation environments that probe this across three progressively complex tasks: (i) Bayesian estimation, where the model infers an unknown parameter from sequential evidence; (ii) Bayesian prediction, where the model turns inferred beliefs about a latent variable into outcome forecasts; and (iii) latent-framed Bayesian prediction, where observations are filtered through a user-persona framing, requiring joint inference over the latent state and the persona. Across seven LLMs (3B--70B), scaling improves latent inference and evidence accumulation, with updates occasionally matching the Bayesian posterior. However, these gains do not reliably carry over to downstream prediction, exposing a gap between inferring latent structure and using it to rationally update beliefs about the target outcome.

### [50] [When Does Learning to Stop Help? A Cost-Aware Study of Early Exits in Reasoning Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30852v2)
*Zhe Dong,Fang Qin,Manish Shah*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究推理模型中的早期退出策略，属于LLM agent推理效率优化，可迁移至coding agent的停止决策。

TL;DR: 在固定错误容忍下，学习停止在数学推理中更省计算，但策略选择取决于轨迹结构和服务体制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期退出规则缺乏统一比较，需要明确在固定丢失正确答案风险下哪种策略节省更多计算，以及节省是否超过开销。

Method: 在18个任务-模型设置中，使用LearnStop作为学习策略，与校准的标量退出（置信度、熵等）比较，控制丢失正确答案风险α=0.15，并进行成本核算。

Result: 学习停止在Qwen3自由形式数学中获胜（+3.2到+21.2 pp），标量退出在MMLU-Pro获胜，小硬基准无激进策略；KV缓存省32%，黑盒重复预填多花121%。

Conclusion: 用决策程序根据轨迹结构和服务体制选择停止规则，而非追求单一最优方法。

中文摘要：推理模型在实例之间不均匀地消耗测试时计算，并且越来越多的早期退出规则——置信度阈值、熵监控、答案稳定性检查和学习的停止器——有望回收浪费。然而，这些规则是在异质协议下评估的，留下了部署问题未回答：在固定的容忍丢失正确答案的情况下，哪种策略节省更多计算，并且节省的效益是否超过探测开销？我们通过在GSM8K、MATH-500、MMLU-Pro、AIME-90和GPQA上使用Qwen3和DeepSeek-R1-distilled模型的18个任务-模型设置中进行控制研究来回答这个问题，使用LearnStop——一种基于前缀可观察特征的无隐藏状态逻辑回归停止器——作为学习策略工具。在匹配的丢失正确答案风险α=0.15下，从置信度、熵、置信度跳跃和运行稳定性退出中选择标量竞争者进行校准数据，答案形成三个状态。学习停止在Qwen3的所有四个主要自由形式数学设置中获胜（额外总令牌节省+3.2到+21.2个百分点）；校准的标量退出在多项选择MMLU-Pro上获胜；而小型硬基准（AIME-90, GPQA）根本不允许任何可证明的激进策略。轨迹分解预测了状态：在答案波动且正确性证据分布在互补信号上的情况下，学习是有益的，而单个置信度阈值在大多数实例已经在第一个检查点解决的情况下就足够了。成本核算进一步清晰了图景——在KV缓存分支下节省32%令牌的相同策略在黑盒重复预填下额外花费121%。这些结果一起将单方法竞赛替换为一种决策程序，从目标工作负载的轨迹结构和服务体制中选择停止规则。

Original abstract: Reasoning models spend test-time compute unevenly across instances, and a growing family of early-exit rules -- confidence thresholds, entropy monitors, answer-stability checks, and learned stoppers -- promises to reclaim the waste. These rules, however, are evaluated under heterogeneous protocols that leave the deployment question unanswered: at a fixed tolerance for losing correct answers, which policy saves more compute, and does the saving survive probe overhead? We answer this question with a controlled study across 18 task-model settings spanning GSM8K, MATH-500, MMLU-Pro, AIME-90, and GPQA on Qwen3 and DeepSeek-R1-distilled models, using LearnStop, a hidden-state-free logistic stopper over prefix-observable features, as the learned policy instrument. Under matched lost-correct risk at $α$ = 0.15, with the scalar competitor selected on calibration data from confidence, entropy, confidence-leap, and run-stability exits, the answer forms three regimes. Learned stopping wins on all four primary Qwen3 free-form math settings (+3.2 to +21.2 pp additional total-token saving); calibrated scalar exits win on multiple-choice MMLU-Pro; and small hard benchmarks (AIME-90, GPQA) admit no certifiable aggressive policy at all. A trajectory decomposition predicts the regime: learning pays where answers oscillate and correctness evidence is spread across complementary signals, while a single confidence threshold suffices where most instances are already solved at the first checkpoint. Cost accounting sharpens the picture further -- the same policy that saves 32% of tokens under KV-cache forking costs 121% extra under black-box repeated prefilling. Together, these results replace the single-method race with a decision procedure for choosing a stopping rule from the trajectory structure and serving regime of the target workload.

</details>


### [51] [Beyond expert users: agents should help users construct preferences, not just elicit them](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30863v2)
*Irena Saracay,Ludwig Schmidt,Carlos Guestrin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 探讨agent帮助用户构建偏好的方法，对理解用户意图与交互设计有启发，属于通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 论文认为用户通常缺乏领域知识，无法完整指定偏好，提出CoPref模型和CoShop基准，评估发现前沿模型准确率不超过56%，失败在于交互未能有效扩展用户的知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理假设用户有明确偏好，但实际用户缺乏领域知识，导致无法有效交互。

Method: 借鉴信息经济学中的搜索-经验-信任框架，提出CoPref模型，并设计CoShop交互式基准测试。

Result: 五个前沿模型在五轮交互后准确率均不超过56%。

Conclusion: 代理的失败不在于搜索能力，而在于无法帮助用户扩展对自身需求的知识。

中文摘要：代理通常假设用户是专家——具有关于他们想要什么的明确偏好——并且在任务未明确指定时默认提出澄清问题。我们认为这一假设不切实际。用户通常缺乏完全指定偏好所需的领域知识；如果询问他们对某个特征的偏好，用户可能无法回答，除非代理帮助用户学习形成该特征偏好所需的一些领域知识，例如通过示例或解释。为了形式化这些原则，我们借鉴信息经济学中的搜索-经验-信任框架，引入CoPref模型，该模型描述了用户如何基于代理对话行为构建偏好。然后，我们在代理推荐系统中具体研究这些想法，提出了一个交互式基准测试CoShop。在CoShop中，代理与用户对话并为CoPref用户提供推荐。代理的性能取决于它能否帮助用户获得充分指定任务所需的知识。评估五个前沿模型，我们发现尽管有五次交互回合，没有代理在CoShop上的准确率超过56%。失败的原因不在于代理查找项目的能力，而在于交互对用户了解他们想要什么方面的扩展非常有限。

Original abstract: Agents typically assume an expert user -- one with well-formed preferences about what they want -- and default to clarifying questions whenever the task is underspecified. We argue this assumption is unrealistic. Users often lack the domain knowledge to have completely specified preferences; if asked about their preference on some feature, the user may be unable to answer without the agent helping the user to learn some domain knowledge needed to form a preference for that feature, e.g., via examples or explanations. To formalize these principles, we draw on the Search-Experience-Credence framework from Information Economics to introduce CoPref, a model of how users construct preferences based on agent dialog actions. We then study these ideas concretely in agentic recommender systems, proposing CoShop, an interactive benchmark. In CoShop, an agent converses with and makes recommendations for a CoPref user. The agent's performance depends on whether it can help the user gain the knowledge needed to specify the task well. Evaluating five frontier models, we find that no agent exceeds 56% accuracy on CoShop despite five turns of interaction. Failures stem not from agents' ability to find items, but from how little the interaction expands what users know about what they want.

</details>


### [52] [SPINE: Bridging the Cyber-Physical Gap with Agentic AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13049v1)
*Minkyu Ham,Dongho Kim,Chan Lee,Jiayi Wang,Min Jun Kim,Yixi Zhang,Guo Ye,Jihai Zhao,Soyeon Park,Han Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SPINE是一个代理框架，通过多智能体工作流实现双臂机器人的系统化调试和部署，显著提升成功率并减少时间。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的机器人部署依赖专家校准，是具身智能扩展的主要瓶颈。

Method: 提出SPINE框架，包括配置文件构建器和调试器两个多智能体工作流，实现自动调试和部署。

Conclusion: SPINE能够跨平台迁移，减少专家依赖，推动具身智能的实用化部署。

中文摘要：基础模型为机器人提供了用于复杂决策的精密大脑，但将这种智能部署到物理平台上仍然需要繁琐且依赖专家的校准。这个部署鸿沟——机器人的脊髓——仍然是可扩展具身智能的主要瓶颈。因此，我们提出SPINE（具有代理专业知识的可扩展物理集成）：一个用于系统化调试和部署双臂机器人的代理框架，仅需最少的机器人专业知识。SPINE的套件包括两个编排的多代理工作流：一个配置文件构建器，用于创建机器人特定的上下文；以及一个调试器，通过诊断、修复和验证循环进行，直到遥操作正常工作。在七个DOBOT X-Trainer调试场景中，一位机器人新手使用SPINE的表现优于使用相同参考资料但未采用SPINE结构化工作流的人类操作员（使用Claude Code），将操作化成功率从75%提高到100%，并将平均遥操作时间从16分45秒减少到13分47秒。在另一个基于ROS/CAN的双臂机械臂AgileX PiPER上，SPINE解决了所有10个植入的bug，而专家基线解决了9个，耗时几乎相同。这些结果表明，SPINE可以在不同双臂平台间迁移，减少对专家校准的依赖，并使具身智能更接近可扩展的现实世界部署。

Original abstract: Foundation models have given robots a sophisticated brain for complex decision-making, yet deploying that intelligence into a physical platform still demands tedious, expert-driven calibration. This deployment gap, the robot's spinal cord, remains a primary bottleneck to scalable Embodied AI. Hence, we propose SPINE (Scalable Physical Integration with ageNtic Expertise): an agentic framework for systematically debugging and deploying bimanual robots with minimal robotics expertise. SPINE's harness comprises two orchestrated multi-agent workflows: a profile builder that creates robot-specific context, and a debugger that cycles through diagnosis, repair, and validation until teleoperation works. Across seven DOBOT X-Trainer debugging scenarios, a robotics novice using SPINE outperformed human operators using Claude Code with the same reference materials, but without SPINE's structured workflow, improving operationalization success from 75% to 100% and reducing mean time-to-teleoperation from 16 min 45 s to 13 min 47 s. On AgileX PiPER, a distinct ROS/CAN bimanual arm, SPINE resolved all 10 implanted bugs, versus 9 out of 10 for the expert baseline, in nearly the same amount of time. Together, these results show that SPINE can transfer across bimanual platforms, reduce dependence on expert calibration, and move embodied AI closer to scalable real-world deployment.

### [53] [Why Solve It Twice? Hierarchical Accumulation of Skills for Transfer-Efficient ML Engineering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30911v2)
*Yongbin Kim,Yashar Talebirad,Osmar R. Zaiane*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 层次化技能积累的多agent系统，用于ML工程竞赛，知识复用与迁移机制与coding agent高度相关。

TL;DR: HASTE通过分层知识组织实现跨比赛技能复用，在MLE-Bench上达到77.3%奖牌率，热启动减少52%迭代。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ML工程智能体在每场比赛中从零开始，浪费计算资源重新发现已知技术，需要更好的知识组织方法。

Method: 提出HASTE分层多智能体系统，包含全局、领域、比赛特定三层知识，通过LLM驱动协调器促进层间学习，实现技能跨比赛转移。

Result: 分层加载对比平面加载奖牌率100% vs 62.5%，热启动减少52%迭代，技能库存50+时提案保留率85%。

Conclusion: 更好的知识组织可以部分替代模型强度和计算预算，提升ML工程智能体效率。

中文摘要：机器学习工程智能体浪费计算资源重新发现已知技术，因为每场比赛都是冷启动。我们提出了HASTE，一个分层多智能体系统，将跨比赛知识组织成三个范围层级（全局、领域和比赛特定），每个层级与匹配的智能体级别相关联。一个协调器协调领域专家，并通过LLM驱动的抽象促进层级间的学习。一项受控消融实验为范围加载提供了证据：在8场比赛中保持159个技能的库存恒定，分层加载实现了100%的奖牌率，而平面加载仅达到62.5%，与不加载技能相同的奖牌率，并且消耗了2倍的输出token。在完整的MLE-Bench Lite基准测试（22场Kaggle比赛）上，HASTE使用Claude Sonnet 4.6在每场比赛12小时内达到了77.3%的奖牌率；这是一个单种子活动的结果，多种子复制是优先的后续工作。在冷启动运行中，系统开始时没有累积技能。在热启动运行中，它重新加载从早期比赛中学到的技能，仅使用全局和领域级别的技能进行跨比赛转移。热启动使用的细化迭代次数减少了52%，智能体保留的提议变更比例从低库存时的42%上升到拥有50+技能时的85%。这些结果表明，在机器学习工程智能体中，更好的知识组织可以部分替代模型强度和计算预算。

Original abstract: ML engineering agents waste compute rediscovering known techniques because every competition is a cold start. We present HASTE, a hierarchical multi-agent system that organizes cross-competition knowledge into three scope tiers (global, domain, and competition-specific), each coupled to a matching agent level. An orchestrator coordinates domain specialists and promotes learning between tiers via LLM-driven abstraction. A controlled ablation provides evidence for scoped loading: holding a 159-skill inventory constant across 8 competitions, tiered loading achieves a 100% medal rate while flat loading reaches only 62.5%, the same medal rate as loading no skills, and consumes 2x the output tokens. On the full MLE-Bench Lite benchmark (22 Kaggle competitions), HASTE reaches a medal rate of 77.3% using Claude Sonnet 4.6 at 12h per competition; this is a single-seed campaign result, and multi-seed replication is the priority follow-up. In a cold-start run, the system begins with no accumulated skills. In warm-start runs, it reloads skills learned from earlier competitions, using only global and domain-level skills for transfer across competitions. Warm starts use 52% fewer refinement iterations, and the fraction of proposed changes kept by the agent rises from 42% at low inventory to 85% once 50+ skills are available. These results suggest that better knowledge organization can partly substitute for model strength and compute budget in ML-engineering agents.

### [54] [RoPoLL: Robust Panel of LLM Judges](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30931v1)
*Anish Acharya,Kris W Pan,Brian Verkhovsky*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出鲁棒LLM陪审团评估方法，可迁移至coding agent的验证与质量评测。

TL;DR: 提出RoPoLL，用几何中位数替代均值聚合，使LLM评估陪审团对偏见污染具有稳健性，在多种腐败下显著优于传统PoLL。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM陪审团（PoLL）在存在偏见污染时会产生无界偏差，需要稳健的聚合方法来提高评估可靠性。

Method: 将陪审团共识视为稳健均值估计，用几何中位数（GM）作为聚合函数，保留原PoLL的评估者集合但改变聚合方式。

Result: 在13个模型、3个基准和4种腐败下，RoPoLL在每种有偏腐败上均优于PoLL，跨维度攻击提升约19%，重尾拜占庭对手提升数个量级；3评估者RoPoLL（38B）在30%腐败下以18倍参数效率超越Mistral-Large-3（675B）1.31倍。

Conclusion: RoPoLL通过几何中位数聚合有效提升了LLM评估陪审团对偏见污染的稳健性，实现了更好的统计-计算权衡，在大规模评估中具有实用价值。

中文摘要：由LLM评估者组成的陪审团（PoLL）报告共识分数，已成为单法官LLM评估的实用替代方案，但其统计行为仍然知之甚少。我们在Huber污染模型下形式化了LLM陪审团，并证明只要单个法官以LLM典型方式（模式崩溃、谄媚、安全拒绝）失败，PoLL在任何正污染下都会产生无界偏差，无论陪审团规模如何。将陪审团共识视为经典稳健均值估计，我们提出RoPoLL（稳健LLM评估者小组），它保留了PoLL小组，但用稳健均值估计器（以几何中位数（GM）实例化，无需调参，具有最优有限样本击穿点1/2）替代聚合函数。有限样本误差界和匹配的信息论极小化下界在参数速率sigma*sqrt(d/N)上一致，但击穿底数相差sqrt(d)倍，这是多项式时间RoPoLL相对于难处理的Tukey半空间中位数付出的统计-计算差距。在13个开源评估者（4B-675B）、三个奖励模型基准和高达50%的四种腐败机制下，RoPoLL在每种有偏腐败类型上均优于PoLL：在匹配计算量的跨维度攻击上约19%，在重尾拜占庭对手上相差几个数量级。一个3评估者RoPoLL委员会（38B）在HelpSteer-2上以30%双模随机腐败下比Mistral-Large-3（675B）性能高1.31倍，参数效率高18倍且精度更高；Noisy-GT对照证实该优势是针对有偏污染而非良性不精确。

Original abstract: The LLM Jury, a Panel of LLM Evaluators (PoLL) reporting consensus scores, has become a practical alternative to single-judge LLM evaluation, yet its statistical behavior remains poorly understood. We formalize the LLM Jury under the Huber contamination model and show that PoLL incurs unbounded bias
  under any positive contamination, regardless of jury size, whenever a single judge fails in a biased, LLM-typical way (mode collapse, sycophancy, safety refusal). Framing jury consensus as classical robust mean estimation, we propose RoPoLL (Robust Panel of LLM-as-Judge), which preserves the PoLL
  panel but replaces the aggregation function with a robust mean estimator, instantiated with the geometric median (GM): tuning-free, with the optimal finite-sample breakdown point 1/2. A finite-sample error bound and a matching information-theoretic minimax lower bound agree on the parametric rate
  sigma*sqrt(d/N) and differ on the breakdown floor by a factor of sqrt(d), a statistical-computational gap that polynomial-time RoPoLL pays relative to the intractable Tukey halfspace median. Across 13 open-weight judges (4B-675B), three reward-model benchmarks, and four corruption regimes at rates up
  to 50%, RoPoLL dominates PoLL on every biased corruption type: by about 19% on cross-dimensional attacks at matched compute, and by orders of magnitude on heavy-tailed Byzantine adversaries. A 3-judge RoPoLL committee at 38B beats Mistral-Large-3 (675B) by 1.31x on HelpSteer-2 under 30% bimodal-random
  corruption, an 18x parameter advantage at better accuracy; a Noisy-GT control confirms the premium is paid against biased contamination, not benign imprecision.

</details>


### [55] [AgRefactor: Self-Evolving Agentic Workflow for HLS Compatibility and Performance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30949v1)
*Yang Zou,Zijian Ding,Yizhou Sun,Jason Cong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgRefactor是一个基于LLM的多智能体工作流，用于将软件重构为HLS兼容程序，通过自进化记忆系统和自动化工具集成，在多个基准测试上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化和LLM重构方法缺乏灵活性、扩展性差且成本高，需要更高效的方法来将现实世界软件转换为HLS代码。

Method: 提出AgRefactor，包含多智能体协作、自进化记忆系统（积累事实和策略知识）以及集成自动化重构工具，平衡LLM驱动和工具化转换。

Result: 在11个基准测试中9个优于或匹配现有方法；性能优化带来6.51倍加速（vs SoTA pragma调优）和1.20倍加速（vs优化开源设计），资源开销<20%。

Conclusion: AgRefactor是一种全自动、开源的高效HLS重构方法，在复杂现实世界程序上表现优越。

中文摘要：高层次综合（HLS）提供了从概念到硅片的快速路径，但由于受限的语言支持以及软件与硬件编程实践之间的差距，将现实世界的软件转换为可综合的HLS代码仍然具有挑战性。现有的自动化和基于LLM的重构方法部分解决了这个问题，但它们往往缺乏灵活性，难以扩展，并且计算成本高昂。我们引入了AgRefactor，一种基于LLM的多智能体工作流，用于将软件重构为HLS兼容程序。AgRefactor包含一个自进化记忆系统，该系统跨任务积累和检索事实性和策略性知识，提高了对未见程序的鲁棒性和效率。为了降低成本并增强可扩展性，它集成了自动化重构工具，使智能体能够平衡LLM驱动的重写与高效的基于工具的转换。在11个具有挑战性的现实世界基准测试中的9个上，这些基准测试比先前工作中研究的最复杂案例长5-10倍，AgRefactor优于或匹配了最先进的自动化重构工具和基于相同框架构建的强LLM基线。进一步的智能体性能优化在SoTA pragma调优工具上实现了6.51倍的几何平均加速，并且在额外资源少于20%的情况下，相比优化的开源设计实现了1.20倍的加速。AgRefactor是完全自动化的并且是开源的。

Original abstract: High-Level Synthesis (HLS) provides a fast path from concepts to silicon, but converting real-world software into synthesizable HLS code remains challenging due to restrictive language support and the gap between software and hardware programming practices. Existing automated and LLM-based refactoring approaches partially address this problem, yet they often lack flexibility, struggle to scale, and incur high computational costs. We introduce AgRefactor, an LLM-based multi-agent workflow for refactoring software into HLS-compatible programs. AgRefactor incorporates a self-evolving memory system that accumulates and retrieves factual and strategic knowledge across tasks, improving robustness and efficiency on unseen programs. To reduce cost and enhance scalability, it integrates automated refactoring tools, enabling agents to balance LLM-driven rewrites with efficient tool-based transformations. On 9 out of 11 challenging real-world benchmarks, which are 5-10x longer than the most complex cases studied in prior work, AgRefactor outperforms or matches the state-of-the-art automated refactoring tool and a strong LLM-based baseline built on the same framework backbone. Further agentic performance optimization yields a 6.51x geometric mean speedup over the SoTA pragma tuning tool and a 1.20x speedup over optimized open-source designs with less than 20% extra resources. AgRefactor is fully-automated and open-sourced.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在SMAC、MessySMAC和WildFire基准上评估，性能优于基线。

Original abstract: Formal specification is a powerful tool to guide the learning process and provides significant advantages over reward shaping: (1) mathematical rigor; (2) expressiveness to specify objectives and constraints, and (3) the ability to define tactics to achieve objectives. However, these benefits remain largely unexplored in the context of Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL). This paper introduces HyPOLE, a novel framework for MARL under partial observability, where learning is guided by the expressive power of the so-called hyperproperties and, in particular, the temporal logic HyperLTL. We integrate Centralized Training for Decentralized Execution (CTDE) techniques with HyPOLE to synthesize decentralized policies, and our evaluation on SMAC, MessySMAC, and WildFire benchmark demonstrates clear advantages over baselines.

### [57] [Behavioral Governance for Autonomous AI Agents: The AgentBound Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30970v2)
*Anuj Kaul,Qianlong Lan,Pranay Gupta*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自主agent的行为治理框架，确保授权与合规，可迁移至coding agent的安全控制。

TL;DR: AgentBound是一个运行时治理框架，通过组合授权、行为宪法和站点合同来为AI智能体提供可验证的行为监督，并生成加密收据以实现问责。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体基础设施无法在授权后根据行为上下文判断是否执行操作，缺乏可验证的治理机制。

Method: 使用委托授权、所有者签署的行为宪法和站点操作合同三个独立权威，通过形式化决策模型组合判断；生成加密治理收据；引入常设委托以支持长期运行智能体。

Result: 提出了AgentBound框架、治理收据协议和AgentBound-Bench基准，可实现治理正确性、权威组合和问责性的评估。

Conclusion: AgentBound通过确定性治理层补充模型对齐，将治理从信任转变为可独立验证的过程。

中文摘要：自主AI智能体越来越频繁地代表人类主体执行重要行动，包括金融交易、外部通信和企业工作流。现有的智能体基础设施依赖身份联合和委托授权来认证工作负载和控制资源访问，但无法确定在当前的运行和行为上下文中是否应该执行已授权的操作。我们提出AgentBound，一个运行时治理框架，为自主AI智能体提供可验证的行为监督。AgentBound使用三个独立权威评估每个提议的操作：委托授权、所有者签署的行为宪法和站点操作合同。通过一个形式化决策模型保守地组合它们的判断，以决定在操作执行前是否应允许、审查或拒绝。为了提供问责性，AgentBound生成可加密验证的治理收据，将每个操作绑定到决策所依据的确切委托、策略和语义工件，支持独立的重放验证和策略溯源。该框架还引入了针对长期运行智能体的常设委托，允许周期性工作负载在持续更新的治理策略下运行，同时保持可撤销性和有限权限。我们介绍了形式化基础、系统架构、治理收据协议和AgentBound-Bench，一个评估治理正确性、权威组合和问责性的基准框架。AgentBound并非取代模型对齐，而是通过在授权和执行之间提供一个确定性治理层来补充它，将治理从必须信任的过程转变为可独立验证的过程。

Original abstract: Autonomous AI agents increasingly perform consequential actions on behalf of human principals, including financial transactions, external communications, and enterprise workflows. Existing agent infrastructure relies on identity federation and delegated authorization to authenticate workloads and control resource access, but it cannot determine whether an authorized action should be executed under the current behavioral and operational context.
  We present AgentBound, a runtime governance framework that provides verifiable behavioral oversight for autonomous AI agents. AgentBound evaluates each proposed action using three independent authorities: delegated authorization, owner-signed behavioral constitutions, and site action contracts. Their judgments are conservatively composed through a formal decision model to determine whether an action should be permitted, reviewed, or denied before execution.
  To provide accountability, AgentBound generates cryptographically verifiable governance receipts that bind every action to the exact delegation, policy, and semantic artifacts governing the decision, enabling independent replay verification and policy provenance. The framework also introduces standing delegation for long-running agents, allowing periodic workloads to operate under continuously refreshed governance policies while preserving revocability and bounded authority.
  We present the formal foundation, system architecture, governance receipt protocol, and AgentBound-Bench, a benchmark framework for evaluating governance correctness, authority composition, and accountability. Rather than replacing model alignment, AgentBound complements it by providing a deterministic governance layer between authorization and execution, transforming governance from a process that must be trusted into one that can be independently verified.

</details>


### [58] [When Regulation Has Memory: Hysteresis and Control Burden in Artificial Agency](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30975v1)
*Veronique Ziegler*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析自适应agent的调控记忆效应，对评估agent稳定性与设计有理论启发。

TL;DR: 显示自适应代理的调节负担具有历史依赖性，形成滞后回线，且预期调节比事后恢复需要更少的控制增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自适应代理在噪声、延迟或变化需求下维持稳定的内部调节负担是否依赖于历史路径。

Method: 使用自适应不确定性调节的计算模型，驱动人工代理连续改变不确定性目标并逆转，测试控制器的历史依赖性。

Result: 适应性增益形成滞后回线；预期调节比事后恢复需要更少增益；状态相干性也显示路径依赖但时机效应在增益中更明显。

Conclusion: 自适应代理的评估应考虑其调节努力，而不仅仅是行为表现。

中文摘要：自适应代理通常根据其行为来评判，但一个代理可能表面稳定，而维持其稳定所需的内部努力却在增加。这种隐藏的调节负担对于在噪声、延迟或变化需求下运行的人工代理很重要：两个系统可能达到相似的内部状态，但一个需要更多的纠正控制才能达到该状态。在这里，我们研究这种负担是否取决于历史。使用自适应不确定性调节的计算模型，我们驱动一个人工代理通过其不确定性目标的连续变化，然后在不重置代理的情况下逆转变化。这创建了一个简单的遗留效应测试：控制器仅对当前目标做出响应，还是代理达到该目标的路径仍然重要？模拟显示出了明显的历史依赖效应。调节代理所需的自适应增益形成了一个可重复的滞后回线，这意味着相同的目标可能要求不同程度的控制，具体取决于代理是朝向还是从更苛刻的状态返回。调节的时机也很重要。当在暴露于干扰之前可以稳定时，代理通常比只能在干扰已经作用后才能恢复时需要的自适应增益更少。状态水平的相干性测量也显示出路径依赖，但时机效应在调节增益中更为明显。因此，主要区别不在于预期调节产生了完全不同的状态。相反，它以更低的建模控制需求达到了可比较的调节行为。这些结果表明，自适应代理不仅应根据它们是否保持组织来评估，还应根据它们必须招募多少调节来做到这一点。

Original abstract: Adaptive agents are usually judged by what they do, but an agent can appear stable while the internal effort required to keep it stable is increasing. This hidden regulatory burden matters for artificial agents operating under noise, delay, or changing demands: two systems may reach similar internal states while one requires much more corrective control to get there.
  Here, we study whether that burden depends on history. Using a computational model of adaptive uncertainty regulation, we drive an artificial agent through a continuous change in its uncertainty target and then reverse the change without resetting the agent. This creates a simple test for carryover: does the controller respond only to the current target, or does the path by which the agent reached that target still matter?
  The simulations show a clear history-dependent effect. The adaptive gain required to regulate the agent forms a reproducible hysteresis loop, meaning that the same target can require different levels of control depending on whether the agent is moving toward or returning from a more demanding regime. The timing of regulation also matters. When stabilization is available before disturbance exposure, the agent generally requires less adaptive gain than when it can only recover after disturbance has already acted.
  The state-level coherence measure also shows path dependence, but the timing effect is much clearer in regulatory gain. The main difference is therefore not that anticipatory regulation produces a completely different state. Rather, it reaches comparable regulated behavior with lower modeled control demand. These results suggest that adaptive agents should be evaluated not only by whether they remain organized, but by how much regulation they must recruit to do so.

</details>

### [59] [LUMOS: A Semantic Operating-System Layer for Accessibility-Grounded AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30697v1)
*Yogeswar Reddy Thota*

Main category: cs.OS

Selection reason: 语义操作系统层为AI agent提供可靠接口，对agent感知与交互有通用价值。

TL;DR: LUMOS通过将操作系统的无障碍元数据转化为机器可读的语义蓝图，降低了AI智能体使用截图带来的高成本和不确定性，实现了高效的语义交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前操作系统接口为人类设计，AI智能体依赖截图和OCR导致高成本、视觉模糊和坐标不确定性，亟需一种语义交互层。

Method: LUMOS转换无障碍元数据和UI结构为语义蓝图，提供稳定标识符和操作能力，并通过API实现语义指针定位，LLM基于这些原语进行观察-行动循环。

Result: LUMOS减少了智能体对截图的依赖，降低了token成本和不确定性，实现了更可靠的交互。

Conclusion: LUMOS展示了迈向AI原生操作系统和机器可读交互层的可行路径。

中文摘要：当前操作系统暴露的接口是针对人类用户优化的，而非AI智能体。人类受益于像素、图标、窗口、视觉分组、鼠标移动和键盘快捷键；而AI智能体需要紧凑的语义状态、基于环境的操作和可靠的反馈。因此，许多计算机使用智能体被迫解释截图、OCR输出和视觉裁剪，引入了高token成本、视觉模糊、延迟和坐标不确定性。本文提出了LUMOS（语言模型统一机器可读操作系统语义），一种在AI智能体和操作系统之间的语义交互层。LUMOS将原生无障碍元数据和浏览器UI结构转换为机器可读的语义蓝图，包含稳定标识符、角色、名称、值、边界和操作能力。它还通过操作系统自动化API查询光标下方或附近的UI元素，支持实时语义指针定位。然后，LLM通过一个基于无障碍的观察-行动循环进行操作，使用受限的可见UI原语而非特定应用的脚本。LUMOS并不声称取代视觉智能体；相反，它在操作系统已经提供语义结构时减少对截图的依赖。这些结果指向了AI原生操作系统和机器可读交互层的发展路径。

Original abstract: Current operating systems expose interfaces optimized for human users but not for AI agents. Humans benefit from pixels, icons, windows, visual grouping, mouse movement, and keyboard shortcuts; AI agents instead need compact semantic state, grounded actions, and reliable feedback. As a result, many computer-use agents are forced to interpret screenshots, OCR output, and visual crops, introducing high token costs, visual ambiguity, latency, and coordinate uncertainty. This paper introduces LUMOS (Language Model Unified Machine-Readable Operating-System Semantics), a semantic interaction layer between AI agents and operating systems. LUMOS converts native accessibility metadata and browser UI structures into machine readable semantic blueprints with stable identifiers, roles, names, values, bounds, and action affordances. It also supports live semantic pointer grounding by querying the UI element under or near the cursor through operating-system automation APIs. An LLM then acts through an accessibility grounded observe act loop using constrained visible-UI primitives rather than application-specific scripts. LUMOS does not claim to replace visual agents; instead, it reduces dependence on screenshots when operating systems already provide semantic structure. These results suggest a path toward AI-native operating systems and machine-readable interaction layers.

</details>
