### [60] [SEVA: Self-Evolving Verification Agent with Process Reward for Fact Attribution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29713v1)
*Aojie Yuan,Yi Nian,Haiyue Zhang,Zijian Su,Yue Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 自演化验证agent，过程奖励与自改进循环，可直接应用于代码优化agent的验证反馈。

TL;DR: SEVA是一种结构化验证代理，通过过程奖励解决多组件输出中标准RL的梯度消失问题，并实现自我进化，在事实归因验证上取得与GPT-4o-mini相当的性能且输出更丰富。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前事实归因验证器仅输出二元标签，无法支持代理自我纠正和审计，限制了LLM代理的可靠性。

Method: 提出SEVA，使用过程奖励将验证质量分解为五个独立组件（70/30权重），通过RL训练，并引入验证-反思-探查-精炼的自我进化循环。

Result: SEVA-3B在ClearFacts上F1达到69.0，匹配GPT-4o-mini；在7B模型上经过四轮自我进化后，HaluEval提升15pp但TruthfulQA下降10-14pp，揭示基准专家现象。

Conclusion: 对于多组件生成的RL任务，奖励粒度必须与输出粒度匹配，该原则应推广。

中文摘要：幻觉是基于LLM的代理的可靠性瓶颈，而事实归因验证器是最后一道防线——然而今天的验证器只发出不透明的二元标签，使代理无法自我纠正，操作员也无法审计。我们提出SEVA，一种结构化验证代理，它发出证据对齐、逐步推理链、校准置信度和六类别错误诊断及可操作修复。使用RL训练这样的代理并非易事：标准二元奖励在多组件输出上触发优势崩溃——组内奖励方差消失，GRPO梯度消失。我们通过一种过程奖励解决了这个问题，该奖励将验证质量分解为五个独立组件，权重70/30偏向过程信号，恢复梯度并引入隐式课程——代理首先掌握验证行为（对齐0.917->0.997，格式72%->100%），然后掌握结果（F1 64.9->69.0）。结构化输出进一步实现了一个验证->反思->探查->精炼的自我进化循环，在7B模型上经过四轮后，揭示了一个意外的结构发现：每一轮产生一个基准专家，而不是通才（同一模型在HaluEval上+15个百分点，在TruthfulQA上-10到-14个百分点，在4倍数据下持续存在）。在ClearFacts上，SEVA-3B匹配GPT-4o-mini（F1 69.0 vs. 69.8），同时产生更丰富、可审计的输出——确认了一个应该推广的原则：对于任何具有多组件生成的RL任务，奖励粒度必须与输出粒度匹配。

Original abstract: Hallucination is the reliability bottleneck for LLM-based agents, and fact attribution verifiers are the last line of defense -- yet today's verifiers emit only opaque binary labels, leaving agents unable to self-correct and operators unable to audit. We present SEVA, a structured verification agent that emits evidence alignments, step-by-step reasoning chains, calibrated confidence, and a six-category error diagnosis with actionable fixes. Training such an agent with RL is non-trivial: standard binary reward on multi-component output triggers advantage collapse -- within-group reward variance vanishes and the GRPO gradient disappears. We resolve this with a process reward that decomposes verification quality into five independent components weighted 70/30 toward process signals, restoring the gradient and inducing an implicit curriculum -- the agent first masters verification behavior (alignment 0.917 -> 0.997, format 72% -> 100%), then outcomes (F1 64.9 -> 69.0). Structured output further enables a Verify -> Reflect -> Probe -> Refine self-evolution loop, which over four rounds on a 7B model surfaces an unexpected structural finding: each round produces a benchmark-specialist, not a generalist (+15 pp on HaluEval, -10 to -14 pp on TruthfulQA in the same model, persistent at 4x data). On ClearFacts, SEVA-3B matches GPT-4o-mini (69.0 vs. 69.8 F1) while producing substantially richer, auditable output -- confirming a principle that should generalize: for any RL task with multi-component generation, reward granularity must match output granularity.

</details>


### [61] [Neural Procedural Memory: Empowering LLM Agents with Implicit Activation Steering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29824v1)
*Chengfeng Zhao,Yuqiao Tan,Shizhu He,Yequan Wang,Jun Zhao,Kang Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出隐式激活引导的agent记忆框架，无需训练，可迁移至coding agent的记忆与执行。

TL;DR: 提出神经程序记忆（NPM）框架，通过隐式激活引导代替显式文本指令来赋予LLM智能体程序记忆，实验表明性能与显式指令基线相当，且结合显式工作流效果更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖RAG注入显式文本指令，导致文本-动作脱节，无法激活正确任务执行所需的内部表征。

Method: 提出NPM，从历史对比经验中提炼程序技能为激活空间中的引导向量，通过直接激活神经机制隐式指导任务执行。

Result: 在四个智能体基准上，NPM性能与使用显式文本指令的基线相当；结合隐式引导与显式工作流可互补优势，提升任务稳健性；表征分析显示引导向量编码一致任务逻辑。

Conclusion: 隐式激活引导为管理智能体记忆提供了一种有前景的方法。

中文摘要：虽然大语言模型（LLMs）擅长作为静态求解器，但将它们转化为自主智能体仍然具有挑战性。这种转变需要持续的环境交互，然而当前的智能体缺乏必要的持久程序记忆。现有方法主要采用检索增强生成（RAG）将显式的文本指南注入模型上下文。然而，仅依赖符号指令可能会引入文本-动作脱节，常常无法激活正确任务执行所需的内部表征。为了解决这一问题，本文引入了神经程序记忆（NPM），一种无需训练的框架，通过隐式激活引导而非显式指令来表示智能体记忆。通过将历史对比经验中的程序技能提炼为激活空间中的引导向量，NPM直接激活与任务相关的神经机制来指导任务执行。在四个智能体基准上的评估表明，NPM的表现与使用显式文本指令的基线相当。此外，结果表明，将隐式引导与显式工作流相结合提供了互补优势，导致更稳健的任务执行。表征分析表明，这些引导向量编码了一致的任务逻辑，在激活空间中形成了有组织的结构。这些发现表明，隐式激活引导为管理智能体记忆提供了一种有前景的方法。

Original abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) excel as static solvers, transforming them into autonomous agents remains challenging. This transition requires continuous environmental interaction, yet current agents lack the necessary persistent procedural memory. Existing approaches predominantly employ Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) to inject explicit textual guidelines into model contexts. However, relying solely on symbolic instructions can introduce a text-action disconnect, frequently failing to activate the internal representations necessary for correct task execution. To address this, the paper introduces Neural Procedural Memory (NPM), a training-free framework that represents agent memory through implicit activation steering rather than explicit instructions. By distilling procedural skills from historical contrastive experiences into steering vectors in the activation space, NPM directly activates the task-relevant neural mechanisms to guide task execution. Evaluations across four agent benchmarks show that NPM performs comparably to baselines using explicit textual instructions. Furthermore, the results show that combining implicit steering with explicit workflows provides complementary advantages, leading to more robust task execution. Representational analyses indicate that these steering vectors encode consistent task logic, forming organized structures within the activation space. These findings suggest that implicit activation steering provides a promising approach for managing agent memory.

</details>


### [62] [Field Order Should Not Matter: Permutation-Invariant Embedding Model Fine-Tuning for Structured Metadata Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30473v1)
*Aivin V. Solatorio,Olivier Dupriez,Rafael Macalaba*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出排列不变性微调用于结构化元数据检索，涉及LLM生成查询，可启发agent检索组件设计。

TL;DR: 提出排列不变微调（PI-FT）解决结构化元数据检索中字段顺序敏感性问题，基于DevDataBench基准微调小模型在15种语言上超越大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准微调在结构化元数据检索中对字段顺序敏感，顺序变化导致检索质量显著下降（7.4 nDCG@10），因此需要一种排列不变的方法。

Method: 提出PI-FT，在微调时对每个记录随机采样字段顺序并随机丢弃字段，迫使模型关注标签而非位置。

Result: PI-FT将顺序变化惩罚降至0.2 nDCG@10，微调118M参数模型在DevDataBench上nDCG@10达到0.707，优于text-embedding-3-large的0.556，在低资源语言上增益最大。

Conclusion: PI-FT简单有效，能消除字段顺序影响，使小模型在多语言结构化数据检索中优于大模型，促进数据通过AI传播。

中文摘要：我们研究了结构化元数据目录的检索问题，其中每个记录是一个小模式，其字段回答不同类型的查询。使用文本编码器嵌入记录时，首先需要将字段序列化为字符串，这会强制选择字段顺序。我们表明，这种通常被视为实现细节的选择，在编码器微调后悄然控制着检索质量。标准微调在索引以不同字段顺序重建时会损失7.4个nDCG@10点，因为它读取的是绝对位置而非字段标签。我们提出了排列不变微调（PI-FT），它在随机字段dropout下以新采样的字段顺序序列化每个记录，从而使含义绑定到标签而非位置。这一改动在数据加载器中大约只有两行代码；它在分布内准确度上的损失可以忽略不计，并将顺序变化惩罚降低到0.2点。我们在开发统计数据的发现中研究了这一问题，这是一个包含近万个指标的目录，应该能够通过一个足够小以至于可以自托管的模型以多种语言进行搜索。随着AI助手和代理越来越多地中介对公共数据和统计数据的访问，这一检索步骤决定了答案是否基于正确的指标或序列，使得可发现性成为通过AI传播数据的先决条件。由于使用日志无法为没有人搜索过的指标提供训练信号，我们生成了查询。DevDataBench是一个完全由LLM生成的基准测试，涵盖15种语言的基于事实、面向方面的查询，覆盖了每个指标，用于训练和评估。一个微调的118M参数CPU编码器在所有零样本基线上取得了更好的性能，包括text-embedding-3-large（nDCG@10为0.707对比0.556），在低资源语言上改进最大。我们发布了基准测试、流程、模型以及可复用的PI-FT框架。

Original abstract: We study retrieval over catalogs of structured metadata, where each record is a small schema whose fields answer different kinds of query. Embedding a record with a text encoder first serializes its fields into a string, which forces a choice of field order. We show this choice, usually treated as an implementation detail, silently controls retrieval quality once the encoder is fine-tuned. A standard fine-tune loses 7.4 nDCG@10 points when the index is rebuilt under a different field order, because it reads absolute position instead of the field labels. We propose permutation-invariant fine-tuning ($\textbf{PI-FT}$), which serializes each record under a freshly sampled field order with random field dropout, so meaning binds to the labels rather than to position. The change is about two lines in the data loader; it costs negligible in-distribution accuracy and cuts the order-change penalty to 0.2 points. We study this in the discovery of development statistics, a catalog of nearly 10,000 indicators that should be searchable in many languages by a model small enough to self-host. As AI assistants and agents increasingly mediate access to public data and statistics, this retrieval step decides whether an answer is grounded in the right indicator or series, making discoverability a precondition for disseminating data through AI. Because usage logs cannot provide training signal for indicators no one has searched, we generate the queries instead. $\textbf{DevDataBench}$ is a fully LLM-generated benchmark of grounded, facet-targeted queries across 15 languages, covering every indicator for both training and evaluation. A fine-tuned 118M-parameter CPU encoder outperforms every zero-shot baseline, including $\texttt{text-embedding-3-large}$ (0.707 vs.\ 0.556 nDCG@10), with the largest gains in low-resource languages. We release the benchmark, pipeline, models, and a reusable PI-FT framework.

</details>


### [63] [A Single Rewrite Suffices: Empirical Lessons from Production Skill Description Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30775v1)
*Yangqiaoyu Zhou,Mohammad Alqudah,Kwei-Herng Lai,Aaron Halfaker,Yingqi Xiong,Yaar Harari*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 优化企业agent技能描述以提升路由准确率，虽是具体应用但涉及自动化策略，略有迁移价值。

TL;DR: 通过自动描述优化流程解决AI代理技能路由中的描述重叠问题，达到与手动调优相当的性能并大幅减少工程工作量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI代理技能数量增加，手动调整技能描述以维持路由准确性成为工程瓶颈，需要自动化方法。

Method: 提出自动描述优化流程，在生产级代理上部署，并通过消融实验分析关键组件（如一次LLM重写、迭代预算、反馈信号等）的影响。

Result: 自动优化达到79.2% F1，与手动调优的79.4%相当，每个技能工程时间从120分钟降至3.8分钟（加速32倍）；消融表明一次LLM重写即可获得大部分改进，其他组件影响小于0.5%。

Conclusion: 描述优化有效解决描述重叠导致的碰撞，但不能解决技能意图真正重叠的情况，并提供了诊断指标（大训练-验证F1差距）以指导架构层面干预。

中文摘要：企业人工智能代理通过将用户查询与自然语言技能描述进行匹配，将查询路由到专门技能。当两个技能具有重叠的描述时，路由LLM会错误路由查询，我们将这种失败称为技能碰撞。随着代理扩展到数十个技能，手动调整描述以保持路由准确性成为一个显著的工程瓶颈。我们在一个生产级企业群聊代理（9个技能，372个回归测试案例）上部署了一个自动描述优化流程。该流程生成的描述平均F1为79.2%，与手动调整描述的79.4% F1相匹配（每个技能的平均差异为-0.20%，在0.78%的多种子噪声容限内），同时将每个技能的工程工作量从120分钟减少到3.8分钟（加速32倍）。然后我们检验了哪些流程组件实际上驱动了这一匹配。在生产系统和ToolBench（16k工具）上的系统消融实验揭示，仅使用任何可用的假阳性和假阴性案例进行一次LLM重写就能捕获大部分可用改进。我们测试的其他设计选择（迭代预算、反馈信号组成、混淆对的双重编辑以及训练集大小）各自对最终F1的影响小于0.5%。描述优化解决了由重叠描述引起的技能碰撞，但无法解决两个技能预期范围真正重叠的情况。我们识别出一个诊断指标（大的训练-验证F1差距），用于标记后一种情况，需要进行架构层面而非文本层面的干预。

Original abstract: Enterprise AI agents route user queries to specialized skills by matching queries against natural language skill descriptions. When two skills share overlapping descriptions, the routing LLM misroutes queries, a failure we term skill collision. As agents scale to dozens of skills, manually tuning descriptions to maintain routing accuracy becomes a significant engineering bottleneck. We deploy an automated description optimization pipeline on a production enterprise group chat agent (9 skills, 372 regression cases). The pipeline produces descriptions averaging 79.2% F1, matching manually tuned descriptions at 79.4% F1 (average per-skill difference -0.20%, within the 0.78% multi-seed noise floor), while reducing per-skill engineering effort from 120 minutes to 3.8 minutes (32 times speedup). We then examine which pipeline components actually drive this match. Systematic ablation on both the production system and ToolBench (16k tools) reveals that a single LLM rewrite using any available false-positive and false-negative cases captures most of the available improvement. Other design choices we tested (iteration budget, feedback signal composition, dual editing of confused pairs, and training set size) each affect final F1 by less than 0.5%. Description optimization addresses skill collisions caused by overlapping descriptions but cannot resolve cases where two skills intended scopes genuinely overlap. We identify a diagnostic (a large train-validation F1 gap) that flags the latter cases for architectural rather than text-level intervention.

</details>


### [64] [Test-Time Verification for Text-to-SQL via Outcome Reward Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30851v1)
*Mattia Tritto,Giuseppe Farano,Dario Di Palma,Gaetano Rossiello,Fedelucio Narducci,Dharmashankar Subramanian,Tommaso Di Noia*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 使用结果奖励模型进行Text-to-SQL测试时验证，可视为代码生成agent的验证方法。

TL;DR: 提出GradeSQL框架，利用结果奖励模型（ORM）进行测试时验证，在Text-to-SQL任务中显著优于启发式策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时推理策略（如Best-of-N和多数投票）依赖启发式信号，语义区分能力有限，需更有效的验证方法。

Method: 提出GradeSQL，通过自动候选生成和基于执行的标注训练任务特定ORM，并集成到验证驱动的Best-of-N流程中。

Result: 在BIRD和Spider基准上，ORM选择优于执行-based Best-of-N和多数投票，分别提升高达4.33%和2.10%。

Conclusion: ORM-based验证是Text-to-SQL中一种简单、有效且可扩展的启发式策略替代方案。

中文摘要：提升大型语言模型（LLM）在推理时的可靠性是文本到SQL等结构化推理任务中的核心挑战。常见的测试时推理策略，包括Best-of-N采样和多数投票，依赖于诸如执行成功或输出频率等启发式信号，这些信号在候选输出中提供的语义区分能力有限。在这项工作中，我们研究了结果奖励模型（ORM）作为文本到SQL测试时验证的学习语义评分函数。虽然ORM之前已被探索用于测试时扩展和对齐，但它们在结构化查询生成中的应用仍未得到充分探索。我们引入了GradeSQL，一个可扩展的框架，通过自动生成候选和基于执行的标注来训练任务特定的ORM，从而实现无需人工标注的验证器训练。我们将ORM集成到基于验证的Best-of-N流程中，并在BIRD和Spider基准上对多个开源LLM系列进行了评估。基于ORM的选择始终优于基于执行的Best-of-N和多数投票，在BIRD上提升高达+4.33%，在Spider上提升+2.10%。我们进一步表明，ORM在更大的候选集上有效扩展，并在复杂查询上产生更强的改进。总体而言，我们的结果表明，基于ORM的验证为文本到SQL提供了一种简单、有效且可扩展的启发式测试时选择策略的替代方案。代码、数据集和模型已公开提供。

Original abstract: Improving the reliability of large language models (LLMs) at inference time is a central challenge in structured reasoning tasks such as Text-to-SQL. Common test-time inference strategies, including Best-of-N sampling and Majority Voting, rely on heuristic signals such as execution success or output frequency, which provide limited semantic discrimination across candidate outputs. In this work, we study Outcome Reward Models (ORMs) as learned semantic scoring functions for test-time verification in Text-to-SQL. While ORMs have been previously explored for test-time scaling and alignment, their application to structured query generation remains underexplored. We introduce GradeSQL, a scalable framework for training task-specific ORMs via automated candidate generation and execution-based labeling, enabling verifier training without manual annotation. We integrate ORMs into a verification-driven Best-of-N pipeline and evaluate our approach on the BIRD and Spider benchmarks across multiple open-source LLM families. ORM-based selection consistently outperforms execution-based Best-of-N and Majority Voting, with gains of up to +4.33% on BIRD and +2.10% on Spider. We further show that ORMs scale effectively with larger candidate sets and yield stronger improvements on complex queries. Overall, our results demonstrate that ORM-based verification provides a simple, effective, and scalable alternative to heuristic test-time selection strategies for Text-to-SQL. Code datasets and models are publicly available.

</details>

### [65] [ARMOR: Adaptive Retriever Optimization for Low-Resource Telecom Question Answering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29706v1)
*Heshan Fernando,Quan Xiao,Yan Xin,Tianyi Chen*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: RAG检索自适应优化，对agent检索组件改进有借鉴。

TL;DR: 本研究提出ARMOR方法，通过查询端检索器自适应而非生成器微调，联合优化RAG似然和InfoNCE目标，在电信领域QA中提升检索和生成性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电信QA中证据分散且依赖技术细节，生成器微调在低资源子领域易过专化，因此探索固定生成器下的查询端检索器自适应作为替代方案。

Method: 提出ARMOR方法，学习RAG检索分布和InfoNCE softmax的独立温度，并正则化自适应查询编码器向基础编码器，联合优化生成效用和语义检索几何。

Result: 在电信检索和生成QA基准上，ARMOR在多个领域内设置中改善了证据检索和答案生成。

Conclusion: 查询端检索器自适应可以优于生成器端自适应，ARMOR通过联合优化RAG和对比目标有效提升电信领域QA性能。

中文摘要：电信问答（QA）是检索增强生成（RAG）的一个具有挑战性的场景：证据分散在标准、论文、百科全书资源和网络文档中，答案通常依赖于技术表格、方程和专门的协议语言。在低资源子领域，生成器微调可能会导致过专化并降低通用能力，因此查询端检索器自适应成为一种有吸引力的替代方案。为此，我们探讨固定生成器、查询自适应RAG系统是否能优于生成器端自适应，以及哪些检索器目标最支持该设置。我们通过容量比较来推动检索（而非生成器微调）作为自适应目标：在有界参数和软检索假设下，当查询编码器调优的有效维度较小时，其估计项可以小于监督微调。我们确定了两个特别相关的目标——潜在文档RAG似然（优化生成效用）和InfoNCE对比目标（改善语义检索几何结构）——并联合使用它们通过一种针对电信领域下游QA性能的检索器优化方法。具体来说，我们引入了ARMOR（自适应正则化混合检索器优化），它学习RAG检索分布和InfoNCE softmax的独立温度，并将自适应查询编码器向冻结的基础查询编码器进行正则化。在电信特定的检索和生成QA基准上，我们展示了ARMOR在多个领域内设置中改善了证据检索和答案生成。代码可在 https://github.com/heshandevaka/ARMOR.git 获取。

Original abstract: Telecom question answering (QA) is a challenging setting for retrieval-augmented generation (RAG): evidence is fragmented across standards, papers, encyclopedic resources, and web documents, and answers often hinge on technical tables, equations, and specialized protocol language. In low-resource subdomains, generator fine-tuning can over-specialize and degrade general capability, making query-side retriever adaptation an attractive alternative. To this end, we ask whether a fixed-generator, query-adapted RAG system can outperform generator-side adaptation, and which retriever objectives best support that setting. We motivate retrieval, rather than generator fine-tuning, as the adaptation target through a capacity comparison: under bounded-parameter and soft-retrieval assumptions, query-encoder tuning can have a smaller estimation term than supervised fine-tuning when its effective dimension is smaller. We identify two particularly relevant objectives -- the latent-document RAG likelihood, which optimizes generation utility, and the InfoNCE contrastive objective, which improves semantic retrieval geometry -- and leverage them jointly through a retriever optimization method targeting downstream QA performance in the telecom domain. Specifically, we introduce ARMOR, Adaptive Regularized Mixture Optimization for Retrievers, which learns separate temperatures for the RAG retrieval distribution and InfoNCE softmax and regularizes the adapted query encoder toward the frozen base query encoder. Across telecom-specific retrieval and generative QA benchmarks, we show that ARMOR improves evidence retrieval and answer generation in several in-domain settings. Code is available at https://github.com/heshandevaka/ARMOR.git.

</details>


### [66] [Diagnosing and Mitigating Context Rot in Long-horizon Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29718v1)
*Shijie Xia,Yikun Wang,Zhen Huang,Pengfei Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 研究长上下文任务中context rot现象及缓解方法，对长程agent任务有指导意义。

TL;DR: 本文研究LLM在长上下文中的“上下文腐烂”现象，发现其导致模型放弃或提前给出不确定答案，并提出通过上下文管理和事后拒绝采样缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在长时域任务中上下文长度增加导致模型能力下降，需要理解并缓解这一现象。

Method: 评估四个开源模型在三项基准上的表现，通过剪枝实验分析累积上下文与腐烂的关系，提出上下文管理和事后拒绝采样两种缓解策略。

Result: 揭示了普遍存在的腐烂现象，系统评估了七种上下文管理方法，并证明了腐烂感知拒绝采样的有效性。

Conclusion: 上下文管理和事后拒绝采样可有效缓解上下文腐烂，且两者结合可进一步提升性能。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地应用于长时域任务，长上下文已成为常态。上下文长度增加导致模型能力退化（称为“上下文腐烂”）已成为这些应用的核心问题。本文聚焦深度搜索场景，旨在研究腐烂现象及其缓解策略。通过在三项基准上评估四个旗舰开源模型，我们揭示了一种普遍但未被注意的腐烂现象：长上下文导致模型直接放弃或过早给出不确定答案，且该问题随上下文增长而加剧。通过剪枝实验，我们论证了累积上下文与腐烂现象之间的关系。此外，我们研究通过上下文管理和事后拒绝采样来缓解该问题。对于上下文管理，我们系统评估了七种不同方法（分属三类），基于性能、成本和对上下文腐烂的影响，为策略选择和使用提供明确指导。对于拒绝采样，我们开发了一种腐烂感知过滤策略，并在三种聚合方法上证明了其有效性。最后，我们展示了这两种方法可以结合以进一步提升性能。

Original abstract: Extensive context has become the norm as Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in long-horizon tasks. The concern that increasing context length degrades model capabilities, known as context rot, has become a central issue for these applications. In this paper, we focus on deep search scenarios, aiming to investigate the rot phenomenon and its mitigation strategies. By evaluating four flagship open-source models across three benchmarks, we reveal a prevalent but unnoticed rot phenomenon: extensive context causes models to directly give up or prematurely provide uncertain answers, and this issue is exacerbated as the context grows. Through pruning experiments, we demonstrate the relationship between the accumulated context and the rot phenomenon. Furthermore, we investigate mitigating this issue through context management and post-hoc rejection sampling. For context management, we systematically evaluate seven different methods across three categories, based on performance, cost, and impact on context rot, providing clear guidance for strategy selection and usage. For rejection sampling, we develop a rot-aware filtering strategy and demonstrate its effectiveness across three aggregation methods. Finally, we show that these two approaches can be combined for further performance improvements.

### [67] [TopoAgent: An Agentic Framework for Automated Topology Learning in Medical Imaging](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29763v1)
*Guangyu Meng,Pengfei Gu,Xueyang Li,Yiyu Shi,Erin Wolf Chambers,Danny Z. Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出LLM agent框架，包含感知-推理-行动-反思循环和双记忆，通用架构可迁移至代码优化agent。

TL;DR: TopoAgent是一个基于LLM的智能体框架，能自动选择最适合医学图像数据集的拓扑描述符并生成特征向量，无需任务特定训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多使用单一固定描述符，缺乏利用多样化拓扑表示的能力，且没有基于LLM的自动化框架来选择最优描述符。

Method: 提出TopoAgent，采用感知-推理-行动-反思循环，集成21个领域工具和双记忆，技能从15种描述符在26个数据集上的系统评估中提炼。

Result: TopoAgent能自动分析图像拓扑特征，选择并配置最优描述符，无需任务特定训练即可生成特征向量用于下游任务。

Conclusion: TopoAgent有效自动化拓扑描述符选择，填补了LLM智能体框架在拓扑学习中的空白，为医学图像分析提供新方法。

中文摘要：拓扑数据分析（TDA），特别是持续同调（PH），能够捕捉医学图像中的几何结构属性（例如，连通分量、环路、形状特征），而这些是传统的像素级深度学习方法经常忽略的。尽管已知许多拓扑描述符可以将持续图（PDs）或原始图像转换为拓扑特征向量，但现有方法大多默认使用单一固定的描述符（例如，持续图像），导致拓扑表示的多样性在很大程度上未被探索。据我们所知，目前还没有已知的基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体框架能够自动确定最适合给定图像数据集的拓扑描述符，并为下游任务生成相应的拓扑特征向量。为了填补这一空白，我们提出了TopoAgent，这是一个基于LLM的智能体框架，可自动化医学图像分析的拓扑学习。TopoAgent通过一个由21个领域特定工具和跨运行积累经验的双重记忆支持的感知-推理-行动-反思循环来运作。其技能集源于对15种拓扑描述符在26个数据集上使用六种分类器进行的系统评估。TopoAgent分析输入图像及其拓扑特征，推理哪些拓扑描述符最适合输入，并确定最优描述符及其配置，整个过程无需任务特定训练。

Original abstract: Topological data analysis (TDA), particularly persistent homology (PH), captures geometric structural properties in medical images (e.g., connected components, loops, shape characteristics), which conventional pixel-level deep learning approaches often neglect. While many topological descriptors are known for converting persistence diagrams (PDs) or raw images into topological feature vectors, existing methods mostly default to a single fixed descriptor (e.g., persistence images), leaving the diversity of topological representations largely unexplored. To the best of our knowledge, there is no known large language model (LLM)-based agentic framework that can automatically determine the most suitable topological descriptors for a given image dataset and produce the corresponding topological feature vectors for downstream tasks. To fill this gap, we propose \textbf{TopoAgent}, an LLM-based agentic framework that automates topology learning for medical image analysis.TopoAgent operates through a Perception--Reasoning--Action--Reflection loop supported by 21 domain-specific tools and dual memory that accumulates experience across runs. Its skill set is distilled from systematic evaluation of 15 topological descriptors across 26 datasets with six classifiers. TopoAgent analyzes input images and their topological characteristics, reasons about which topological descriptors best suit the input, and determines the optimal descriptor and its configuration, all without task-specific training.

### [68] [To Tab or Not to Tab: Measuring Critical Engagement in AI Code Completion Tools Using Behavioral Signals and Attention Checks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30549v1)
*Jessica Hutchison,Ian Tyler Applebaum,Kenneth Angelikas,Kush Rakesh Patel,Phuoc Nguyen,Antonio Lazaro,Nicholas Rucinski,Rahad Arman Nabid,Stephen MacNeil*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Clover工具和交互指标分类体系，通过注意力检查揭示学生反思性参与问题，发现Tab接受率与注意力检查表现负相关，停留时间与表现正相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前定性研究表明学生未能批判性评估AI代码建议，需要量化工具和方法来测量和促进反思性参与。

Method: 开发Clover工具记录交互并嵌入注意力检查，基于文献构建行为交互指标分类体系，分析交互模式、注意力检查表现与任务性能的关系。

Result: 较高的Tab接受率与较低的注意力检查表现相关，较长的停留时间与较高的注意力检查表现相关。

Conclusion: 编程过程数据和注意力检查可支持AI辅助编程中的反思性参与。

中文摘要：AI代码补全工具，如Github Copilot，通过提供代码建议来帮助学生编写程序。然而，近期的定性研究表明，学生未能批判性地评估这些建议。我们提出了Clover，一个代码补全工具，它记录学生与代码建议的交互，并额外提供注意力检查以探究编程任务中的反思性参与。我们还基于文献，开发了一套用于AI辅助编程的行为交互指标分类体系。我们分析了交互模式、注意力检查参与度与任务表现之间的关系。我们观察到，更高的Tab接受率与较低的注意力检查表现相关，而更长的停留时间则与较高的注意力检查表现相关。最后，我们讨论了编程过程数据和注意力检查如何支持AI辅助编程中的反思性参与。

Original abstract: AI code completion tools, such as Github Copilot, provide students with code suggestions to help them write programs. However, recent qualitative studies suggest that students fail to critically evaluate these suggestions. We present Clover, a code completion tool that logs students' interactions with code suggestions and additionally offers attention checks to probe reflective engagement during programming tasks. We also develop a taxonomy of behavioral interaction metrics for AI-assisted programming, informed by literature. We analyzed relationships between interaction patterns, engagement with attention checks, and task performance. We observed that higher rates of tab accept were associated with lower attention check performance, while increased dwell time was associated with higher attention check performance. We conclude by discussing how programming process data and attention checks might support reflective engagement in AI-assisted programming.

</details>

### [69] [Mandol: An Agglomerative Agent Memory System for Long-Term Conversations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29778v1)
*Yuhan Zhang,Zhiyuan Guo,Ziheng Zeng,Wei Wang,Wentao Wu,Lijie Xu*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: 提出统一聚合记忆系统，优化查询与上下文生成，直接贡献于agent记忆管理，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: Mandol通过统一的记忆原生架构和聚合语义数据结构，实现了长期对话智能体高效准确的跨会话记忆管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体记忆系统依赖异构数据库导致碎片化、高延迟和检索噪声，影响LLM的准确性和效率。

Method: 提出分层记忆模型（基础层+抽象层）、聚合语义数据结构（融合键值/向量/图）和定量查询机制（自适应路由、去噪、令牌约束），检索不涉及LLM。

Result: 在LoCoMo和LongMemEval上取得最佳准确率，并实现5.4倍检索加速和4.8倍插入加速（10 QPS并发），在消费级硬件上低延迟。

Conclusion: Mandol证明了统一记忆架构能有效提升长期对话中记忆检索的准确性和效率，优于现有异构数据库方案。

中文摘要：长期对话智能体需要记住并查询跨会话、多类型的具有复杂相关性的信息。现有的智能体记忆系统依赖于异构的向量和图数据库，这导致记忆信息碎片化并引起高跨数据库I/O延迟。在检索方面，常见的RAG风格方法倾向于引入噪声、遗漏相关线索且缺乏令牌预算控制，降低了LLM的准确性和效率。我们提出Mandol，一种聚合记忆系统，将碎片化的记忆表示和存储统一到原生的记忆架构中。其核心组件包括：（1）分层记忆模型，将记忆组织为表示原始记忆信息的基础层和将基础记忆聚合为可追溯抽象记忆的高级抽象层，两者统一表示为结构化语义图；（2）结合SemanticMap和SemanticGraph的聚合语义数据结构，原生融合键值、向量和图结构，并提供统一的混合检索操作符以消除跨数据库I/O；（3）定量查询机制，具有查询自适应路由、定量去噪和冲突解决以及令牌约束的上下文生成，检索过程中不涉及LLM。在两个广泛使用的长期对话基准LoCoMo和LongMemEval上的实验表明，Mandol在代表性智能体记忆系统中取得了最佳的整体准确率。在性能比较方面，Mandol在10 QPS并发负载下获得了5.4倍的检索加速和4.8倍的插入加速，同时在消费级硬件上仍保持低延迟。

Original abstract: Long-term conversational agents need to remember and query cross-session, multi-typed information with complex correlations. Existing agent memory systems rely on heterogeneous vector and graph databases, which fragment memory information and cause high cross-database I/O latency. For retrieval, common RAG-style methods tend to introduce noise, miss correlated clues, and lack token budget control, degrading LLM accuracy and efficiency.
  We propose Mandol, an agglomerative memory system that consolidates fragmented memory representations and storage into a unified memory-native architecture. Its core components include: (1) a hierarchical memory model that organizes memory into a basic layer representing raw memory information and a high-level abstract layer that agglomerates basic memories into traceable abstract memories, both uniformly represented as structured semantic graphs; (2) an agglomerative semantic data structure combining SemanticMap and SemanticGraph, which natively fuses key-value, vector, and graph structures and provides unified hybrid retrieval operators to eliminate cross-database I/O; and (3) a quantitative query mechanism with query-adaptive routing, quantitative denoising and conflict resolution, and token-constrained context generation, all without involving LLMs during retrieval. Experiments on two widely used long-term conversation benchmarks, LoCoMo and LongMemEval, show that Mandol achieves the best overall accuracy among representative agent memory systems. For performance comparison, Mandol also obtains a 5.4x retrieval speedup and a 4.8x insertion speedup under 10 QPS concurrent load, while still maintaining low latency on consumer-grade hardware.

</details>


### [70] [Experience Graphs: The Data Foundation for Self-Improving Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29823v1)
*Gang Liao,Yujia He,Abdullah Ozturk,Zhouyang Li,Ying Wang,Zhitong Guo,Hongsen Qin,Yaobin Qin,Tao Yang,Zewei Jiang,Dianshi Li,Jort Gemmeke,Jiangyuan Li,Liyuan Li,Nathan Yan,Masha Basmanova,Uladzimir Pashkevich,Matt Steiner,Pedro Pedreira,Rob Fergus,Anirudh Goyal,Carole-Jean Wu,Gaoxiang Liu,Andrew Witten,Daniel J. Abadi*

Main category: cs.DB

Selection reason: 提出经验图作为agent数据基础，支持长程任务、经验复用和闭环训练，直接相关代码优化agent。

TL;DR: Trellis将智能体探索产生的经验图作为数据库状态管理，使崩溃恢复、跨会话复用和训练数据提取成为架构副产物，在KernelEvolve中实现10倍加速和52%更低令牌成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体框架将经验视为可丢弃的状态（JSON检查点、会话日志），无法在崩溃后恢复、跨用户查询或物化为训练数据，限制了智能体的累积和扩展。

Method: Trellis将经验图作为一等公民的数据库状态，将搜索操作（前沿选择、跨会话复用、训练数据提取、时间旅行查询）映射为数据库访问模式，使智能体成为无状态计算。

Result: 在Meta的KernelEvolve生产系统中，Trellis实现跨会话复用，达到约10倍目标加速，令牌成本降低52%。

Conclusion: Trellis将推理时搜索从可丢弃计算转变为持久的机构资产，使经验图具有累积性，类似日志使数据库可靠。

中文摘要：数据库社区通过认识到新的工作负载需要新的系统架构，不断推动技术发展。我们认为，长期智能体任务——代码生成、科学发现、硬件设计——正是这样的工作负载。这些智能体进行探索：它们生成工件、执行工具、观察失败、分支并在数百个步骤中进行修复。这种搜索产生了一个结构化对象，我们称之为经验图：可执行的工件、工具输出、奖励、兄弟比较和因果谱系。然而，现有的智能体框架将这种经验视为可丢弃的状态——JSON检查点和会话日志，在崩溃后无法恢复，无法跨用户查询，也无法物化为训练数据。我们提出Trellis：一个数据基础，将经验图视为一等公民、受管、可查询的数据库状态。核心洞察是，对经验图的搜索是一种数据库访问模式。前沿选择是一个查询，跨会话复用是向量驱动的图检索，训练数据提取是一个物化视图，而重建智能体在过去任何步骤的知识是一个时间旅行查询。当数据库拥有经验图时，智能体变成无状态计算，崩溃恢复、水平扩展和闭环训练飞轮作为架构副产物出现。我们在Meta的生产加速器核优化器KernelEvolve中落地了该设计，其中跨会话复用达到了约10倍的目标加速，同时令牌成本降低了52%。更广泛地说，Trellis将推理时搜索从可丢弃的计算转变为持久的机构资产：日志使数据库可靠；经验图可能使智能体具有累积性。

Original abstract: The database community has repeatedly advanced the state of the art by recognizing that new workloads demand new system architectures. We argue that long-horizon agentic tasks -- code generation, scientific discovery, hardware design -- are such a workload. These agents explore: they generate artifacts, execute tools, observe failures, branch, and repair over hundreds of steps. This search produces a structured object we call an experience graph: executable artifacts, tool outputs, rewards, sibling comparisons, and causal lineage. Yet existing agent frameworks treat this experience as disposable state -- JSON checkpoints and session logs that cannot be recovered after a crash, queried across users, or materialized into training data. We propose Trellis: a data foundation that treats the experience graph as first-class, governed, queryable database state. The core insight is that search over experience graphs is a database access pattern. Frontier selection is a query, cross-session reuse is vector-seeded graph retrieval, training-data extraction is a materialized view, and reconstructing what an agent knew at any past step is a time-travel query. When the database owns the experience graph, agents become stateless compute, and crash recovery, horizontal scaling, and a closed-loop training flywheel emerge as architectural byproducts. We ground the design in KernelEvolve, a production accelerator-kernel optimizer at Meta, where cross-session reuse reaches a target speedup roughly 10x faster at 52% lower token cost. More broadly, Trellis turns inference-time search from disposable computation into a durable institutional asset: logs made databases reliable; experience graphs may make agents cumulative.

</details>

### [71] [Always-OnAgents:A Survey of Persistent Memory, State, and Governance in LLMAgents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30306v1)
*Tianyu Ding,Aditya Nannapaneni,Bingfan Liu,Ling Zhang*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 持久状态agent综述，系统分析agent记忆与治理，对agent设计有直接启发

TL;DR: 论文通过六个诊断轴和生命周期分析始终在线智能体的持久状态，发现现有工作偏向积累和检索而忽视治理，提出了AOEP-v0评估协议以弥补这一缺口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献在持久状态管理上侧重积累和检索，对治理、恢复和放弃关注不足，需要系统性调查并引入具体评估方法。

Method: 基于435篇编码文献的语料库，使用六轴诊断（权威性、范围、可变性、来源、可恢复性、可操作性）和生命周期模型进行分析，并推出AOEP-v0评估协议。

Result: 发现文献集中于状态积累与检索，而治理、恢复和放弃等环节薄弱；AOEP-v0协议通过评分状态变更和恢复义务来量化治理要求。

Conclusion: 该调查将始终在线智能体与多个领域连接，并强调治理需求的重要性，为未来研究提供了具体方向。

中文摘要：始终在线的智能体是这样一类系统，其未来行为依赖于早期交互中累积的持久状态。我们将它们视为持久状态系统：操作系统包括可检索的记忆，还包括任务账本、权限、凭证、承诺、来源和审计记录、共享状态、触发条件以及链接到这些记录的外部承诺效果。该调查通过六个诊断轴（每个状态项：权威性、范围、可变性、来源、可恢复性和可操作性）和一个生命周期（状态被写入、验证、组织、检索、执行、更新、遗忘、审计，有时回滚）来阅读文献。在435篇编码的文献语料库（被视为有范围的地图而非详尽普查）中，文献更侧重于积累和检索状态，而非治理、恢复或放弃它。因此，我们引入了始终在线评估协议（AOEP-v0），一个试点评估合同，通过评分状态变更和恢复义务而非仅答案质量，使这些治理需求具体化。由此产生的议程将始终在线智能体与数据库、分布式系统、形式化方法、能力安全性和机器遗忘联系起来。

Original abstract: Always-on agents are systems whose future behavior depends on durable state accumulated across earlier interactions. We treat them as persistent-state systems: the operative system includes retrievable memories, but also task ledgers, permissions, credentials, commitments, provenance and audit records, shared state, trigger conditions, and externally committed effects linked to those records. The survey reads the literature through six diagnostic axes for each state item, authority, scope, mutability, provenance, recoverability, and actionability, and through a lifecycle in which state is written, validated, organized, retrieved, acted upon, updated, forgotten, audited, and sometimes rolled back. Across a 435-work coded corpus, treated as a scoped map rather than an exhaustive census, the literature concentrates more heavily on accumulating and retrieving state than on governing, recovering, or relinquishing it. We therefore introduce the Always-On Evaluation Protocol (AOEP-v0), a pilot evaluation contract that makes these governance requirements concrete by scoring state mutation and recovery obligations rather than answer quality alone. The resulting agenda connects always-on agents to databases, distributed systems, formal methods, capability security, and machine unlearning.

</details>


### [72] [Translating Natural Language to Strategic Temporal Specifications via LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30441v2)
*Marco Aruta,Francesco Improta,Vadim Malvone,Aniello Murano,Vladana Perlić*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 用LLM将自然语言转换为形式化规约，支持多智能体系统验证，可辅助agent规约生成。

TL;DR: 提出基于LLM的框架，将自然语言策略需求翻译为ATL/ATL*公式，通过微调小模型达到与强基线相当的性能，并集成到模型检查器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动编写MAS的形式化规范容易出错、耗时且需要专业知识，缺乏从自然语言推导MAS规范的现有方法论。

Method: 创建专家验证的数据集，对小型LLM（3-7B参数）进行领域内微调，以执行NL到ATL/ATL*的翻译；评估不同LLM作为裁判的可靠性，并将工具嵌入策略逻辑模型检查器。

Result: 微调的小模型达到0.84语义准确率，与强少样本专有基线（0.86）统计相当；开源模型Llama-3.3-70B作为裁判最可靠，而强专有模型不可靠。

Conclusion: 所提框架能够使非专家用户用自然语言指定策略属性，且开源模型在保护隐私的同时可与专有模型竞争，但裁判选择需谨慎。

中文摘要：系统需求的严格形式化是对多智能体系统（MAS）进行验证的基本前提。然而，编写正确的形式化规范是一项众所周知的容易出错、耗时且需要专业知识的任务。在MAS中，这一困难更加突出，因为需求必须捕捉策略能力和时间目标。目前，尚无成熟的方法从自然语言推导MAS规范。我们提出了一个框架，利用大型语言模型（LLM）将策略需求的自然语言描述翻译成良构的ATL/ATL*公式。由于没有可用的数据集支持NL到ATL/ATL*翻译任务的监督学习，我们创建并整理了一个新颖的、经专家验证的数据集，用于训练和评估微调模型。在保留测试集上，根据与专家注释一致性最高的LLM裁判评估，领域内微调的小型开源模型（3-7B参数）匹配了强大的少样本专有API基线。我们最佳微调系统的语义准确率达到0.84，在统计上与最强少样本专有基线的0.86相当，同时将需求保持在本地。我们进一步发现，裁判可靠性与生成器强度成反比。开源模型Llama-3.3-70B与人类判断最接近，而最强的专有模型是最不可靠的裁判，过度拒绝参考的忠实释义。为了评估生成规范的实际适用性，我们将我们的工具嵌入现有的策略逻辑模型检查器中，使非专家用户能够用自然语言指定策略属性。

Original abstract: A rigorous formalization of system requirements is a fundamental prerequisite for the verification of Multi-Agent Systems (MAS). However, writing correct formal specifications is well known as an error-prone, time-consuming, and expertise-intensive task. This difficulty is further accentuated in MAS, where requirements must capture strategic abilities and temporal objectives. At present, there is no established methodology for deriving MAS specifications from natural language. We present a framework for translating Natural Language descriptions of strategic requirements into well-formed ATL/ATL* formulas using Large Language Models (LLMs). Since no available dataset supports supervised learning for the NL-to-ATL/ATL* translation task, we create and curate a novel expert-validated dataset, employed for training and evaluating fine-tuned models. On a held-out test set, evaluated under the LLM judge that best agrees with expert annotations, in-domain fine-tuning of small open-weight models (3 - 7B parameters) matches strong few-shot proprietary API baselines. Our best fine-tuned system reaches 0.84 semantic accuracy, statistically on par with 0.86 for the strongest few-shot proprietary baseline, while keeping requirements on-premises. We further find that judge reliability is inverse to generator strength. The open-weight Llama-3.3-70B tracks human verdicts most closely, whereas the strongest proprietary models are the least reliable judges, over-rejecting faithful paraphrases of the reference. To assess the practical applicability of the generated specifications, we embed our tool to an existing strategic logics model checker, enabling non-expert users to specify strategic properties in natural language.

</details>


### [73] [A Role-Based Multi-Agent Model for Climate Adaptation Deliberation Across Living Labs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00046v1)
*Önder Gürcan,David Eric John Herbert,F. LeRon Shultz,Christopher Frantz,Ivan Puga-Gonzalez*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种模块化多层次基于智能体的架构，整合认知决策和制度行为，用于模拟民主气候治理过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ABM研究要么关注制度动态，要么关注个体行为机制，缺乏将两者整合的统一框架。

Method: 构建模块化多层次ABM，结合（i）基于动机的个体决策（HUMAT/MOA）、（ii）社会同质网络影响、（iii）NGO、媒体和政客的策略模块，并支持经验校准与场景探索。

Result: 提出了一个可校准的、模块化的架构设计及其集成逻辑，但未呈现实证结果。

Conclusion: 该多层次方法有助于建模民主气候治理，未来可通过实证验证和泛化进一步推进。

中文摘要：气候治理过程涉及异质性公民、倡导团体、媒体行动者和政治决策者之间的复杂互动。虽然基于智能体的模型（ABMs）已被广泛用于研究环境政策和社会生态系统，但许多现有方法要么单独关注制度动态，要么单独关注个体行为机制。本文提出了一种模块化的多层次基于智能体的架构，该架构将经验驱动的认知决策模型与战略性制度行为整合在一个统一的模拟框架中。该架构结合了（i）通过HUMAT和MOA框架操作化的基于动机的个体决策，（ii）通过人口统计同质性网络实现的社会嵌入影响过程，以及（iii）针对环境非政府组织（NGOs）、媒体智能体和政治家的制度策略模块。政治决策源于多种信号的聚合，包括专家输入、公众动员、政党倾向和媒体框架。该模型设计为通过从调查数据中得出的合成群体以及通过生活实验室利益相关者参与所知的制度参数进行经验校准，并支持气候相关土地利用治理过程的场景探索。本文不呈现实证结果，而是聚焦于该模型的设计原则、模块化结构和集成逻辑。我们讨论了这种多层次方法如何有助于对民主气候治理进行建模，并概述了泛化和未来验证的路径。

Original abstract: Climate governance processes involve complex interactions between heterogeneous citizens, advocacy groups, media actors, and political decision-makers. While agent-based models (ABMs) have been widely used to study environmental policy and socio-ecological systems, many existing approaches focus either on institutional dynamics or individual behavioural mechanisms in isolation. This paper presents a modular multi-level agent-based architecture that integrates empirically grounded cognitive decision models with strategic institutional behaviour within a unified simulation framework. The architecture combines (i) motive-based individual decision-making operationalised through the HUMAT and MOA frameworks, (ii) socially embedded influence processes via demographic homophily networks, and (iii) institutional strategy modules for environmental non-governmental organisations (NGOs), media agents, and politicians. Political decisions emerge from the aggregation of multiple signals, including expert input, public mobilisation, party alignment, and media framing. The model is designed to be empirically calibrated through synthetic populations derived from survey data and and institutional parameters informed through Living Lab stakeholder engagement, and to support scenario-based exploration of climate-relevant land-use governance processes. Rather than presenting empirical results, this paper focuses on the architectural design principles, modular structure, and integration logic of the model. We discuss how this multi-layered approach contributes to the modelling of democratic climate governance and outline pathways for generalization and future validation.

</details>

### [74] [Trust Your Instincts: Confidence-Driven Test-Time RL for Vision-Language-Action Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29892v1)
*Siyao Chen,Jiakang Yuan,Jiaxin Wang,Tao Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: VLA模型自我改进的测试时强化学习，利用内部置信度，对agent自我改进有启发。

TL;DR: T^2VLA利用VLA模型的内在评估能力，通过轨迹相似性作为内在奖励实现无需外部反馈的RL策略改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL方法依赖外部环境反馈，而VLA模型具有内在评估能力，可用来驱动策略改进。

Method: 提出T^2VLA框架，使用轨迹相似性作为内在奖励，并设计置信度驱动的双专家引导机制。

Result: 在LIBERO和RoboTwin上超越监督基线，接近使用真实奖励的Oracle RL性能。

Conclusion: T^2VLA无需外部奖励即可实现有效的策略改进，并适用于不同VLA架构。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）已成为推动视觉-语言-行动模型（VLA）超越静态模仿学习不可或缺的方法。然而，现有的RL方法通常需要外部环境反馈，依赖预定义的成功信号来指导策略更新。在这项工作中，我们展示了VLA模型拥有有用的内部评估能力：在离散动作的VLA中，具有更高生成置信度的轨迹更有可能成功。基于这一观察，我们引入了T^2VLA（测试时VLA），这是一个与架构无关的测试时RL框架，使VLA模型能够实现自我引导的策略改进。T^2VLA不依赖外部奖励，而是利用轨迹级别与高置信度专家演示的相似性作为内在奖励信号。此外，我们提出了置信度驱动的双专家引导机制，它动态平衡了用于探索的局部伪专家和用于训练稳定性的全局专家池。在LIBERO和RoboTwin基准上的大量实验表明，T^2VLA持续优于监督基线，并且接近使用真实奖励的Oracle RL性能，实现了无需外部奖励反馈的有效改进。此外，T^2VLA适应不同的VLA范式，包括OpenVLA-OFT和pi系列。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become indispensable for pushing Vision-Language-Action Models (VLAs) beyond static imitation learning. However, existing RL methods typically require external environmental feedback, relying on predefined success signals to guide policy updates. In this work, we show that VLA models possess useful internal evaluative capabilities: in discrete-action VLAs, trajectories with higher generation confidence are significantly more likely to succeed. Based on this observation, we introduce T^2VLA (Test-time VLA), an architecture-agnostic test-time RL framework that enables VLA models to achieve self-bootstrapping policy improvement. Instead of relying on external rewards, T^2VLA leverages trajectory-level similarity to high-confidence expert demonstrations as an intrinsic reward signal. In addition, we propose a Confidence-Driven Dual Expert Bootstrapping mechanism, which dynamically balances a Local Pseudo-Expert for exploration and a Global Expert Pool for training stability. Extensive experiments on the LIBERO and RoboTwin benchmarks show that T^2VLA consistently outperforms supervised baselines and approaches oracle RL performance with ground-truth rewards, achieving effective improvement without external reward feedback. Furthermore, T^2VLA adapts to distinct VLA paradigms, including both OpenVLA-OFT and the pi series.

</details>


### [75] [Critical Interval MSE: Toward Reliable Offline Validation for Robot Manipulation Policies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29898v1)
*Haoxu Huang,Tongsam Zheng,Yifan Chen,Jiacheng You,Yang Gao*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 机器人策略离线验证指标CI-MSE，可迁移至coding agent的评估与验证。

TL;DR: 提出CI-MSE指标，通过限制在任务关键片段计算误差并配合动作对齐，显著提升离线验证与实际性能的相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界评估成本高、难以复现，且验证损失与实际性能相关性差，需要更好的离线验证指标。

Method: 提出临界区间均方误差（CI-MSE），将误差计算限制在任务关键片段，并引入动作对齐程序以匹配部署行为。

Result: 在仿真和真实实验中，CI-MSE的Spearman秩相关性达到-0.87，远超原始MSE的-0.61，且对超参数鲁棒。

Conclusion: 提供了一种简单可靠的离线验证工具，加速策略迭代。

中文摘要：真实世界评估是机器人策略的黄金标准，因为它针对机器人最终需要处理的物理条件和部署挑战进行测试。然而，真实世界评估也是迭代机器人策略的瓶颈：成本高昂、难以复现，并且往往过于稀疏，无法可靠地比较相近的模型变体。一个直接的性能代理是专家演示的验证损失，但这个代理通常与真实世界性能的相关性较差。在本文中，我们引入了临界区间均方误差（CI-MSE），一种直观简单但有效的离线验证指标。CI-MSE将误差计算限制在任务关键片段，并配以简单的动作对齐程序，以更好地匹配部署时的行为。通过仿真和真实世界实验，CI-MSE在验证误差与部署性能之间产生了比原始MSE更强的相关性。在广泛的策略检查点上，CI-MSE的Spearman秩相关性达到-0.87，比原始MSE的-0.61更接近理想值-1，显示出显著的改进。我们通过敏感性分析表明，我们的指标对广泛的超参数具有鲁棒性。我们进一步研究了CI-MSE在评估分布偏移下的有效性，并提出了使用该指标的设计边界。总之，本文提供了一个简单可靠的离线验证工具，用于加速策略迭代。项目网页：https://ci-mse.github.io/

Original abstract: Real-world evaluation is the gold standard for robot policies because it tests them against the physical conditions and deployment challenges they are ultimately designed to handle. However, real-world evaluation is also the bottleneck for iterating on robot policies: it is costly, difficult to reproduce, and often too sparse to reliably compare nearby model variants. A straightforward proxy for performance is validation loss on expert demonstrations, but this proxy is often poorly correlated with real-world performance. In this paper, we introduce Critical Interval MSE (CI-MSE), an intuitively simple yet effective offline validation metric. CI-MSE restricts error computation to task-critical segments and pairs it with simple action-alignment procedures that better match rollout-time behavior. Across simulation and real-world experiments, CI-MSE yields a stronger correlation between validation error and rollout performance than raw MSE. Across a wide range of policy checkpoints, CI-MSE achieves a Spearman's rank correlation of $-0.87$, much closer to the ideal value of $-1$ than raw MSE's $-0.61$, demonstrating a significant improvement. We show through sensitivity analysis that our metric is robust to a wide range of hyperparameters. We further study the effectiveness of CI-MSE under evaluation distribution shifts and suggest design boundaries when using this metric. In summary, this paper provides a simple and reliable offline validation tool for accelerating policy iteration. Project webpage: https://ci-mse.github.io/

</details>


### [76] [Pondering the Way: Spatial-perceiving World Action Model for Embodied Navigation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29908v1)
*Hong Chen,Daqi Liu,Zehan Zhang,Haiguang Wang,Tianhao Lu,Longfei Yan,Haiyang Sun,Fangzhen Li,Hongwei Xie,Bing Wang,Guang Chen,Hangjun Ye,Yihua Tan*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 世界动作模型用于导航规划，对agent规划有潜在启发，但领域特定。

TL;DR: SWAM是一个任务中心的联合观察-动作生成框架，通过单次推理同时生成RGB-D序列和动作轨迹，显著提升视觉导航的成功率和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于世界模型的规划器采用验证为中心范式，解耦目标意图与轨迹合成，导致候选依赖、计算开销大以及采样动作与预测视觉不一致。

Method: 提出SWAM框架，通过单次推理联合生成中间RGB-D序列和动作轨迹；训练时使用深度伪标签但推理仅需单目RGB；引入视觉引导动作精炼模块和轨迹尺度正则化损失。

Result: 实验表明SWAM在成功率、轨迹准确性和推理效率上显著优于最先进的两阶段规划器，并展现鲁棒的零样本泛化能力。

Conclusion: SWAM通过任务中心的联合生成范式有效解决了现有方法的局限性，为视觉导航提供了高效准确的解决方案。

中文摘要：现有的基于世界模型的规划器在进行视觉导航时通常遵循一种以验证为中心的范式，将目标意图与轨迹合成解耦。这种方法存在候选依赖、计算开销大以及采样动作与预测视觉不一致等问题。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了SWAM（空间感知世界动作模型），一种以任务为中心的联合观察-动作生成框架。给定起点和终点的RGB观测，SWAM通过单次推理同时生成中间RGB-D序列和对应的动作轨迹，从而促进与目标一致的轨迹生成并提高空间可行性。虽然SWAM在训练时利用深度伪标签来内化空间先验，但在推理时仅需要单目RGB输入。我们进一步引入了一个视觉引导的动作精炼模块和一个轨迹尺度正则化损失，以强制运动与视觉线索之间的细粒度对齐，并稳定不同距离下的预测。大量实验表明，SWAM在成功率、轨迹准确性和推理效率上显著优于最先进的两阶段规划器，同时在未见环境中展现出鲁棒的零样本泛化能力。

Original abstract: Existing world model-based planners for visual navigation typically follow a verification-centric paradigm, decoupling goal intent from trajectory synthesis. This approach suffers from candidate dependence, heavy computational overhead, and inconsistencies between sampled actions and predicted visuals. To address these issues, we propose SWAM (Spatial-perceiving World Action Model), a task-centric joint observation-action generation framework. Given start and goal RGB observations, SWAM performs single-pass inference to simultaneously generate intermediate RGB-D sequences and corresponding action trajectories, promoting goal-consistent trajectory generation and improved spatial feasibility. While SWAM leverages depth pseudo-labels during training to internalize spatial priors, it requires only monocular RGB input at inference time. We further introduce a visual-guided action refinement module and a trajectory-scale regularization loss to enforce fine-grained alignment between motion and visual cues while stabilizing predictions across varying distances. Extensive experiments show that SWAM significantly outperforms state-of-the-art two-stage planners in success rate, trajectory accuracy, and inference efficiency, while demonstrating robust zero-shot generalization to unseen environments.

</details>


### [77] [Automating the Design of Embodied Agent Architectures](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30111v2)
*Jian Zhou,Sihao Lin,Jin Li,Shuai Fu,Gengze Zhou,Qi Wu*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 自动搜索具身agent架构，方法论可迁移至coding agent设计。

TL;DR: 本文将智能体架构搜索（AAS）迁移至具身代理领域，提出AgentCanvas运行时和KDLoop搜索过程，实验表明架构级搜索能带来成功率提升，但受制于噪声、局部最优和信用分配问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具身代理通常手工设计依赖直觉，缺乏自动化搜索；文本域AAS未在具身域系统评估，需研究迁移可行性。

Method: 提出AgentCanvas类型图运行时和KDLoop编码智能体搜索过程，在四个具身执行器上评估三种AAS变体。

Result: 架构级搜索在具身任务上取得成功率提升，但存在泄露候选、优化信号被噪声掩盖、搜索陷入局部最优、信用分配不完整等问题。

Conclusion: 表征了具身代理自动架构搜索的前景（可部署增益）与当前局限（噪声、局部最优、信用分配困难），指出需进一步解决这些约束。

中文摘要：具身代理通常被构建为手工设计的感知、记忆、规划与行动模块的组合。这种模块化暴露了巨大的架构设计空间，但当前系统仍依赖研究者的直觉来选择信息存储位置、观测处理方式以及模型调用连接方式。智能体架构搜索（AAS）实现了文本域代理的此类设计自动化，但尚未通过模拟器 rollout 在感知性具身代理上进行系统评估。我们研究这一迁移。我们引入了 AgentCanvas，一个类型图运行时，它将具身执行器托管为可编辑的节点-连线程序，支持感知模拟器的执行和剧集级日志；以及 KDLoop，一个编码智能体搜索过程，循环执行提案、批评、实验和蒸馏，并在停滞时触发反思。我们评估了三种 AAS 变体，涵盖四个具身执行器，涉及视觉语言导航、具身问答和语言条件操控。得到的 3x4 矩阵表明，架构级搜索能够在具身任务上产生可部署的方向性成功率提升，同时一个明显的高分候选者因存在泄露而被拒绝。同时，实验揭示了在文本域 AAS 中被掩盖的约束：优化信号可能被 rollout 噪声掩盖，搜索可能陷入局部编辑盆地，并且即使有详细日志，剧集级信用分配也仅部分出现。这些结果表征了具身代理自动化架构搜索的前景与当前局限性。

Original abstract: Embodied agents are typically built as hand-designed compositions of perception, memory, planning, and action modules. This modularity exposes a large architectural design space, but current systems still rely on researcher intuition to choose where information is stored, how observations are processed, and how model calls are connected. Agent Architecture Search (AAS) automates such design for text-domain agents, but has not been systematically evaluated on perceptual embodied agents through simulator rollouts. We study this transfer. We introduce AgentCanvas, a typed-graph runtime that hosts embodied executors as editable node-and-wire programs with simulator-aware execution and episode-level logs, and KDLoop, a coding-agent search procedure that cycles through proposal, critique, experiment, and distillation, with triggered reflection after stalls. We evaluate three AAS variants across four embodied executors spanning vision-language navigation, embodied question answering, and language-conditioned manipulation. The resulting 3x4 matrix shows that architecture-level search can produce deployable and directional success-rate gains on embodied tasks, while one apparent high-scoring candidate is rejected as leak-bearing. At the same time, the experiments expose constraints that are muted in text-domain AAS: optimization signals can be masked by rollout noise, search can become trapped in local edit basins, and episode-level credit assignment only partially emerges even when detailed logs are available. These results characterize both the promise and the current limits of automated architecture search for embodied agents.

</details>


### [78] [Motion Planning in Compressed Representation Spaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30940v1)
*Lukas Lao Beyer,Sertac Karaman*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 在压缩表示空间进行运动规划，其搜索与规划方法可启发agent的决策与路径生成。

TL;DR: 提出一种通过高压缩自编码器学习层次离散潜在空间，并在其中进行搜索以统一深度学习和模型驱动运动规划的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习方法虽能捕捉复杂行为但依赖大规模数据，模型驱动方法灵活且可整合领域知识但缺乏学习能力，现有两种范式各有优劣，需要统一框架兼具生成能力与灵活性。

Method: 首先训练一个高压缩比的自编码器，将运动数据编码为层次有序的离散令牌潜在空间；然后在测试时通过在该潜在空间中进行搜索来优化任意目标函数，利用自编码器的生成能力产生逼真运动轨迹。

Result: 在nuPlan和Waymo开放运动数据集上，该方法在闭环运动规划和多智能体引导场景合成任务中均取得强性能，且无需任务特定训练。

Conclusion: 所提框架成功统一了学习与模型驱动范式，通过潜在空间搜索实现高效灵活的运动规划，为多种引导行为生成任务提供了通用解决方案。

中文摘要：深度学习方法极大地扩展了机器人应用中运动规划的能力，因为从大规模数据中学习先验已被证明对于捕捉解决诸如操作或自动驾驶车辆导航等任务所需的极其复杂行为至关重要。同时，基于搜索或优化的模型驱动规划算法由于其灵活性、高效性以及通过专家设计的算法和目标函数整合领域知识的能力，仍然是一种必不可少的工具。我们提出了一种新的生成框架来统一这两种范式。首先，我们学习一个具有高压缩比和层次有序离散值令牌潜在空间的自编码器。利用自编码器学习的降维和层次化粗到细结构，我们通过直接在令牌的潜在空间中进行搜索来执行运动规划。这种搜索可以优化测试时指定的任意目标函数，提供了很大的灵活性，同时保持效率，并依靠高压缩自编码器的生成能力产生逼真的解决方案。我们在nuPlan和Waymo开放运动数据集上评估了我们的方法，展示了潜在空间搜索如何用于各种引导行为生成任务，在闭环运动规划和多智能体引导场景合成中实现了强性能，无需任何任务特定训练。

Original abstract: Deep learning methods have vastly expanded the capabilities of motion planning in robotics applications, as learning priors from large-scale data has been shown to be essential in capturing the highly complex behavior required for solving tasks such as manipulation or navigation for autonomous vehicles. At the same time, model-based planning algorithms based on search or optimization remain an essential tool due to their flexibility, efficiency, and the ability to incorporate domain knowledge via expert-designed algorithms and objective functions. We propose a new generative framework to unify these two paradigms. First, we learn an autoencoder with a high compression ratio and a latent space of hierarchically ordered, discrete-valued tokens. Leveraging both the dimensionality reduction and the hierarchical coarse-to-fine structure learned by this autoencoder, we then perform motion planning by directly searching in the latent space of tokens. This search can optimize arbitrary objective functions specified at test time, providing a large degree of flexibility while maintaining efficiency and producing realistic solutions by relying on the generative capabilities of the highly compressed autoencoder. We evaluate our method on nuPlan and the Waymo Open Motion Dataset, showing how latent space search can be used for a variety of guided behavior generation tasks, achieving strong performance for closed-loop motion planning and multi-agent guided scenario synthesis without requiring any task-specific training.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [79] [Towards Generalizable and Evidential Nuclear Magnetic Resonance-Based Molecular Structure Elucidation via Large Language Model Agent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29776v1)
*Zheng Fang,Chen Yang,Yusen Tan,Yunpeng Zhao,Fanjie Xu,Hongxin Xiang,Hanyu Sun,Hanyu Gao,Xiaojian Wang,Wenjie Du,Yuqiang Li,Jun Xia*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 化学领域的LLM agent，模仿专家推理流程，计划-候选-验证-优化循环对代码优化agent有启发。

TL;DR: NMRAgent是一个基于LLM的证据推理智能体，通过整合谱图分析工具和知识图谱，模仿人类专家推理，显著提升了未知分子结构解析的准确性和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在数据库检索和新骨架识别之间存在权衡，且缺乏原子级别的可解释性。

Method: 利用大语言模型结合专用谱图分析工具和化学知识图谱，以实验NMR谱图和分子式为输入，通过规划、候选结构生成、峰-原子一致性验证和片段优化来推理。

Result: 在骨架划分基准上，top-1准确率提升46.5%，Tanimoto相似度提升0.502，并成功解析两种未知天然产物和纠正文献错误。

Conclusion: NMRAgent通过高精度预测与透明、基于证据的推理，为分析化学中的可解释AI建立了新范式。

中文摘要：核磁共振（NMR）波谱学是分子结构解析的黄金标准，然而解析复杂谱图中的未知分子仍然是一个依赖人类专业知识的瓶颈。尽管人工智能推动了这一领域的发展，但当前方法面临一个关键折衷：数据库检索无法识别新骨架，而从头分子结构解析模型作为黑箱运行，缺乏原子级别的可解释性，而这正是严格科学验证所必需的。在这里，我们介绍了NMRAgent，一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的证据推理智能体，它通过整合专门的谱图分析工具与化学知识图谱来弥合这一差距。与以往方法不同，NMRAgent模仿人类专家的演绎推理：它以实验NMR谱图和分子式作为输入，规划解析过程，提出候选结构，验证峰-原子一致性，并通过公式感知的片段优化来修正错配的子结构。凭借其证据推理能力，NMRAgent超越了最先进的方法，在测试集包含新骨架的骨架划分基准上，将top-1准确率提高了46.5%，Tanimoto相似度提高了0.502。此外，我们通过解析从绣球（Hydrangea davidii）和蔓荆（Vitex trifolia）中分离的两种先前未知天然产物的结构，以及纠正已建立文献中的结构错误分配，展示了该智能体的实际效用。通过将高精度预测与透明且基于证据的推理相结合，NMRAgent为分析化学中的可解释人工智能建立了一个新范式。

Original abstract: Nuclear Magnetic Resonance (NMR) spectroscopy is the gold standard for molecular structure elucidation, yet interpreting complex spectra for unknown molecules remains a bottleneck reliant on human expertise. While artificial intelligence has advanced this field, current methods face a critical trade-off: database retrieval cannot identify novel scaffolds, while de novo molecular structure elucidation models operate as black boxes, lacking the atom-level interpretability required for rigorous scientific validation. Here, we present NMRAgent, an evidential reasoning agent powered by large language models (LLMs) that bridges this gap by integrating specialized spectral analysis tools with chemical knowledge graphs. Unlike previous approaches, NMRAgent mimics the deductive reasoning of human experts: it takes experimental NMR spectra and molecular formula as input, plans the elucidation process, proposes candidate structures, verifies peak-atom consistency, and refines misaligned substructure through formula-aware fragment optimization. Enabled by its evidential reasoning, NMRAgent outperforms state-of-the-art methods, improving top-1 accuracy by 46.5% and Tanimoto similarity by 0.502 on a scaffold-split benchmark with novel scaffolds in the test set. Besides, we demonstrate the agent's practical utility by elucidating the structures of two previously unknown natural products isolated from Hydrangea davidii and Vitex trifolia, and by correcting structural misassignments in established literature. By combining high-accuracy prediction with transparent and evidence-based reasoning, NMRAgent establishes a new paradigm for interpretable AI in analytical chemistry.

### [80] [EVAF: A Test-Retest Protocol for Selective Parametric Consolidation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29916v1)
*Haoliang Han*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出参数化记忆巩固机制和测试-重测协议，直接涉及agent记忆与持续学习，可迁移。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时语言代理需要区分哪些经验应持久保留，现有检索系统无法体现选择性参数巩固，因此需要新机制实现经验内化与事实记忆分离。

Method: 引入EVAF（回声-效价吸引场）门控LoRA巩固机制，配合路由记忆路径；设计测试-重测协议测量选择性参数巩固。

Result: EVAF在GPT-2和TinyLlama上优先巩固高效价、高惊奇经验；干扰后行为持久性优于冻结、检索和未门控基线，且参数漂移和跨污染低。

Conclusion: 记忆访问（检索事实）与记忆深度（内化经验）是不同计算操作，EVAF实现了选择性经验巩固而不损害事实检索。

中文摘要：长期运行的语言代理需要机制来决定在工作上下文消失后哪些经验应该持久化。检索系统可以重新插入过去的文本，但它们本身并不能表明经验已被选择性地巩固到模型自身的行为中。我们引入了EVAF，一种用于门控LoRA巩固的回声-效价吸引场机制，以及一种用于在受控干扰下测量选择性参数巩固的测试-重测协议。在GPT-2和TinyLlama上，EVAF优先巩固高效价、高惊奇度的经验，同时通过补充的路由记忆路径保留可检索的事实记忆。测试-重测测量显示，与冻结、仅检索和非门控持续更新基线相比，干扰后行为持久性更强，同时保持参数漂移和跨角色污染较低。结果支持记忆访问与记忆深度之间的分离：检索事实和内化经验是不同的计算操作。

Original abstract: Long-running language agents need mechanisms for deciding which experiences should persist after the working context is gone. Retrieval systems can reinsert past text, but they do not by themselves show that an experience has been selectively consolidated into the model's own behavior. We introduce EVAF, an Echo-Valence Attractor Field mechanism for gated LoRA consolidation, and a test-retest protocol for measuring selective parametric consolidation under controlled interference. Across GPT-2 and TinyLlama, EVAF preferentially consolidates high-valence, high-surprise experiences while preserving retrieval-accessible factual memory through a complementary routed memory path. Test-retest measurements show stronger post-interference behavioral persistence than frozen, retrieval-only, and ungated continual-update baselines, while keeping parameter drift and cross-persona contamination low. The results support a separation between memory access and memory depth: retrieving a fact and internalizing an experience are distinct computational operations.

### [81] [DuoMem: Towards Capable On-Device Memory Agents via Dual-Space Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29961v1)

TL;DR: 提出DuoMem双空间蒸馏框架，通过上下文空间和参数空间蒸馏将大模型程序性任务解决能力迁移到小模型，在ALFWorld上4B模型达到77.9%成功率，比72B模型快3倍。

Method: 双空间蒸馏：上下文空间蒸馏用教师高质量记忆替换学生记忆；参数空间蒸馏在成功教师轨迹上微调LoRA适配器。

Result: 4B模型成功率从4.3%提升至77.9%，接近72B教师模型87.1%，且速度快3倍以上，仅增加<10M参数和几MB记忆。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体可以通过多轮交互解决复杂的程序性任务，但这种能力通常依赖于大模型、长上下文以及重复推理调用。这使得先进的记忆增强智能体难以部署在资源受限的设备上。我们提出了DuoMem，一个双空间蒸馏框架，将程序性问题解决能力从大型教师模型迁移到紧凑的学生模型。DuoMem在两个互补空间中进行蒸馏：（1）上下文空间蒸馏，用教师生成的高质量程序性记忆替换学生生成的记忆，并将其前置到学生输入中；（2）参数空间蒸馏，在成功的教师轨迹上微调轻量级LoRA适配器。在具有挑战性的具身决策基准ALFWorld上评估，DuoMem将一个4B参数模型的任务成功率从4.3%提升到77.9%，缩小了与72B教师模型（87.1%）之间的大部分差距，同时仅增加不到10M可训练参数和几兆字节的预计算教师记忆。此外，增强后的4B模型完成任务的实际时间比72B教师模型快3倍以上，使其适用于实时的边缘部署，而这对教师模型来说具有挑战性。在跨越2B-72B参数的八个模型上进行的大量消融实验表明，两个蒸馏轴贡献互补。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents can solve complex procedural tasks by interacting with environments over multiple turns, but this ability typically depends on large models, long contexts, and repeated inference calls. This makes advanced memory-augmented agents difficult to deploy on resource-constrained devices. We introduce DuoMem, a dual-space distillation framework that transfers procedural problem-solving ability from a large teacher model to compact student models. DuoMem distils in two complementary spaces: (1)context-space distillation, which replaces student-generated memories with higher-quality teacher-generated procedural memories prepended to the student's input, and (2)parameter-space distillation, which fine-tunes lightweight LoRA adapters on successful teacher trajectories. Evaluated on ALFWorld, a challenging embodied decision-making benchmark, DuoMem boosts a 4B-parameter model from 4.3% to 77.9% task success rate, closing most of the gap to a 72B teacher model (87.1%), while adding fewer than 10M trainable parameters and only a few megabytes of pre-computed teacher memories. Moreover, the DuoMem-enhanced 4B model completes tasks over 3x faster than the 72B teacher in wall-clock time, making it viable for real-time edge deployment, which would be challenging for the teacher.Extensive ablations across eight models spanning 2B-72B parameters reveal that both distillation axes contribute complementary

### [82] [Neural Subspace Reallocation: Continual Learning as Retrieval-Based Subspace Memory Management](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30067v1)
*Byeong Hoon Yoon*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于检索的子空间内存管理实现持续学习，可迁移至agent记忆机制。

TL;DR: NSR通过压缩和相似性检索的LoRA内存管理实现高效连续学习，在固定容量下性能优于学习策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将LoRA视为一次性任务适配器，缺乏对历史知识的有效重用，导致在循环环境中恢复缓慢和遗忘严重。

Method: 提出神经子空间重分配（NSR），通过SVD压缩LoRA存入任务知识库，基于嵌入相似性召回进行热启动，并重新分配子空间，结合蒸馏保护旧任务。

Result: 在Split-CIFAR-100上恢复时间减少10倍，在5-Datasets上准确率最高且遗忘最少；控制实验表明内存机制（压缩和相似性检索）比学习分配策略更关键。

Conclusion: 连续学习性能的主要驱动力是内存管理机制（压缩和相似性检索），而非学习到的分配策略；压缩知识库在固定容量下保持小尺寸。
}

中文摘要：我们引入了神经子空间重分配（NSR），它将连续学习重新定义为参数子空间上的内存管理。NSR并不将低秩适配（LoRA）模块视为每个任务的一次性适配器，而是通过一个循环周期将它们管理为冻结主干网络上的可压缩、可检索的内存单元：(1) 通过SVD压缩学习到的LoRA，(2) 将它们存储在任务知识库中，(3) 通过嵌入相似性召回相关的过去LoRA以热启动新任务或返回的任务，以及(4) 相应地重新分配活动子空间，并通过蒸馏保护先前任务。我们证明，在循环环境中，任何无内存分配策略相对于基于知识库的历史感知策略都会累积遗憾Omega(T(M-1)Delta_switch)（定理1）。实验上，在Split-CIFAR-100上，知识库将循环恢复时间减少了10倍，完全符合预测；在异构的5-Datasets基准上，NSR实现了最高的准确率和最少的遗忘，比无内存启发式方法接近9倍地更接近零后向迁移。关键的是，我们进行了一项控制研究，以隔离哪个组件起作用：保持知识库固定，仅改变分配规则，我们发现一个简单的基于相似性的检索规则与学习的强化学习控制器匹配或超越（在0步 vs 1.8步内恢复重复任务，并达到相同的准确率）。因此，我们核心且诚实的发现是，在固定容量下，驱动连续学习性能的是内存机制——压缩和相似性检索——而不是学习的分配策略。内存预算分析证实压缩后的知识库保持很小——每个任务0.29 MB的参数内存——因此一个top-K保留上限限制了总占用，同时为保留的任务保留了快速恢复。

Original abstract: We introduce Neural Subspace Reallocation (NSR), which reframes continual learning as memory management over parameter subspaces. Instead of treating Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) modules as disposable per-task adapters, NSR manages them as compressible, retrievable memory units on a frozen backbone through a recurring cycle: (1) compress learned LoRAs via SVD, (2) reserve them in a TaskKnowledgeBank, (3) recall related past LoRAs by embedding similarity to warm-start new or returning tasks, and (4) reallocate the active subspace accordingly, with distillation protecting prior tasks. We prove that in cyclic environments any memoryless allocation policy incurs cumulative regret Omega(T(M-1)Delta_switch) relative to a history-aware policy backed by the Bank (Theorem 1). Empirically, on Split-CIFAR-100 the Bank reduces cyclic recovery time by 10x, exactly as predicted, and on the heterogeneous 5-Datasets benchmark NSR achieves the highest accuracy and the least forgetting, about 9x closer to zero backward transfer than the memoryless heuristics. Crucially, we run a controlled study that isolates which component matters: holding the Bank fixed and varying only the allocation rule, we find that a simple similarity-based retrieval rule matches or beats a learned reinforcement-learning controller (recovering recurring tasks in 0 vs 1.8 steps and reaching equal accuracy). Our central, honest finding is therefore that the memory mechanism -- compression and similarity retrieval -- rather than a learned allocation policy, drives continual-learning performance under fixed capacity. A memory-budget analysis confirms the compressed Bank stays small -- 0.29 MB of parameter memory per task -- so a top-K retention cap bounds the total footprint while preserving fast recovery for retained tasks.

</details>


### [83] [Query-Aware Spreading Activation for Multi-Hop Retrieval over Knowledge Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30133v1)
*Illia Makarov,Mykola Glybovets*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 图RAG多跳检索方法，可迁移至agent的检索模块。

TL;DR: 提出一种基于传播激活的查询感知图检索方法，通过余弦相似度语义门实现固定步数遍历，并集成到单个Cypher查询中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Graph RAG方法中，图遍历是查询盲的，且QAFD-RAG需要加载全图到内存并使用可变步数迭代求解器，集成复杂。

Method: 使用传播激活方法，每步以候选实体描述与问题的余弦相似度作为语义门权重，固定迭代次数，整个检索过程表示为单个Cypher查询在Neo4j内完成。

Result: 在MuSiQue上EM 32.80（接近QAFD-RAG的33.50），优于HippoRAG 5.3 EM和3.4 F1；在2WikiMultiHopQA上HippoRAG和QAFD-RAG因短语节点架构保持优势；消融实验表明语义门带来F1提升3.6-7.4，延迟降低1.5-4.9倍。

Conclusion: 所提方法在保持高效性的同时达到与QAFD-RAG相当的性能，且避免了全图加载和复杂集成，通过语义门显著提升效果和效率。

中文摘要：基于知识图谱的检索增强生成（Graph RAG）通过利用图结构在多跳问答上优于平面段落检索。然而，在大多数现有系统中，问题仅设置种子节点；后续遍历变得“查询盲”，仅依赖于图结构。例外是QAFD-RAG，它通过结合边重新加权的流扩散求解器实现了查询感知遍历。该架构需要将整个图加载到Python内存中，并且需要一个迭代次数可变的迭代求解器，这使与图数据库的集成复杂化。我们提出了一种传播激活方法，通过单个每步语义门实现相同的查询感知遍历：步骤权重是候选实体描述与问题之间的余弦相似度，且迭代次数固定。整个检索过程——种子映射、传播、top-K选择和上下文组装——被表示为一个单一的Cypher查询，在到Neo4j的一次往返中执行；图从未离开数据库。在MuSiQue上，我们的方法在精确匹配上匹配QAFD-RAG（32.80对比33.50），并在我们的比较中优于最强的纯结构基线HippoRAG，EM高5.3，F1高3.4；在2WikiMultiHopQA上，由于它们的短语节点架构，HippoRAG和QAFD-RAG保持优势。一项禁用门的消融实验证实，该门是同时获得F1提升3.6到7.4分以及检索延迟降低1.5到4.9倍的原因。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation built on knowledge graphs (Graph RAG) outperforms flat passage retrieval on multi-hop question answering by leveraging graph structure. In most existing systems, however, the question only sets the seed nodes; the subsequent traversal becomes "query-blind", depending solely on the graph structure. The exception is QAFD-RAG, which implements query-aware traversal via a flow-diffusion solver with combined edge re-weighting. This architecture requires loading the full graph into Python memory and an iterative solver with a variable number of iterations complicating integration with the graph database. We propose a spreading-activation method that achieves the same query-aware traversal with a single per-step semantic gate: the step weight is the cosine similarity between the candidate entity's description and the question, and the number of iterations is fixed. The whole retrieval procedure - seed mapping, propagation, top-K selection and context assembly - is expressed as a single Cypher query executed in one round-trip to Neo4j; the graph never leaves the database. On MuSiQue our method matches QAFD-RAG by exact match (32.80 vs 33.50) and outperforms the strongest purely-structural baseline in our comparison, HippoRAG, by 5.3 EM and 3.4 F1; on 2WikiMultiHopQA HippoRAG and QAFD-RAG retain an advantage due to their phrase-node architectures. An ablation with the gate disabled confirms that the gate is the source of a simultaneous F1 gain of 3.6 to 7.4 points and a retrieval-latency reduction by a factor of 1.5 to 4.9.

### [84] [Towards Continual Motion-Language Agents: LoRA Variants for Incremental Motion Understanding and Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30266v1)
*Bertram Taetz,Hugo Albuquerque Cosme da Silva,Gabriele Bleser-Taetz*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 运动语言agent的持续学习方法（LoRA/MoE），可启发coding agent持续学习

TL;DR: 提出基于LoRA和混合专家架构的持续学习方法，解决运动-语言双向学习中的灾难性遗忘，在五任务基准上实现近乎无遗忘，并发现硬专家选择优于软混合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主智能体在动态环境中需要持续学习新运动概念而不遗忘旧技能，现有方法在静态设置下表现良好但缺乏对稳定性-可塑性权衡的考虑，且双向运动-语言学习中的任务干扰问题未被充分研究。

Method: 基于冻结的大语言模型，引入LoRA变体缓解任务间干扰，并提出混合专家架构，使用自编码器路由器在推理时选择任务特定专家（无需任务标签），通过语义聚类HumanML3D构建五任务基准。

Result: 在M2T和T2M两个方向上几乎无遗忘，生成和描述质量高；硬专家选择（路由）在质量指标上显著优于软专家混合；发现token级准确率与下游生成质量存在差异。

Conclusion: 保持专家隔离对持续学习性能至关重要，硬路由优于软混合；未来需要更全面的评估协议来关注生成质量而非仅token准确率。

中文摘要：运动-语言智能体必须同时具备理解人类运动（运动到文本，M2T）和从自然语言生成运动（文本到运动，T2M）的双向能力。虽然基础模型在静态环境下已取得强性能，但在动态环境中运行的自主智能体必须持续融入新的运动概念——例如新颖的体育风格或专门手势——而不会灾难性遗忘先前习得的技能。我们研究了在顺序任务暴露下双向运动-语言学习中的稳定性-可塑性权衡。基于冻结的大语言模型骨干，我们引入了旨在缓解任务间干扰的低秩适配（LoRA）变体。我们特别提出了混合专家架构，该架构利用基于自编码器的路由器在推理时选择任务特定的专家，从而无需任务标签。为评估这些方法，我们通过语义聚类运动描述从HumanML3D构建了一个可重复的五任务基准。我们的实验结果表明，在M2T和T2M两个方向上几乎无遗忘，同时保持高质量的生成和描述能力。此外，我们表明通过路由进行硬专家选择在质量指标上显著优于软专家混合，这表明在持续学习环境中保持专家隔离对维持性能至关重要。最后，我们观察到标记级准确率与下游生成质量之间可能出现差异，这突出了未来关于终身运动-语言智能体的研究中需要更全面的评估协议。

Original abstract: Motion-language agents must possess the bidirectional capability to both understand human movement (motion-to-text, M2T) and generate it from natural language (text-to-motion, T2M). While foundational models have achieved strong performance in static settings, autonomous agents operating in dynamic environments must continuously incorporate new motion concepts -- such as novel athletic styles or specialized gestures -- without catastrophic forgetting of previously acquired skills. We investigate the stability-plasticity trade-off in bidirectional motion-language learning under sequential task exposure. Building on a frozen large language model backbone, we introduce low-rank adaptation (LoRA) variants designed to mitigate inter-task interference. We specifically propose mixture-of-experts architectures that utilize an autoencoder-based router to select task-specific experts at inference time, so that no task-label is needed. To evaluate these methods, we establish a reproducible five-task benchmark derived from HumanML3D through semantic clustering of motion descriptions. Our experimental results demonstrate near-zero forgetting across both M2T and T2M directions while maintaining high generation and captioning quality. Furthermore, we show that hard expert selection via routing significantly outperforms soft expert blending in quality metrics, indicating that preserving expert isolation is critical for maintaining performance in our continual learning setting. Finally, we observe that a divergence between token-level accuracy and downstream generation quality may occur, highlighting the need for more comprehensive evaluation protocols in future research on lifelong motion-language agents.

### [85] [From Search to Synthesis: Training LLMs as Zero-Shot Workflow Generators](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30704v1)
*Gan Luo,Zihan Qin,Bin Dong,Wotao Yin*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: MetaFlow训练LLM生成工作流，适用于coding agent工作流自动生成

TL;DR: MetaFlow是一种将工作流生成视为元学习问题的方法，通过两阶段训练（监督微调+RLVR）生成跨实例鲁棒的工作流，在多个任务上取得与SOTA相当的领域内性能并展现强零样本泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动设计任务级工作流需要大量专业知识和努力，限制了其广泛应用；现有自动工作流生成方法要么不能学习任务级模式，要么无法泛化到新配置。

Method: MetaFlow将工作流生成作为元学习问题，给定任务和算子集，模型学习组合策略。两阶段训练：先在合成工作流数据上监督微调，再通过RLVR使用跨实例执行反馈优化。

Result: 在问答、代码生成和数学推理基准上，MetaFlow在领域内任务上单次推理性能与SOTA相当，并在领域外任务和算子集上展现出色的零样本泛化能力。

Conclusion: MetaFlow通过元学习范式自动生成结构化工作流，在保持领域内性能的同时显著提升泛化能力，减少了对手动设计的依赖。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在广泛任务中表现出色，但其针对具体实例的解决方案往往缺乏可靠性部署所需的结构一致性。在任务层面编码重复算法模式的工作流提供了原则性框架，能带来跨实例变体的鲁棒性、可调试的可解释轨迹以及跨问题实例的可重用性。然而，手动设计此类工作流需要大量专业知识和努力，限制了其广泛应用。虽然自动工作流生成可以解决这一瓶颈，但现有方法要么生成实例特定解决方案而不学习任务级模式，要么无法泛化到训练配置之外。我们提出MetaFlow，将工作流生成视为元学习问题：给定任务和算子集，模型学习组合解决方案策略。MetaFlow分两个阶段训练：首先在合成工作流数据上进行监督微调，然后使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），利用任务中跨问题实例的执行反馈来改进端到端成功率。生成的模型能为训练过的任务生成有效工作流，并展现出对未训练任务和新算子集的强泛化能力。在问答、代码生成和数学推理的基准测试中，MetaFlow在领域内任务上单次推理即可达到与最先进基线相当的性能，同时在领域外任务和算子集上展现出显著的零样本泛化能力。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) excel across a wide range of tasks, yet their instance-specific solutions often lack the structural consistency needed for reliable deployment. Workflows that encode recurring algorithmic patterns at the task level provide a principled framework, offering robustness across instance variations, interpretable traces for debugging, and reusability across problem instances. However, manually designing such workflows requires significant expertise and effort, limiting their broader application. While automatic workflow generation could address this bottleneck, existing methods either produce instance-specific solutions without learning task-level patterns, or cannot generalize beyond their training configurations. We present MetaFlow, which casts workflow generation as a meta-learning problem: given a task and an operator set, the model learns to compose solution strategies. MetaFlow trains in two stages: supervised fine-tuning on synthetic workflow data, followed by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) that uses execution feedback across problem instances in the task to improve end-to-end success. The resulting model produces effective workflows for trained tasks and exhibits strong generalization to untrained tasks and novel operator sets. Across benchmarks in question answering, code generation, and mathematical reasoning, MetaFlow achieves performance comparable to state-of-the-art baselines on in-domain tasks with single inference, while demonstrating remarkable zero-shot generalization capabilities on out-of-domain tasks and operator sets.

### [86] [DRIFT: Difficulty Routing Self-DIstillation with Rhythm-Gated Exploration and Success BuFfer Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30345v1)
*Haisen Luo,Yiwei Liu,Haoning Wang,Dan Liu,Junxi Yin,Haotian Wang,Lei Zhang,Xiaoyu Tian,Shuaiting Chen,Yuansheng Song,Baoyan Guo,Xiongfei Yan,Bolan Yang,Chengwei Liu,Ming Cui,Jiong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出自蒸馏与强化学习结合的自我改进框架，涉及困难路由和课程学习，可迁移至agent规划与反思。

TL;DR: DRIFT通过难度路由和节奏门控实现LLM的在线自我进化，在多个基准上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自蒸馏和强化学习方法缺乏跟踪问题级学习进度和调整优化策略的机制，导致过度优化简单问题、弱监督难题、未充分探索边界案例。

Method: 提出DRIFT框架，包含难度路由（问题级动态分配自蒸馏和RL信号）和节奏门控（令牌级细化更新），并引入成功缓冲区和两阶段课程学习。

Result: 在五个基准和三个模型规模上，DRIFT在所有指标上超过GRPO和SDPO，平均79.5%（+9.5%/+7.5%），ToolUse达79.2%（+13.5%/+10.7%），创造SOTA。

Conclusion: DRIFT通过联合难度路由和节奏门控实现了LLM的稳定自我提升，显著优于现有方法，建立了新的SOTA结果。

中文摘要：使大型语言模型在没有外部专家监督的情况下实现稳定的自我提升仍然是复杂推理任务中的一个核心挑战。现有的自我蒸馏和强化学习方法缺乏显式的机制来跟踪问题级别的学习进度并相应地调整优化策略。因此，训练可能会过度优化简单问题，从难题中获得较弱的监督信号，并且未能充分探索边界案例。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了DRIFT，一种面向大型语言模型的在线自我进化策略优化框架。DRIFT通过联合使用难度路由和节奏门控来调节模型的自我改进过程。前者在问题级别识别模型的学习状态并动态分配自我蒸馏和强化学习信号，而后者在令牌级别细化策略更新，将探索集中在关键推理位置。通过进一步结合成功缓冲区和两阶段课程学习策略，DRIFT保留了高质量的历史经验，同时逐步引导模型从可靠的行为获取走向稳定的策略进化。在五个基准测试和三种模型规模上的评估中，DRIFT在所有评估指标上均超过了GRPO和SDPO的峰值性能。在五个基准测试的平均分数上，DRIFT达到了79.5%，比GRPO高出9.5%，比SDPO高出7.5%，创造了新的最先进结果。值得注意的是，在ToolUse上，DRIFT达到了79.2%的准确率，比GRPO提高了13.5%，比SDPO提高了10.7%，创造了新的最先进水平，并显著优于所有同期方法。

Original abstract: Enabling large language models to achieve stable self-improvement without external expert supervision remains a central challenge in complex reasoning tasks. Existing self-distillation and reinforcement learning methods lack explicit mechanisms for tracking problem-level learning progress and adapting optimization strategies accordingly. Consequently, training may over-optimize easy problems, receive weak supervision from hard problems, and fail to sufficiently explore borderline cases. To resolve these issues, we propose DRIFT, an online self-evolution policy optimization framework for large language models. DRIFT regulates the model's self-improvement process through the joint use of Difficulty Routing and Rhythm Gating. The former identifies the model's learning state at the problem level and dynamically allocates self-distillation and reinforcement learning signals, while the latter refines policy updates at the token level, concentrating exploration on critical reasoning positions. By further incorporating a success buffer and a two-stage curriculum learning strategy, DRIFT preserves high-quality historical experience while progressively guiding the model from reliable behavior acquisition toward stable policy evolution. Evaluated across five benchmarks and three model scales, DRIFT surpasses the peak performance of both GRPO and SDPO across all evaluated metrics. On the average score over the five benchmarks, DRIFT achieves 79.5$\%$, outperforming GRPO by 9.5$\%$ and SDPO by 7.5$\%$, establishing a new state-of-the-art result. Notably, on ToolUse, DRIFT reaches an accuracy of 79.2$\%$, improving over GRPO by 13.5$\%$ and SDPO by 10.7$\%$, setting a new state-of-the-art and substantially outperforming all concurrent methods.

### [87] [TraceLab: Characterizing Coding Agent Workloads for LLM Serving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30560v2)
*Kan Zhu,Mathew Jacob,Chenxi Ma,Yi Pan,Stephanie Wang,Arvind Krishnamurthy,Baris Kasikci*

TL;DR: 我们收集并分析了约4,300个编码代理会话，揭示了长自主循环、长上下文短输出、多样工具调用和高前缀缓存命中率等特征，并提出了优化方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现编码代理工作负载具有长自主循环、长上下文短输出、工具调用多样且重尾分布、前缀缓存命中率高但不完美的特点。

Conclusion: 这些负载特征指向低开销工具调用、追加长度感知预填充、语义感知工具延迟预测和改进KV缓存管理等优化机会。

中文摘要：编码代理正迅速成为代理型LLM的主要应用，但高效服务它们仍然具有挑战性。解决这一挑战需要理解真实工作负载模式，然而，用于此类分析的数据在很大程度上是缺失的。现有的公共轨迹和基准测试并未捕获真实的、日常的编码代理使用情况，涉及多个代理和模型家族以用于服务系统分析。为填补这一空白，我们收集并发布了一个包含大约4,300个编码代理会话的轨迹，其中包含约350,000个LLM步骤和430,000个工具调用，这些数据来自我们自己日常使用Claude Code和Codex的情况。我们的分析表明，编码代理工作负载具有长自主循环、长上下文短输出、多样且重尾分布的工具调用，以及高但非完美前缀缓存命中率等特点。这些发现指出了优化的具体机会，包括低开销工具调用、追加长度感知预填充、语义感知工具延迟预测以及围绕人工间隔改进KV缓存管理。我们在https://github.com/uw-syfi/TraceLab.git发布数据集、轨迹收集管道和分析代码，项目网站为https://tracelab.cs.washington.edu。

Original abstract: Coding agents are rapidly becoming a major application of agentic LLMs, but serving them efficiently remains challenging. Progress on this challenge requires understanding real workload patterns, yet the data needed for such analysis is largely absent. Existing public traces and benchmarks do not capture real, day-to-day coding-agent usage across multiple agents and model families for serving-system analysis. To help fill this gap, we collect and release a trace of roughly 4,300 coding-agent sessions, containing about 350,000 LLM steps and 430,000 tool calls from our own day-to-day use of Claude Code and Codex. Our analysis shows that coding-agent workloads feature long autonomous loops, long contexts with short outputs, diverse and heavily-tailed tool calls, and high but imperfect prefix cache hit rates. These findings point to concrete opportunities for optimizing serving, including lower-overhead tool calling, append-length-aware prefill, semantic-aware tool-latency prediction, and improved KV-cache management around human-paced gaps. We release the dataset, trace collection pipeline, and analysis code at https://github.com/uw-syfi/TraceLab.git the project website is https://tracelab.cs.washington.edu.
